Dragon Knight
Job Base: Knight
Written By:
Leinarth
Job Bonuses
STR AGI VIT INT DEX LUK
5 4 6 10 8 4


Overview

Hi everyone, Leinarth here. I'm going to teach you what I learned during my stay on NovaRO about Dragon Knights. Here I will teach you about the most interesting builds I have the knowledge of. If there's an acronym you don't understand, you should check out the list I made at the bottom. If you have any questions, you may find me on Novacord under the name Leinarth. Feel free to PM me too, my discord tag is pimousse.

Disclaimer: this guide is purely tailored for NovaRO and will not be fit for any other private server, and you may not redistribute it elsewhere, nor use it as a base for your own guide. Seriously, get creative by your own means.


A bit of news : The arrival of 4th classes and Dragon Knight means a lot of guide updating, for now the stats and skills are done and the gears (and potential builds) will come later.

Stats

  • STR - Strength is crucial for damage, do not neglect it as a RK. It increases a lot Weapon ATK, and RKs mostly play with high ATK weapons like two-handed swords, so it's more than worth it.
  • AGI - Agility should be usually high for all builds (except IB if you can't spam), since you need max ASPD for optimal DPS.
  • VIT - Vitality increases your already great HP pool, don't forget that your HP gets nearly tripled under Berserk (Interesting for sustain if you're playing Berserk).
  • INT - Intelligence will increase your Enchant Blade damage, as well as your tiny SP pool. Do not hesitate to put some points here if you feel like you're often out of SP, or you'll have to play with mana potions.
  • DEX - Dexterity is awesome in case you're playing a skill-based build like Spiral Pierce or Ignition Break, because you need to reduce the cast as much as possible (Instacasting is great for increasing your DPS).
  • LUK - Luck will be really important if you're playing the Critical build, otherwise it's not something you should focus on.

4th Class Characteristics status

  • POW - Power directly impacts physical damage, and is taken into account as a multiplier in several DK skills; it is our main 4th class stat and thus must be maxed, yes even for the Dragon Breath build (more on that later in the Skills section).
  • STA - Stamina increases RES (Physical Resistance), which reduces physical damage taken. This is not really interesting for us as our main concern is dealing damage.
  • WIS - Wisdom increases MRES (Magic Resistance), which reduces magical damage taken. Same as above, none of our concern.
  • SPL - Spell is the magic version of POW, and since we don't do any magic damage, we also ignore this stat.
  • CON - Concentration is kind of the 4th class version of LUK as it increases various stats (HIT, FLEE, P.ATK and S.MATK). If you go for a non-critical build, this will be your second main stat.
  • CRT - Creative is a weird stat which increases both the 40% base Critical Damage modifier (not the same mod as what we get from gears) and... H.PLUS for better heals. Forget that last part and pick up this stat as your second main one if you wish to go for a Critical build.

Skills

Here we'll talk about what to level up in your skill trees, what skills are important; I'll give you what I leveled up but feel free to change it to your liking. This skill build is a versatile build intended to be used for all builds except the dragon skills, so this list might not be what you're looking for if you're going down the Dragon Breath path.

First Job Skills
First Job Skills are pretty much up to you, the most important is unlocking the skills you'll have after your job changes.
Skill Notes Type
Sword Mastery Lv 1 Increases ATK with daggers and one-handed swords. You only need this at level 1 to unlock 2HS Mastery; there's no one-handed sword or dagger that are worth it for RKs (maybe you'll take it if you plan on use something like Combat Knife on a Dragon Breath PVP build, or if you're going on a meme adventure with Faceworm Queen's Leg and a full int build ?). Passive
Two-Handed Sword Mastery Lv 10 Some free ATK once you get a 2HS like Lindy Hop (RK's best sword waifu fellow), good enough. Passive
Magnum Break Lv 5 It pushes back all enemies around you, deals Fire property damage in a 5x5 AoE, and it gives you a temporary 20% Fire damage boost based on your ATK. You need this at level 5 for Aura Blade when you get Lord Knight, and lvl 3 for Bowling Bash as a Knight. Offensive
Increase HP Recovery Lv 10 Gives higher HP recovery and increases the regeneration you get from consumables, always nice to have, especially when you have the platinum skill Moving HP Recovery. Passive
Bash Lv 10 Your main single target spamming skill as a Swordsman, it deals up to 400% damage based on your ATK and has the ability to stun with the platinum skill Fatal Blow. You can get a Bongun card if you want to go trolling in PvP with this and Charge Attack for maximum pushback. Offensive
Provoke Lv 5 This skill decreases the defense of the enemy while increasing his attack; this skill is mainly used for luring mobs since they'll target you once you Provoke them. You need it at level 5 for both Endure as a Swordsman and Parry as a Lord Knight. Active
Endure Lv 8 With this you won't get anim-locked for up to 7 hits, great to use when you need to get out of a mess or you're making a mob train. It also increases MDEF by a tiny bit. Active
Auto Berserk Lv 1 This skill does a reduced version of Provoke on yourself; it gives a neat 32% ATK boost in exchange for a 55% decrease of your soft DEF; You can keep it always activated for instances/MvPs, since you don't have any DEF under Berserk anyway. Passive-Active
Second/Trans Job Skills

You won't be able to take all these skills as a Knight/Lord Knight ! I used some of my Rune Knight points into my 2nd class tree because I don't play Dragon Breath build, and most of the RK skills do not interest me except some of them that I'll explain in the Third Job Skills section.

Skill Notes Type
Two-Hand Quicken Lv 10 The sweet melody of good ol' AGI knight buddy comes from this skill. It used to be a +30% ASPD bonus but since Renewal it has become a +7 flat ASPD bonus which lasts 300 seconds. You need this skill maxed first to be able to kill monsters quickly without relying on SP consumables. Don't forget to get the ASPD potion corresponding to your level for maximum sword-spamming in the enemies' faces. Since the KRO Mass Skill Rebalance, this skill now gives in addition to the usual buff, +10% ASPD, and Crit and HIT per skill level, to a maximum of Crit + 12 and HIT + 20. Active
Auto Counter Lv 5 This makes you wait for an attack during the whole cast of the skill; if you get attacked in front of your character, the attack will be blocked and you'll automatically counter with a hit. This skill might have been useful in pre-renewal but it's not the case anymore. You need to level it up to 5 to unlock Bowling Bash. Active
Bowling Bash Lv 0 (or 10) This skill is great for killing monsters in AoE, though it gets sometimes another behaviour where only the monster you clicked on will get damaged and it'll get pushed bash far away; this is due to the gutterlines problem (Use your Google-fu and check it out if you don't know it). Since the KRO Mass Skill Rebalance, there's no gutterline anymore, it has a 1 second cooldown and deals more damage with a two-handed sword. On my current build I don't have it because I do not use it anymore (as a crit RK you mainly do single target DPS), to allow for more diversity in my build like the possibility of getting Spiral Pierce and a Peco Peco/Dragon. If you are leveling, you should of course take it for faster grinding. Offensive
Riding Lv 1 You have the possibility of walking 25% faster as well as having 1k added to your maximum weight capacity so of course you should take it (Except if you want to be the edgy RK walking slowly away from your victims). Passive
Cavalry Mastery Lv 5 If you take a mount, obviously you need this or you'll hit slower than a Novice lvl 1. You need it at level max to prevent losing ASPD when you get a mount. Once you are a Rune Knight, you don't need this skill anymore except for the requirement on Dragon Training, so only get it level 1 when that time comes. Passive
Spear Mastery Lv 10 Works the same as the two previous masteries you can get as a Swordsman, but for spears (both one-handed and two-handed). You need it at level max to unlock Spiral Pierce once you get Lord Knight, if you're only a Knight don't bother with spear skills like this one, except if you have a really good spear you can use. Passive
Pierce Lv 5 This skill was mostly used in pre-renewal for leveling with a spear on large monsters, because it can deal its damage several times depending on the size of the monster (1 hit for small, 2 for medium, 3 for large monsters). Same as before, take it if you have a good spear or simply because you want to play a spear Knight build for leveling on large monsters. You need it at level 5 to unlock Spear Stab. Offensive
Spear Stab Lv 5 This skill is unused by the majority of the spear users, because it does mediocre damage and you usually don't want to push back the enemies you want to fight. Even though it's crap, you must get it to level 5 to unlock Spiral Pierce, once you're a Lord Knight. Offensive
Brandish Spear Lv 2 Brandish Spear is an alternative to Bowling Bash for spear users; I personally don't use it but some people prefer using this for leveling instead of BB. I only get it level 2 to unlock the RK's skill Phantom Thrust. Brandish Spear is now a ranged skill since the KRO Mass Skill Rebalance, and its damage depends a lot on your STR. Offensive
Spear Boomerang Lv 5 Spear Boomerang is optional, you can take it if you decide to have a multi-purpose build like me; I can take it thanks to the skill points I do not use for Bowling Bash since I don't use it anymore, and it adds a small amount of damage to the skill Hundred Spear (there's a 40% chance of casting it instantly after H-Spear Lv 10). If you will never use spears, you may redistribute these points somewhere else. Offensive

Transcended Job Skills

Skill Notes Type
Aura Blade Lv 5 Aura Blade gives +100 ATK on your attacks and it's unaffected by your enemies' DEF now gives flat damage based on your level (kRO MSR). You know the drill, free ATK buffs' are always nice to have. Active
Parrying Lv 10 This skill is really awesome for surviving as a two-handed sword user; it allows you to parry physical attacks at a whooping 50% chance at level max, it's like Auto Guard but much better. You can even tank several physical skills like Asura Strike or Spiral Pierce with it. Be careful though, it only lasts 60 seconds so don't forget to keep it always active, and also cast it before you use Berserk so you don't suffer too much early from your lack of DEF. Active
Concentration Lv 5 For a short duration, Concentration further increases the power of the madman you are; it gives you +50 HIT, increases your ATK by 25% and decreases your DEF by 25% (who cares about DEF when you can hit like a truck ? ;D). It also gives you the effect of Endure for a small duration, and you can reset the 7 hits by using Endure after. Active
Tension Relax Lv 1 This skill is optional as it is quite oriented for solo grinding; it triples your HP recovery speed and makes you sit down, but if anything happens to you (that includes taking damage, standing up, using consumables, equipping stuff), the buff is canceled. You may take it if you play often solo, do not use HP items and have points to spend on your LK skill tree. Active
Berserk Lv 1 Now we're talking ! Berserk is pretty much the bread and butter of the Crit RK; you won't be able to do anything than attacking your enemies without skills, but you'll have :
  • Full recovery of your HP
  • HP tripled
  • Double damage
  • +15% ASPD
  • Endure effect
  • Increased movespeed
  • Flee halved
  • DEF/MDEF reduced to 0

It also drains your HP by 5% every 15 seconds, so don't forget to fall back once you get really low, that way you can wait for the effect to end, resplenish your SP to buff yourself again, Berserk again and get back into the fight. If the fight ends before your Berserk does, you can ask a Sorcerer to use Dispell on you or an AB to use Clearance (Use chatrooms/emoticons to talk in Berserk). Also, please do not forget that you can't level the skill until you're job 50 as a Lord Knight.

Active
Spiral Pierce Lv 5 This is the strongest offensive skill you unlock as a Lord Knight. It has proven itself back in pre-renewal in PvP and WoE as a frightening skill that could one shot lots of classes without enough PvP-tanking stuff, because it ignores Soft and Hard DEFs. It's still great in Renewal, and it's especially strong if you make your build based on this skill; % ranged damage bonuses and DEX will be this skill's friends.

With the kRO MSR, Spiral Pierce's cast time has been quite reduced, both in FCT and VCT, as well as the After Cast Delay which got halved. The skill's special size penalty got improved and now the damage formula also depends on BASE LEVEL. Here's the old formula of the skill, taken from RMS (to give you an idea of how it works) :

  • Damage = [(80% of weapon's weight * (100%+ skill level*50%) + (round.down(STR/10^2) + Upgrade Damage) * size modifier (S 125%, M 100%, L 75%)) * card factors * element factors ]* 5 hits

To summarize it up with the factors that increase its damage:

  • +% ranged damage bonus
  • Weight of your weapon
  • STR
  • +% damage cards
  • Elemental advantage
  • Base Level
 Offensive
Head Crush Lv 0 It used to be nice in pre-renewal because it allowed you to bleed enemies to death, since not everybody had high VIT and LUK (for the bleeding success rate, it's not the same as External Bleeding); but with third classes pretty much everybody has put a lot of points into these stats. Don't bother leveling it. Offensive
Joint Beat Lv 0 This skill can do a lot of different strong status alignements on enemies, but it's highly impeded by Hard DEF (comes from VIT). Same as Head Crush, it was good back in pre-renewal, don't level it. Offensive
Third Job Skills
Skill Notes Type
Rune Mastery Lv 10 Basically the reason why you're called a Rune Knight, it allows you to create the runes you can consume as a RK. Each level unlocks a rune, and also increases the success rate of the crafting (starts at a 53% base rate and stops at a 71% base rate) so you should get it level max. The most important runes you should try to get are Turisus (Giant Growth), Asir (Fighting Spirit) and Rhydo (Crush Strike). The other runes are situational, you should first focus on creating a big supply of these 3 as you'll be keeping them up everytime because of how strong they are (except Rhydo, you should keep them for big monsters or when you need to end quickly a fight).

If you want to know more about the runes, you should check out the section dedicated for it here.

Passive
Enchant Blade Lv 10 This skill allows you to add your MATK as additional magic damage to your normal attacks, and it adds 200 MATK during the duration. This means you can directly add stat points into INT for damage, although some tests have shown that the upgrade in damage is quite small (Somebody tested the impact of MATK and saw a difference of 2-3K damage between 1 and 90 INT). Despite this, you should take it because for early game it'll give you a slight advantage on your normal attacks and later on it'll be useful for a shadow gear equipment that gives ASPD based on this skill. Active
Sonic Wave Lv 10 It's a quick ranged attack pretty useful early on for farming little monsters (especially if you have a Peuz set). It is one of the several builds possible on RK as this skill has great potential with its ability to crit and also the fact that there is an endgame weapon that heavily reduces the cooldown of it, making it spammable and damn strong. Offensive
Death Bound Lv 5 This skill is an evolution of Auto Counter, and not a good skill to get in my opinion. Waiting for an enemy to strike has never been good in RO and will never be (except if we one day get Max Pain as a skill but that will never happen). We get it level 5 to unlock Ignition Break. Offensive
Wind Cutter Lv 5 This is a self-target AoE skill that hits everything around you up to 7x7 cells with a small cooldown 0.35 seconds at level 5. The skill has different mechanics depending on the weapon you use :
  • With a two-handed sword : 2 hits instead of 1 hit, at a 1250% per hit skill modifier, and the skill will pierce DEF
  • With a spear weapon : the damage is considered ranged instead of melee, with a 2000% skill modifier
  • With other weapons : nothing specific, with a 1500% skill modifier
 Offensive
Ignition Break Lv 5 This is one of the big ATK AoE skills of the Rune Knight, it now deals 2000% ATK on an entire area of 9x9 cells around you, and will apply critical hits. It has a cooldown that makes it kinda slow to use but later on there are several gears to reduce it eventually to 0, making it spammable (but also extremely expensive). Offensive
Phantom Thrust Lv 3 This spear-only skill can bring your enemies (or allies) next to you, as well as attacking them (not to allies of course). It has a range of 7 cells at level 3, and you can use it either to save an ally who went too far into the battlefield or to troll party members (you might get kicked of the party for that, be careful). Offensive
Hundred Spear Lv 5 A spear exclusive skill pretty strong and extremely fast to cast which hits in a 7x7 AoE from afar; it has some CD that can be nearly completely removed through some gears to allow some spam. Offensive
Dragon Training Lv 5 This skill is the same as Riding&Cavalry Mastery, you'll need it if you got these two, RKs can't ride Peco-Pecos anymore because they're "afraid" of the mana that emanates from the RKs (RP reason outta nowhere of why the devs were too lazy to make two mount sprites). Passive
Dragon Breath Lv 0 This is a strong dragon skill that does ranged, Fire, AoE damage that ignores flee and may cause the Burning effect. It's mainly used in its own build: it's quite good when you get DEX Temporal Boots and a way to reduce After Cast Delay like Tae Goo Lyeon or the Excellion set. This build is too much specialized in stat investment and stuff so I didn't invest points into it. Runes can enchant your Dragon Breath with different elements ! Use Turisus to make it Holy element, and Lux Anima to change it to Shadow element (Lux takes priority over Turisus). Offensive
Dragon's Water Breath Lv 0 It's the same as the previous one, except it does Water damage instead and may inflict the Freezing status. Same as for Dragon Breath, you can enchant this skill with different elements, including Ghost property if you use the Asir runestone, and Neutral property if you use Lux Anima (Lux takes priority over Asir). Offensive
Dragon Howling Lv 0 Dragon Howling causes the Fear status with a high success rate (80% at level 10) in a big area around the caster (15x15 at level 10), thus immobilizing them momentarily. This skill is nice for luring monsters and packing them at one place, either to kill them with Dragon Breath or to allow your team to deal with them efficiently. I never use this skill but depending on your gameplay you might find it quite useful, even if you don't play DB build (especially for PvP content). Active
Full Throttle Lv 0 or 5 Full Throttle is a skill common to all 3rd classes that restores your life to the max, increases your stats by 20% temporarily while consuming a percentage of your max HP every second. Despite the fact that it seems really strong, you get a cooldown of 30 minutes on the skill, and at the end of the duration you'll get the Rebound status and become literally crippled; your movement speed decreases and your natural HP and SP recoveries are disabled. If you have skill points to spend, you should get it to level max or not at all because the first levels are pretty much crap. It can help you in a difficult situation if you're not under Berserk, or you can use it BEFORE Berserk to go fully on the offensive and hope you don't die before both the skill and Berserk's HP consumptions alongside the enemies' attacks slaughter you. If you end up leveling it, keep it for the MvPs. Active
Fourth Job Skills
Skill Notes Type
Servant Weapon Lv 5 The first and core skill of the Servant Weapon branch, it allows you to summon continuously for a specific duration up to 5 floating swords which can be used either for boosting AA attacks with some bonus 9x9 splash (halved) critical damage (which is influenced also by your base level and your POW stat), or consume them with the other Servant skills. This skill regenerates 6 times the skill's level in AP upon casting it. Active
Servant Weapon - Sign Lv 5 The second skill of the Servant branch, it will apply a temporary mark on the targeted enemy for a small duration; it is necessary for using the 2 other Servant Weapon skills. Active
Servant Weapon - Phantom Lv 5 The third skill of the Servant branch, it will make the user dash to the Sign-marked target and inflict damage to the target and around it in a 5x5 AoE, with a number of hits equal to the current quantity of summoned weapons available. This skill scales on base level, POW and critical damage, with a normal critical chance. It has a high chance of inflicting the Pitch-Darkness status (Unknown on what it does for now). Offensive
Servant Weapon - Demolition Lv 3 The fourth and last skill of the Servant branch, it consumes all weapons to do melee physical damage hits per consumed weapon, to all Sign-marked targets within a 13x13 radius and restores a number of Servant Weapons equal to the amount of enemies hit. This skill scales on base level, POW and critical damage, with a normal critical chance. It also recovers 3 AP. Offensive
Charging Pierce Lv 0 A buff skill exclusive to spears and two-handed sword users, it allows the player to stack "Charging counter" charges when using Pierce/Spiral Pierce/Hundred Spears/Madness Crusher. These charges last for 5 seconds and if no charging skill is cast within 5 seconds, the stacks will be reset. Once the user reaches 10 charges, the previously mentioned skills will be heavily boosted. Active
Two Hand Defending Lv 10 A very basic passive which gives two-handed weapons users a bit more survivability thanks to some size% damage reduction modifier, only when using a two-handed sword/axe/spear. Passive
Hack and Slasher Lv 5 Exclusive to two-hand sword/spear users, this targeted skill deals 2-hits AoE damage on the target and enemies around it up to a maximum of 9x9 range depending on the skill level. This skill is influenced by base level and POW, and will change its damage type whether you use a sword (Melee) or a spear (Ranged). After the third job rework patch, this skill now can crit ! Offensive
Madness Crusher Lv 0 Exclusive to two-hand sword/spear users, this skill inflicts ranged damage to a target and the surrounding enemies in an area up to 7x7 around it. This skill is influenced by base level, POW, weapon level and weapon weight. When casted this skill recovers 2 AP. Offensive
Storm Slash Lv 5 Exclusive to two-hand sword/axe users, this spammable single-target skill does an increasing quantity of damage and number of hits based on the skill level. It can crit (with a normal crit rate) and is influenced by base level and POW, and there is also a chance of doing double damage while under the influence of Giant Growth (Turisus Runestone). This skill also recovers 1 AP per cast. Offensive
Vigor Lv 10 One of the two ultimate skills of Dragon Knights which can be casted for 150 AP, Vigor heavily increases the damage of basic auto attacks for 5 minutes, while also increasing a lot damage against Demi-Human and Angel enemies. This great boost comes with a downside of consuming a small amount of HP on every attack. Active
Dragonic Aura Lv 0 The other ultimate Dragon Knight skill which can also be casted for 150 AP, Dragonic Aura inflicts a very strong ranged attack (strangely ATK% based, and influenced by base level and POW) upon a single target, with a higher percentage if the target is Demi-Human or Angel. After casting it, the user will also deal increased damage with the 3rd class Dragon Breath skills and Hundred Spears during 300 seconds. This skill will also passively influence the damage of Dragon Breath skills, through POW and P.ATK. Offensive
Dragonic Breath Lv 0 Similar to the old Dragon Breath skills but also quite different, this skill deals AoE DEF-piercing ranged damage increased by Max HP & Max SP, but is also ATK% based, and increased by base level and POW. Dragonic Breath recovers 2 AP per cast and its damage will be more impacted by HP & SP when under the effect of Dragonic Aura. Offensive

How to become a Rune Craftsman 101

Here you'll learn how to become a master in the art of rune-crafting. But first, here's a description of what these runes do:

  •  Turisus Runestone : Giant Growth
    • Increases your STR by 30
    • 30% chance to add 250% on your next attack (basically it adds the damage to your normal attack then it is multiplied by all the attack modifiers, like Lex Aeterna and Double Attack). The bonus damage is also applied on skills, but at a 100% chance instead.
    • Increases by 15% your melee damage
    • Cast Time : 1 second (Fixed Cast Time)
    • Duration : 15 minutes
  •  Asir Runestone : Fighting Spirit
    • Increases your ATK by a flat value + a bonus which depends on the number of party members
    • Increases your ASPD by 4
    • Duration : 15 minutes
  •  Rhydo Runestone : Crush Strike
    • Deals enormous damage on your next single hit with a 20% chance to break your weapon
      • ATK[{Weapon_Lv (Weapon_Upgrade + 6) 100} + (Weapon_ATK) + (Weapon_Weight)]%
    • Considered as a normal attack, so it can stack with some strong skills/buffs (Double Attack, critical, Lex Aeterna,...). 1M damage is not hard to do if you manage to get these buffs
    • Duration : 30 seconds
    • Cast Time : 1 second (Fixed Cast Time)
    • Cooldown : 30 seconds
  •  Pertz Runestone : Storm Blast
    • Produces a shockwave around the player, dealing high physical damage which knockbacks all enemies around you; this skill can also proc a critical hit.
    • Formula to be verified : ATK[RuneMastery_Lv + (STR 8) 100]%
    • Area of Effect : 7x7
    • Cast Time : 2 seconds (Variable Cast only)
    • Casting Delay : 1 second
  •  Verkana Runestone : Millenium Shield
    • Creates between 2 and 4 spirit spheres that act as a shield. They each have 1K HP as well as your DEF and MDEF. The amount of damage the sphere suffers cannot exceed its health, meaning you can also block between 2 to 4 mortal hits (for example, Earthquake)
    • Number of shields summoned:
      • 50% chance to spawn 2 shields
      • 30% chance to spawn 3 shields
      • 20% chance to spawn 4 shields
    • Area of Effect : 7x7
    • Duration : 15 minutes
    • Cooldown : 1 minute and 30 seconds
    • Casting Delay : 1 second
    • Kyrie Eleison will take priority over the Millenium Shield's spheres
  •  Isia Runestone : Vitality Activation
    • Increases all the healing effects (except regen ones) you have (and will get) by 50%.
    • Reduces melee reflect damage by 50%.
    • Duration : 15 minutes
  •  Hagalas Runestone : Stonehard Skin
    • Consumes 25% of your HP to create a shield that protects you against damage (with the HPs consumed), and increase both your DEF and MDEF. Your hardened skin will allow you with a 30% chance to break your opponent's weapon, or in case of a monster, reduce its ATK by 25% for 10 seconds
    • DEF and MDEF bonus : (JobLv RuneMastery_Lv) 4
    • Duration : 15 minutes
    • Cast Time : 2 seconds (Fixed Cast Time)
  •  Urj Runestone : Abundance
    • Regenerates your SP every 10 seconds for an amount of 60 SPs.
    • Duration : 15 minutes
  •  Nosiege Runestone : Refresh
    • Cleanses you from the following status effects, and prevent them for the duration:
      • Stun, Sleep, Curse, Petrification
      • Poison, Blind, Silence, Bleeding
      • Chaos, Frozen, Deep Sleep, Burning
      • Freezing, Crystallization, Marsh of Abyss, Howling of Mandragora
    • The rune can be used while being stunned, frozen or asleep.
    • Duration : 1 minute
    • Cast Time : 1 second (Fixed Cast Time)
    • Cooldown : 2 minutes
  •  Lux Anima Runestone : Lux Anima
    • The runestone has been reworked since the 7th of November; it now behaves as a jack of all trades rune because of all its effects :
      • Adds a 15% chance to autocast Storm Blast when dealing normal attacks.
      • Increases physical damage against all size enemies by 30%.
      • Increases critical damage by 30%.
      • Increases melee physical damage by 30%.
      • Increases ranged physical damage by 30%.
      • Adds 30% Max HP and Max SP.
    • Duration : 15 minutes
  • (Siege-only)  Algiz Runestone : Vintage Lux Anima
    • This custom runestone has been implemented to compensate for the lack of the old Lux Anima in PvP content. It directly applies Millenium Shield, Stone Skin and Vitality Activation to all allies within the given area.
    • Duration : 1 minute
    • Area of Effect : 7x7
    • Cooldown : 1 minute


Rune Activation Trivia

There are some quite rare cases where the rune fails and you won't get buffed. The success rate formula (considering Rune Mastery is Lv10) is the following:

[60 + Skill_Lv + (DEX + LUK) 20]%

Thankfully, it doesn't happen often as we have by default a very high success rate (95% if you have Rune Mastery at Lv 10 and 1 in both DEX and LUK). Here is a list of what could happen if you failed the consumption of your rune:

Effect Chance Details
Nothing 80% Nothing but confusion about what happened to your missing rune buff.
Status Effect 10% What an unlucky fellow ! You get "blessed" with one of the following status effects: Blind, Silence, Sleep, Poison, Stun, and Frozen.
Explosion 3% I hope you didn't cast while being at low HP... The rune blows up, dealing you (Rune_Weight 1000) magic damage.
Recovery 3% This rune had an identity problem, and behaved like a Red Potion. It heals you for (Rune_Weight 1000) HP.
Teleport 2% Why would you buy Fly Wings when you have runestones ? You get teleported to another location on the map.
Full Recovery 1% You crush the rune, only to discover that it was in reality an Yggdrasil Berry. You get a full recovery !
Mass Resurrection 1% This rune felt like your party members didn't deserve their death, and resurrects them all (you're really lucky if it happens, this is about a 100 times harder to proc than dropping an MvP card).

If at some point it looks like your runes have no effect, please make sure your Rune Mastery skill is leveled (and obviously maxed out) ! It directly impacts the effectiveness of your runes !


Rune Crafting

Now it's time for the crafting part; we're going to see how it works, and how you can craft the most runes.

The success formula is : [Base_Success_Rate + (DEX 30 + LUK 10 + JobLv 10) + Runestone_Bonus - Rune_Rank]%

Base_Success_Rate goes from 32% at Rune Mastery Lv1, up to 50% at Lv10. So to get the best crafting rate, always make sure you got the skill maxed out. Keep in mind also that it affects directly the efficiency of the runes; if you have Rune Mastery at a very low level or not even leveled at all, your runes will be extremely weak !

If you're playing a Critical Rune Knight build, you may notice that it's much easier for you to craft them thanks to the high investment in the LUK stat. Otherwise if you're playing another build or simply want to minmax, you might want to register a crafting build with 130 DEX, 130 LUK, at the Build Manager in the Main Office to get the highest success rate possible.

The Rune_Rank penalty depends on the runestone you're crafting, it goes from 5% up to 20%, so as a rule of thumb, always keep the 20% penalty in your calcuations if you make a crafting build. Some people have reported having a better success chance increased their numbers of crafted runes, others said it was purely random, needs to be tested thorougly.

To complete the formula, you'll need the success bonus from the rough runestone consumables, you can find it here :

Runestone Grade Success Rate Way to obtain
 General +2% Sold in the Main Office
 Quality +5% Abandoned Teddy Bear

Horror Toy Factory

 Rare +8%

Basic Equipment

Here we'll see some basic stuff you can find on the floor at Prontera if you're lucky at that time or at a small price in the market (watch out for rip-offs !). There will be also mid-game equipment, and a few end-game items. Please do not forget that if you are a total beginner and the equipments feel unobtainable at first on the market, you can keep playing with the Eden Gears until a higher level like 150 as they are reliable enough if you do all the quests at the Eden HQ, considering there are progression gears even for after level 99.

Sets

I didn't put any price here as there are different items to look up in the market, feel free to visit it here.

Set Level Way to obtain Notes & Set's effects
 Eden's set 12 Eden quests (Use @go eden to go there) This is the earliest set you can get on all classes, you should get this if you have trouble leveling with a cotton shirt. You don't get any effect from having the whole set, so feel free to change some parts of your set for something stronger.
 Goibne's set 54 Thanatos' minions in Thanatos Tower This is the earliest set you can get as a Knight, it gives HP, SP, DEF, MDEF, VIT and elemental reductions. It used to be a really good set back in Pre-Renewal, it still is for beginners in Renewal. It can be quite hard if you're a beginner so check the market to see if you can find the equipments there instead.
 Odin's Blessing's sets 65 Skeggiold or Grizzly This one's part of the good old Pre-Renewal sets. Odin's Blessing can be combined with several different equipments for a total of 5 different sets; so if you find the armor, try to get one of the other stuffs to lessen your leveling pain.
 Ur's set 100
  • Armor dropped by Khalitzburg
  • Accessory dropped by Vanberk and Isilla
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 This set makes you a bit sturdier, and increases your Hundred Spear damage if you plan on using the skill a lot, alongside the possibility of using Auto Guard Lv 1. This should help you get through your harsh period of leveling if you plan to go on a offtank/tank leveling build.
 Peuz's set 100
  • Armor dropped by Raydric
  • Accessory dropped by Skogul and Frus
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 This set is for AGI Knight veterans who want to make full use of their powerful left click. You'll get an overall increase in damage, critical chance and your Sonic Wave's damage will be doubled. You will also autocast Concentration and Storm Blast (it's a rune skill, check the rune hyperlink in the skills' section for more info). It's also excellent for the new Wind Cutter build, and should be your primary goal when starting out on it.
 Gray Set 120 Ghost Palace This set will give you a really high +% Holy resistance per part of the set, and you can refine each piece of the set to increase even further the resistance. If you get all the pieces, you get +15% Neutral resistance and a chance to cast Drain Life on your enemies when you get physically (and melee) attacked.
 Airship's set 125 Airship Assault You'll get +25% HP & SP with this set, along with a permanent movespeed bonus.
Essences of Evil

If you don't know them, Essences of Evil (more commonly known as EoE) are card-like items that you can put anywhere, regardless of the item. You can get them in the instance Temple of the Demon God. These "cards" give bonuses based on their stat name, but they'll also decrease another stat. There's also 3 versions of each "stat card", the third one giving the biggest bonus (and it's also the most expensive one). If you aim for a budget build, you can get EoE 1 or 2 as they're usually incredibly cheap on the market.

Item Effect Lowest price Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 ... This is neat for getting more flat ATK, useful when you don't have anything you find useful to put in some slots like the headgears, the boots or you simply don't want to spend too much money on Gold Scaraba Cards for your accessories.
 Essence of Evil AGI 3 AGI+4, Flee+8, VIT-4 ... In case you were really craving for more AGI,you can get this EoE to help you achieving that sweet 193 maximum attack speed. Be careful though, this will decrease your VIT so if you were planning to get stun immunity, you might need to reset your stats to put more points there.
 Essence of Evil VIT 3 VIT+4, DEF+12, MDEF+8, AGI-4 ... This is often used by tanks as you can easily achieve thanks to its big MDEF bonus the frozen and stone curse immunity at 100 Hard MDEF; might be useful in case you're going for a tank build or a Dragon Breath build.
 Essence of Evil DEX 3 DEX+4, HIT+8, LUK-4 ... This EoE will only be useful in case you're going for a instant cast build like Spiral Pierce, because you'll need a LOT of DEX to complete the IC formula (INT+DEX*2=530).
 Essence of Evil LUK 3 LUK+4, Critical+4, DEX-4 ... You'll probably need this if you're aiming for 100% critical chance (without considering the critical defense of the enemies of course). If you're pretty close to 100 in Critical, you can forget about putting points in DEX as you'll be most of the time doing critical hits, which have perfect hit and aren't affected by your HIT rate (and this also means that the decrease in DEX of the EoE does nothing to you, so it's basically a win-win situation for you).
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Rideword's Hat [1] Upper Custom Headgear Quests This is a really strong hat as it gives you a chance to convert your damage as HP and/or SP. It's so great for leveling and farming that you might see Ridewords munching people's head pretty much everywhere in towns.
 Ancient Gold Ornament [1] Upper Biolab Gear Commonly known as AGO, it gives a neat ATK+8%. It's a great budget hat for high damage physical skills such as IB, Spiral or HS.
 Heart Wing Headband [1] Upper Master of Coin If your build is focused on spamming a skill and there's an ACD on it, this might be really good at +6 or +9 because it decreases your casting delay and your SP consumption. It starts at -5% Cast Delay and -10% SP Consumption, and is usually refined till +9 where it gives -14% Cast Delay and -19% SP Consumption.
 Abysmal Knight Helm [1] Upper Biolab Gear Increases your resistance to bosses and Demi-Humans by 10%. A specific tank hat but nice nonetheless for survival against MvPs.
 Ship Captain Hat [1] Upper Nova Shop This hat will be great if you plan on playing a DB build or spear build (Spiral or HS) as it's a really good investment, the only hat that gives a bit more %ranged damage costs about 500M (The increase in damage is not worth it in my opinion) whereas this one costs about ~25M depending on the rate of the Nova Shop reseller.
 Sigrun's Wings Middle Nova Shop Gives +1 flat ASPD, useful for building up a high APSD.
 Angel Spirit Middle Nova Shop ATK and MATK+2%, STR+2. Similar to Ancient Gold Ornament, it's great if you want to keep increasing your ATK; but you won't have a slot on this hat.
 Wing of Diablo [1] Middle Evil Wing Ears & Spiritual Auger from the Nova Shop It used to be one of the best slotted accessories you could get overall as a RK. The bonus is quite small though, but you get to use a card !
 Gemini-S58 Eyes Middle Nova Shop If you're looking for an alternative to a Gemini card because you want to use another card in your top hat and you can't afford a slotted middle hat, you could go for this one since it does the same thing as the card.
 Gangster Scarf Lower Custom Headgear Quest Gives a small bonus of ATK, always nice to have, especially on a slot where there's nothing really amazing at a low price.
 Scarlet Rose Lower Nova Shop Once you get a lot of ATK (let's say more than 600 on the bonus ATK in your stats), you might want to switch to this one instead of Bandit's Scarf because it will give more ATK.
 Samurai Mask Lower Military Headgear Box from the Nova Shop It gives +1% physical damage, it's better than Bandit's Scarf if you have a lot of ATK already.
 Well-chewed Pencil Lower Nova Shop If you're looking for Instant Cast for some reason or you're missing a lot on your hits, this might help you.
Dark Pinguicula Card Card Dark Pinguicula Gives you +10 ATK and a small chance to drop poisonous herbs. One of the cheapest headgear ATK cards you can get.
Duneyrr Card Card Duneyrr Gives you +10 ATK and a 1% chance to increase your Perfect Dodge by 10 for 4 seconds. It's a bit better than Dark Pinguicula for the second effect but you shouldn't waste your money on this one if you don't care about P.Dodge.
Marduk Card Card Marduk Silence immunity can be quite useful if you play a skill-spamming build like Dragon Breath or Ignition Break. It's really frustrating otherwise if you forget to bring green potions.
Vanberk Card Card Vanberk Gives you +2 STR and a very small chance (0.5%) of getting a temporary +100 Critical Chance bonus when doing physical damage; this will make you do critical hits nearly everytime during the duration, except against high LUK enemies. Don't worry about the small chance, it still happen often; 0.5% on each hit you do can happen much more frequently than you might think.
Gemini-S58 Card Card Gemini-S58 A great card to have to strengthen your resistance to status effects like Stone Curse.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Meteo Plate Armor [1] Salamander or Queen Scaraba An old armor, still performs good enough for early game as it gives you a small stun and freeze resistance.
 Frozen's Breastplate [1] Ferre or Jitterbug This is a cheap and slotted elemental armor you can get either on the market or from Jitterbug runs. You'll get the Water property once you equip it.
 Earthen's Breasplate [1] Nightmarish Jitterbug Same as the previous one, except that you get the Earth property instead.
 Diabolus Armor [1] Wounded Morroc or Satan Morroc Another old pre-renewal armor that can be equipped early on, it can be enchanted for a small stat bonus at the NPC in Prontera near the south gate.
 Hero Plate [1] Prize of Hero Good overall armor, it will take advantage of your INT in case you leveled it up a bit because it autocasts Heal and Storm Gust lvl 10 when you physically attack. Be careful though, the Storm Gust autocast might be more bothering than useful if you kill monsters one by one, since it keeps moving your enemies around.
 Engraved Armor [1] In the hidden room of Old Glast Heim Engraved Armor is really nice because it'll give you a big +25 MDEF and it has one of the highest DEF rates. It's very useful since the MATK formula update for monsters, to lessen the pain you get from the monsters who use strong magic (Golden Scaraba... oof).
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF. It emphasizes again on the all-out strategy where you don't care about your defense; if you play with a two-handed sword and use Parrying, this will not be a problem.
Ancient Mimic Card Ancient Mimic If you're playing on the critical build and you have trouble getting max ASPD or you want to spend less points into AGI, you can get this card since you'll have 120 LUK (because of the Temporal Boots of Luck) and get +6 AGI.
Bathory Card Bathory Bathory Card will enchant your armor with the Shadow property, allowing you to tank easily shadow and undead attacks from some monsters.
Evil Druid Card Evil Druid Evil Druid Card will enchant your armor with the Undead property, you'll get immunity to status effects like Stone Curse and Frozen. But be careful if you play in a party, you cannot be resurrected if you have undead property.
Marc Card Marc Marc Card will increase your resistance to Water element a little (5%) and give you Freeze immunity.
Peco Peco Card Peco Peco If you feel like you have not enough HP (even though you're a natural meat bag), you can opt for this neat 10% HP bonus. A good budget card you could use for a DB build.
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Krasnaya [3] Drake A 200 ATK two-handed sword with a rare capacity of 3 slots that gives you a small ATK bonus (+20) if you have 96 STR or more. This could prove to be a good alternative to other 2HS because of the versatility of the 3 slots; you could put a Hunter Fly card for life stealing and still keep 2 ~20% damage cards (like Hydra, Skeleton Worker, White Knight).
 Heavy Sword [1] In the hidden room of Old Glast Heim A 330 ATK two-handed sword made for full offensive, equipping it will give you +20 STR. Also, its weapon level is 1, so you can safely refine it to +7 (but it won't make a big difference since lvl 1 weapons don't get as much bonus as lvl 3 and 4).
 Atlas Weapon [1] Atroce This weapon is an underestimated versatile budget weapon. It increases your critical rate and has a big weight, so it can work for both the Critical and the Spiral builds.
 Crimson Twohand Sword [2] Tamruan or Baroness of Retribution or Abysmal Knight or Sword Master or Egnigem Cenia This sword is quite interesting if you manage to get it with the Fire element; it will increase your Ignition Break damage by +50%, making this skill quite effective for killing mob trains. Most monsters in endgame content are weak to Fire, so your damage should increase decently.
 Death Guidance [2] Amdarais A 200 ATK two-handed sword that give you a lot of survival capacity; it gives you +20 Perfect Dodge and the possibility to do an AoE life steal when you physically attack. Watch out for the Hell Power that you can sometimes autocast on yourself, it'll prevent you from being resurrected for several minutes.
 Thanatos Great Sword [1] Ghost Palace This two-handed sword is really nice for survival because it gives you a chance to regenerate a small part of the damage you do on a attack, including AoE attacks. It's really strong on Ignition Break and Dragon Breath builds; if you have a Rideword Hat and a Hunter Fly Card in your weapon you'll regenerate lots of HP quite often. Since the new Ghost Palace update, you can also enchant your Thanatos weapon, you can get nice effects like an elemental enchantment (they're similar to Vicious Mind enchantments).
 Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Great Demon Baphomet in Sealed Shrine Tae Goo Lyeon is a weapon mostly used for end-game Dragon Breath build because of its bonuses when refined at +9; your cast delay between skills gets reduced by 20%, same thing for your SP consumption. You'll even be able to enchant it with %ranged damage twice (Expert Archer enchantment).
 Crimson Spear [2] Stem Worm or Naga One of the famous crimson weapons. The base ATK is low but it'll get much stronger thanks to the special ATK bonus that increases each time you refine it, up to +15. It's a very interesting choice thanks to its element option, it allows you to disregard element enchant consumables or skills, making it a good investment if you plan on staying in a place for a long time (Fire-enchanted for Scaraba Hole, Holy-enchanted for Gefenia, OGH, Ghost Palace....).
 Crimson Lance [2] Owl Duke or Anacondaq or Gryphon Pretty much the same as the spear, but this one is two-handed and has more weight; it's more offensive-oriented (since you can't use a shield anymore) and is a better choice for Spiral Pierce than the spear if you want to stay in the crimson weapons.
 Crescent Scythe [0] Baphomet You want to do a critical build but you're too poor to afford big critical bonus items ? Fear not, the Crescent Scythe is here for you with its whooping +30 critical ! But be careful if you're going to use Turisus Rune as it'll enable the possibility of breaking your weapon, and this one isn't indestructible. You might want to try slotting the weapon, and in case you manage to get a Crescent Scythe slotted, put a Golem Card inside to have an indestructible weapon and forget about the possibility of breaking your item.
 Robot's Mechanical Arm [2] Charleston 3 It's about the same as the previous one but there are some differences: first of all it's a mace so it's an indestructible weapon (special property of all maces), it has 2 slots whereas the Crescent Scythe doesn't have one by default (and can only get one if you manage to slot it), and the critical bonus is smaller (20 instead of 30). You'll also have a much better ASPD with it since it's a one-handed mace (the previous weapon is a two-handed spear). It used to be my main weapon when I started my RK career, because of how good and underrated it is.
 Crimson Mace [2] Li Me Mang Ryang or Petite or Errende Ebecee or Solider The reason why you would want to go for this weapon is either because you have one with a good elemental advantage (Fire and Holy are great) and refined +7 or more (otherwise you'd probably better off with a Robot's Mech Arm +7~), either it's simply refined past +10 and you wish to make use of it (even if it has a useless element like Poison).
Golem Card Golem You'll get a small ATK bonus (+5) and the indestructible property on your weapon. Very useful if you wish to use Turisus and Rhydo runes and your weapon is not indestructible by default.
Abysmal Knight Card Abysmal Knight This is the card you'll probably want to use if you plan on killing MvPs since it gives +25% damage against bosses. Because Geffenia is a common farming map, you can get this card really cheap ! A good choice for MvP beginners.
Banaspaty Card Banaspaty Banaspaty isn't the usual card you would expect on a weapon but it has already proved its worth on high HP enemies. It only works on normal monsters, boss monsters are immune to the Burning status.
Hunter Fly Card Hunter Fly If you plan on defeating all your enemies by grouping them up together and using AoE attacks, this is for you. Hunter Fly Card allows you to regenerate health based on the damage you deal, at a low chance. Hitting more monsters means you're repeating the probability several times, and it ramps up the chance of making the card proc; add this card to a Thanatos Weapon and use a Rideword and you'll notice you get full health in no time while killing monsters, basically making you unstoppable machine that does not need a support or potions. The skills you would want to use with this combo, are Ignition Break, Bowling Bash, Magnum Break and the Storm Blast rune (this means using a consumable (the rune) but it's freaking strong).
Knight Sakray Card Ghost Palace The chance of you using this card is pretty low simply because there aren't a lot of them on the server since it's quite new, they are currently expensive, but you could theorically get them for free if you farm Ghost Palace daily (you need 10,000 Gray Shards). It's one of the best card you can have for an evil cleansing purpose as it gives a neat ATK bonus and a big 30% increase in damage against Undeads and Demons.
White Knight Card Old Glast Heim This card IS the meta card for all physical damage dealers. It gives a 20% physical damage increase against medium and large monsters (most of the monsters you'll encounter mid to late game) and a small ATK bonus. If you're playing any one-handed weapon, you might want to get the combo with Khalitzburg Knight card which does the same in the defensive category, and getting the set will give you another 15% increase in damage. They cannot be dropped, but they can be crafted at the entrance of the instance Old Glast Heim against drops of the instance (it's much easier to create them with loots of the Hard Mode).
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Platinum Shield Sword Guardian This shield doesn't have a slot, but it does a 15% reduction effective for most enemies (Medium and Large) and also 10% reduction against Undead monsters (the race, not the element). It's also great for fighting against magic, because it gives a small +5 MDEF bonus and also a 15% chance to get Magic Mirror for 2 seconds (40% chance to reflect magic attacks) everytime you're magically attacked.
 Rosa Shield [1] Alice or Dark Pinguicula or Alicel It's a basic cheap slotted shield that you can get fairly easily, and has one of the highest defense rates (even though defense is not really important anymore in Renewal).
 Strong Shield [1] Bloody Knight If you are getting knocked away by skills like Jupitel Thunder too often and you hate it, you might want to take a look at this shield. This is a shield that gives you immunity to Knockback, but it'll increase all the damage you receive by 20%; you should try to get a card that compensates the damage amplification like Khalitzburg Knight Card or Hodremlin Card.
 Valkyrja's Shield [1] Valkyrie It's the favourite shield of a lot of PvP players, mainly because it gives a 20% damage reduction against Fire, Water, Shadow and Undead properties, and it used to be pretty much the best shield back in Pre-Renewal. If you need survivability against monsters that use nasty magic skills like Dark Soul Strike or Dark Grand Cross, this shield will be pretty neat.
Hodremlin Card Hodremlin This card gives a 15% physical reduction against all sizes so it's great if you only want to keep one shield. There's also supposed to be a chance to get +30 Perfect Dodge during 10 seconds, but I've heard that this was currently not working, if you feel like this is important, you should make a suggestion on the forum to remind our dear developpers about the issue or post on a already existing topic about it.
Thara Frog Card Thara Frog This the card you need to get if you plan on doing some PvP action or grinding in an area with lots of demi-human monsters.
Alice Card Alice Really cheap in case you want to start doing field MvPs (as they are easier to do solo than instance MvPs).
Gaster Card Gaster If you plan on simply grinding on normal monsters and avoiding bosses, this is a great card against all kinds of monsters.
Horn Card Horn If you don't mind switching your stuff often, getting a Horn Card is great when you're up against ranged monsters (like Kavach Icarus for example). You'll greatly increase your chances of survival if you get swarmed.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). If you don't have any, you might want to get one of the cheapest for starters. The +10 MDEF is really neat and if you get a pair of Temporal Boots (any of the boots, even the basic ones should work), you'll also get a +15% HP and +5% SP set bonus.
 Nidhoggur's Shadow Garb [1] Nidhoggur Shadow This one might be a bit complicated to obtain if you're new, but it can be a really good alternative to GSS if you plan on playing Dragon Breath or Ignition Break build and you need a bit of survivability: this garment gives you a +7% resistance to ALL elements and a 1% chance to regenerate 1% of your damage dealt on one attack (AoE attacks work). You also have a SP bonus per refine so if you get a high enough refine, you can compensate a little for the lack of the HP&SP bonus from the GSS set.
 Valkyrian Manteau [1] Valkyrie Randgris The Valkyrian Manteau won't help much in terms of defense but you'll get a +% reflect based on your refine so it can be nice to help proc some bonuses that work on physical attacks dealt to the enemies.
Giant Whisper Card Giant Whisper This card should be pretty affordable since MCAs are kind of common now (even though they're still expensive) and people sell most not wanted mini bosses' cards quite cheap. Its effects are : +10 FLEE, +20 ATK if your STR is 80+, MHP+3% if your VIT is 80+, CRIT+3 if your LUK is 80+. There are much better choices out there on garment so you should only keep this for the beginning.
Jejeling Card Jejeling 200 flat HP every 10 VIT points. Really nice if you plan on doing a Dragon Breath Build, you'll reach 2,4K bonus HP with this card if you go for 120 VIT.
Noxious Card Noxious Great for PvP, this card gives +10% resistance to neutral property attacks and +10% resistance to ranged physical attacks.
Raydric Card Raydric Increases your resistance to neutral property attacks by 20%. This one is really good because all monsters hit physically with neutral attacks, so you reduce most of the damage from monsters by 20%. This is really great for grinding solo or doing tough monsters.
Wakwak Card Wakwak This is one of the garment stat cards, it will increase your ATK based on your STR. You get +5 ATK every 10 base STR points.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat This card is a better version of Wakwak Card, you will get more ATK and a great ASPD bonus but it's more expensive than Wakwak.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Variant Shoes Beelzebub These boots used to be expensive in Pre-Renewal but not anymore, since most players prefer using the "new" Temporal Boots from Old Glast Heim. I suggest getting them from the market, because killing Beelzebub is difficult. They give a big 20% increase in both HP and SP but beware, don't upgrade them or you'll lose % bonuses per refine made on the shoes.
 Temporal Boots Old Glast Heim If you find the enchanted Temporal Boots on the market too expensive, and you're fine with the HP&SP set bonus with the Giant Snake Skin, you can get these because the bonus works even with these.
 Temporal Boots of Strength Old Glast Heim The Temporal STR Boots are usually not super expensive, and provide a great ATK bonus; if you refine it at +3 (safe refine) and you have 120 STR, you'll get 57 ATK thanks to these boots. You get +50 ATK by having 120 points in STR, and you get +7 ATK every 3 refines.
 Temporal Boots of Dexterity Old Glast Heim The DEX boots are great in case you're spamming skills with Fixed Cast Time. These are the boots you should get in case you play a skill spam build like Dragon Breath or Spiral Pierce, because it gets rid of 0.5 seconds of Fixed Cast Time if you have at least 120 in DEX (which is in most case, enough to eliminate the FCT of your skill's cast).
Green Ferus Card Green Ferus The usual easy-to-get card that gives you a nice +10% HP buff (it gets tripled during Berserk so +30% max HP is pretty good).
Matyr Card Matyr Same as Green Ferus Card, but it gives +1 AGI instead of +1 VIT. You might want to take this one instead if you need every possible bonus for your ASPD.
Verit Card Verit Easy to obtain, it's ok for a Dragon Breath build as it increases both your HP and your SP by 8%.
Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie This is one of the few offensive cards on the boots card slot, it's only worth it if you refine your boots a lot (something like +6 to +9), and it might be a bit expensive for beginners.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Sheriff's Left Badge Rock Ridge's main quest For what it does, this accessory is pretty strong. It suits every build you could play as a RK since it increases your ATK by 3%, your HP by 1000 and your ranged damage by 3% if you leveled up your stats to at least 90. (respectively STR, VIT and DEX). To get it, you only need to do the main quest of Rock Ridge (Fistful of Zeny), which is mostly speaking to NPCs and you only need to be level 100 to do it.
 Sarah's Right Earring Sarah and Fenrir This accessory eliminates the need of Fly Wings or a Creamy card, and you can enchant it for great effects like Expert Archer or Fatal. While the accessory is easy to get (because you only need to complete the instance once), you need Shards of Gigantes to enchant the earring, which you can get from the instance or on the market (the prices dropped right now, after the enchants on GMT rings came out). You can get more accessories by spending 1 Shard of Gigantes for each accessory, and you can also get a Left Earring if you want to have 2 of them at the same time. The accessory is account-bound so you can't buy it off the market.
 Str Glove Eclage You're looking for more ATK and the other accessories are too expensive ? Look no further, this is one of the possible budget choices. The ATK you'll get is kind of small for an accessory though.
 Luk Glove Eclage This glove is great if you're in dire need of critical hits. You get +1 CRIT per 10 LUK base points and 1% critical damage if you have 110+ LUK.
 Peuz's Seal Skogul or Frus This is a RK-only accessory, it gives 20 ATK and 20 SP. It's also possible to enchant it; it's an ok ATK budget accessory.
Kobold Card Kobold Gives critical rate and STR, it's cheaper than a EoE Luk, you can get this if you're on a strict budget.
Gold Scaraba Card Gold Scaraba This is the card that gives the most flat ATK on the accessory slot. If you're playing with a low ATK weapon, this might be better than the Buffalo combo (since it gives a % bonus on your ATK).
Tiyanak Card Tiyanak In case you'd want to do a critical build in PvP, this will give you a lot of crits.
Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Str+4 and ATK+4%, and you get a strong effect if you combine this card with the next one.
Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Shotgun Buffalo Bandit AGI+7 and HIT+7, and if you combine it with the previous one, you'll also get STR+3 and ATK+3%.
Shadow Gears

These sets can be obtained in the Monster Hunter (MH1) special instance; there you can hunt a special MvP of your choice with your team, and earn components from the monster's body to craft your set (like in the real MH game). As it can be quite difficult for some gears, I advise you to check the wiki and learn everything you need to know beforehand. MH2 shadow sets will come at a later date for each build when I have the time to write them down.

Builds

Please do remember that there's not always a "BEST BUILD", and that all builds are viable. One may pop ahead of the rest and become "THE META" but it will also come accompanied by scarcity and high prices of the corresponding gears. All builds have different strengths and weaknesses, will peak in performance (and also differ in prices) at different steps of the game, from early to endgame.

Critical AA

Remember these wise words from your sensei:

  • The best defense is a good offense, and the best offense is a good ol' AA RK

Even though the Critical AA build that I'll teach you may seem appealing, please do not forget that's it's not easy to exp with it, especially if you follow the stats, which are given for level 175 (You'll get nowhere with 1 point in DEX if you don't have a great critical rate). You should first take a look at the Wind Cutter build as it's easier to do and it'll give you a spike in damage when leveling after switching to Rune Knight.

Stats

Here are the stats I use for my Crit RK:

  • STR 120
  • AGI 100+
  • VIT 90+
  • INT 40+
  • DEX 1
  • LUK 120

If you're not stuffed good enough yet or want to play solo without foods, AB buffs or a Minstrel, you might want to switch STR and AGI so you can get 190~ ASPD. This build has the goal of making the highest melee damage possible, and it's much better to get as much attack speed as possible before trying to upgrade your damage, since it outshines the little atk boost you get from the 20 last points you could put in STR.

Skills

How to Crit RK 101:

I'm not even kidding here, these are the only 3rd class skills you need to perform correctly as a Critical Rune Knight. Critical build is all about buffing before simply auto-attacking the enemy, no other skills required. Of course, there are several 2nd class skills that you mustn't forget !

RK November 2019 rework update: Ignition Break and Sonic Wave will be able to crit, and Enchant Blade will get buffed, so don't miss out on these skills !

Strategy

The strategy on a Critical build is pretty simple; buff yourself as much as possible before going Berserk and killing everything. The skills and buffs you need to cast before Berserk are better used in this order, because of their duration:

Auto Berserk > Berserk Potion > Enchant Blade > Two-Hand Quicken > Aura Blade > Turisus Runestone > Asir Runestone > Rhydo Runestone > Concentration > Parrying > Magnum Break > Berserk

This might seem like it's kind of useless but if the fight drags on, you're still under Berserk and your buffs start disappearing (like the runes for example), you will lose a big part of your DPS and end up waiting for Berserk to stop so you can buff again, making you possibly lose a lot of precious time.

If you're simply killing lots of trash mobs, you could also forget Berserk as it could lead to your doom since you could get mobbed and get crushed because your FLEE is halved and you got 0 DEF/MDEF. This is something I try to avoid in Sky Fortress for example, as the Ragged Zombies there hurt quite a lot. Instead, switch to this combo:

Auto Berserk > Berserk Potion > Enchant Blade > Two-Hand Quicken > Aura Blade > Turisus Runestone > Asir Runestone > Rhydo Runestone > Concentration > Parrying

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the Critical AA build. Don't forget that you can always take a look again at the General Equipment list, if some items here do not suit you or they are too expensive for you.

Sets

I keep together the set pieces that are only worth running together here.

Set Way to obtain Notes
 Peuz's set
  • Armor dropped by Raydric
  • Accessory dropped by Skogul and Frus
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 You're just starting out but wanna play critical AA, and just hearing about the cost of Lux Anima runes makes you sweat ? Fear not ! The Peuz set allows you to autocast Storm Blast without using Lux runes ! It can be enchanted with critical chance enchants if you manage somehow to get your armor and garment to +9. The full set also gives you +100% damage to Sonic Wave so it's a nice bonus when hunting mobs and teleporting.
 Grace Knight set Eden Academy A fairly new set that is available through a custom beginner content, this practically free set will boost you in many ways: ATK, ASPD, critical damage... If you have no gears yet, going for this set will help you get more easily into midgame. My only issue with it if you're starting out is that it provides basically no critical rate, so you'll have to rely on other sources like your base LUK, buffs or manage to set in your stuff some crit rate equipments/cards. A good idea would be to combine it with the Fox Ear Ribbons which will solve all your crit rate issues in the beginning.
 YSF01 Seyren's set YSF01 Seyren The YSF01 set is a fairly nice armor if you get every piece +9, for content with sky-high DEF thanks to its DEF pierce ability. It provides also a good amount of ATK% and %Critical damage but only if you get the stat requirements (125 STR and 125 LUK respectively).
 Illusion Sprint set Illusion of Twins The Illusion Sprint combo between the Mail and the 2 accessories (Ring and Glove) is actually a very interesting underdog option. The armor by itself offers a few VIT points as well as 2 Nive slots on which you can put Powerful Nives for up to +14% damage to all races, and can be comboed with the 2 accessories for a whooping +15% max HP/SP !. The accessories cannot have Nives but they can be enchanted with some stats. You can then combo these pieces with the Shoes as well, which will bring a lot to the table as well: +10% ATK, +70 ATK, +25% damage against bosses when comboing the Mail and the Shoes, then with the Shoes and the accessories you will get some on-hit chances to gain the gigantic +150 STR and +150 AGI buffs ! Beweare though, the combo of the shoes with the accessories will continuously drain your HP and SP, so you might want to have some swap equipment to avoid losing HP&SP when not fighting, and bring some leech effects if you plan on using this combo so you can regenerate in the middle of the fight.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Fox Ear Ribbons [1] Top Nova Shop This hat gives 10% ASPD bonus, and when you physically attack, you have a chance of transforming into Moonlight Flower: it gives you a %ranged damage bonus, and +100% critical chance. I've seen this hat being used sometimes on Crit RK builds so I thought I would add it here, but this isn't that worth it as there are many ways to achieve +100% critical chance. But it could still be viable since you'd free a lot of other equipment/card slots; you wouldn't need to get any critical bonus anymore, and you could theoretically invest strongly on pure power (like ATK). I consider them training wheels that will allow you to get a 100% critical rate until you get the items required to have it.
 Snake Head Hat [1] Top Nova Shop This cute little buddy is your best early friend as it gives you the thief skill Double Attack at level 5. Since a patch from several years ago, you can both proc critical attacks and double attacks on the same hit. This is in my opinion core to the build as you get a big DPS spike thanks to your high ASPD and your already sky-high damage. Do not forget that also the Turisus rune sometimes doubles the damage of one of your hits, and it stacks with Double Attack. Yes, the quadruple attack spike is not a dream, and it's theoretically possible to use it on the dreadful Crush Strike rune.
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat.s.
 Clark Sidecap [1] Top Master of Coin From a recent hat update bringing lots of combos regarding the OS weapons from episode 17.1, this hat is pretty interesting amongst its pairs, especially for us, because of not only its combo with the Beam Claymore-OS but also for the perks it gives by itself; it gives 20 ATK every 2 refines, and 2 great boosts at refines +9 and +11: at +9 we get the rare melee modifier with a whooping +15% (Melee modifier works the same as ranged%, it acts as a final modifier so it's very interesting to have) and at +11 we get a +15% size modifier to Small and Medium.
 Illusion Hot-blooded Headband [1] Top Illusion of Teddy Bear An unexpected contender to the critical AA scene, this hat is there to balance out the mountain of critical damage% you've got. If you aren't lacking in critical hit, this hat provides a ton of bonuses based on the refine of the hat : +10% damage against against wind, water, earth and neutral monsters at +7, +15% damage against small and large monsters at +9. It can also be enchanted, the most recommended enchant for us is the Powerful Nive which, depending on its level, gives a bonus of STR at a specific refine and an all races% bonus at a higher refine. Thanks to all these bonuses, this option can get pretty close and on specific targets (thanks to the elemental bonuses) it can even overcome the ORC's damage if you already have a lot of crit damage. Beware as it doesn't bring any critical rate, so to switch from ORC to this hat, you might need to rebuild a bit your overall stuff !
 Old Rune Circlet [1] Top Tomb of the Fallen Currently one of the strongest hats for its refine bonuses and enchants, but also the hardest to get. Every 2 refines, you have 20% bonus damage on Ignition Break, and 15% on Hundred Spear. On the Critical build, you'll want the Acute enchantment, which gives Crit+3 and Critical Damage+15% every level after the first one.
 Racing Cap (Rune Knight) [1] Top Ancient Juperos A strong contender to the Old Rune Circlet, this weapon will give you Double Attack Lv5, 50% critical damage and will also make your weapon indestructible. If you manage to get the Racing enchant for RK, you'll get even more damage through the bonus %size mod and ATK, as well as get a chance to ignore size penalty temporarily when attacking. Depending on the situation this hat can beat the ORC, but it is not a clear win depending on how you gear up; I have performed some calculations that are available on my author page you can access here.
 Tiger King Doll Hat-LT [1] Top Master of Coin An improved version of the White Drooping Eddga, this one provides a lot of bonuses even outside of the transformation: +2 STR,DEX,POW,CON and 10% ASPD and damage against Brute monsters by default, up to +25% Melee mods and +10% ATK through refines, as well as up to 5% ATK, +3 POW and +9 P.ATK through grading. For the transformation part, we get gifted with amazing boosts: +35 ATK per refine and +20 P.ATK if the hat is refined at least to +10 ! That hat can be very viable because of the huge steroid buff it gives, but beware as it does not provide any critical damage.
 Sigrun's Wings Middle Nova Shop As shown in the general equipment part, this will give you a flat ASPD point. It might be useful in case you want to reduce the AGI you have and invest the points somewhere else, or simply if you're stuck at 191 or 192 and need a little help.
 Wing of Diablo [1] Middle Evil Wing Ears & Spiritual Auger from Nova Shop If you're fine on both critical and ASPD, you can then opt for ATK items. Get these ears alongside an EoE STR 3. You may also go for the Angel Wing Ears if you prefer.
 Fafnir Skin Middle Weakened Fafnir's quest This hat gives +3% Critical chance. It comboes with the Fafnir Mask, they give together +5% Critical chance as well as +5% Critical damage (as a combo). The natural HP regeneration loss is no problem for us as we can always pull Berserk in case of low HP.
 Magical Booster [1] Middle Magical Booster quest This hat allows us to get good bonuses such as critical rate, raw ATK and ATK%, while having an available card slot. As a Critical RK, you'll want to get critical rate (or raw ATK if you already got too much critical rate) and ATK%.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD%, but what interests us the most is the enchant part since we can get up to 6 critical rate through that, while keeping a card slot.
 CD in Mouth Lower Nova Shop This will help in case you need to proc temporal boots enchants like Lucky Day or Runaway Magic; it autocasts bolts randomly when physically attacking, and it synergises well with Enchant Blade.
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good budget option as it directly increases your physical damage by 1%.
 Fafnir Mask Lower Weakened Fafnir's quest It gives +2% Critical chance and combos with the Fafnir Skin shown before.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin. Going for that hat as well as a GSS full of STR will give you a good increase in damage, resilience and attack speed. It's a nice alternative especially when you already have too much critical damage, as this combo will give you a great amount of ATK.
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest This is pretty interesting as a lower hat for its all stats and ATK bonuses, if you're not using a FWM (in which case a VMA would be the best) nor the Fafnir Skin, it is a very strong lower hat you can get.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, one could argue the +2 all stats is better than the +1 version with 5 ATK, considering Storm Blast scales directly with STR. As it directly depends on the rest of your gears and the difference is really small, it's something you have to test by yourself.
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory The most expensive and rare lower hat, it is also for now the BiS hat for us, when in combo with the Fallen Warrior Manteau. It brings effects similar to the Heroic Backpack, bringing us ATK, ASPD and critical damage based on our stat investment.
 Silver Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Melee damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Phylla Card Card Phylla Before the Bio5 update I used this to get past the 100 critical cap as it procs often enough with high ASPD (Vanberk is not worth it as the chance is too low, here it's ok to get a smaller bonus since we already have critical from everywhere else). Stacking 2 Phylla cards will make it proc quite often.
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This new card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you should go for an EoE STR 3. The endure effect won't be of any use to us as we already got it under Berserk.
 Angra Mantis Card Card Angra Mantis It only gives 3% critical damage since we're not a Thief class, but you'll want to put this in case you get the Chaotic Killer Mantis Card for a bonus 5% critical damage.
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A very good ATK hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus but considering our build is not concerned by HP, you shouldn't bother and just put an offensive card on the shoes.
 Deep Sea King Dramoh Card Card Deep Sea King Dramoh This card is able to overcome the Purple Ferus Card thanks to its combo with Deep Sea Merman Card (check out the shoes section to learn more about it). The card by itself though brings just a bit of ATK% based on the refine of your hat, so if you don't plan on using the combo set, it is recommended to stay on the Purple Ferus Card as it's better in that case. Also in case you were worried about your health pool, there's another combo with the normal King Dramoh Card that brings +15% HP, effectively canceling the con of that card and bringing at the same time 10% more HP.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Abusive Robe [1] You can craft it with 600 Honor Tokens, these are obtainable in the Banquet for Heroes quests. This is the more common robe for physical builds since you get a %defense bypass on Demi-Humans, Undeads and Demons per refine, as well as the skill Attention Concentrate at level 1 (Very nice as we love everything that revolves around AGI&ASPD). The reason why it's commonly used and refined to +7 is also because of the enchants you can apply on it. If you manage to get one overrefined to +11 or more, you'll get much bigger benefits from the enchants, as well as a very good %DEF pierce.
 Excellion Suit Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from the instances Charleston Crisis and King's Heels This used to be a very good armor you could get for offensive purposes, as you can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki.
 Lava Leather Suit [1] Magma Dungeon F3 This armor increases your ATK by a lot, and if you manage to get it +9, you'll even benefit from its neat critical damage bonus. It provides more ATK when it's +7 than a +7 Excellion Suit with STR ATK ATK blueprints.
 Soaring Physical Armor [1] Temporal Armors This armor unknown by many is actually very handy for leveling up, as it can be equipped at level 1 and offers a nice flat amount of ATK as well as ATK% and physical damage and pierce on Demon & Brute monsters, and comboes with the Temporal Boots of Strength for more ATK% and DEF pierce. It can be enchanted with many interesting stats as well as neat properties like undestructible armor or a random element for your armor.
