 Unexpected Fortune Armor [1] Temporal Armors Same as the previous armor, this is the LUK version; it will combo of course with the Temporal Boots of Luck and will provide critical damage% instead of ATK%.
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the LLSuit and the YSF01 Plate thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants at least, and if you wanna use that armor on other classes like SS Ranger, you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Luk Soutane [1] Odin's Past The Luk Soutane is an interesting choice in case you're going for IB autocast or critical on MH2, as you need a gigantic amount of critical rate, and this armor gives us a ton of it : we get critical rate, damage and LUK per refine. At +12 the armor gives +18 Crit rate, +20 LUK which gives also +6 Crit rate, and 24% Critical damage. The special Luk enchant gives us +10 LUK, +15% Crit damage, +10 Crit rate and +12% DMG against all sizes. So in total you get : +37 Critical rate, 39% Critical damage and +12% against all sizes. The only downside of this armor is the lack of ATK bonuses, so it's really a compromise you need to decide on.
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it very competitive for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races.
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new contender from 17.2 ! This armor can be enchanted with a variety of different enchants, the interesting ones for us are  Automatic Module (Critical Force) to help us reaching a good spot on our critical rate if using a garment without any critical rate bonus (like Temporal STR/AGI manteaux), and  Automatic Module (Attacker Force) for the rare melee modifier it provides. You may also go for the  Automatic Module (Power) if you are looking for a cheap module.
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. Also we now get access to other skills through these enchants, and this time there's a very specific one we want to go for: the Wolf Orb (Melee Duple). This Archbishop enchant provides us 40% Melee at +11, making it effectively a super strong and versatile replacement for skill mods, very useful for us. The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the huge amount of ATK, ATK% and Melee% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF. It emphasizes again on the all-out strategy where you don't care about your defense; if you play with a two-handed sword and use Parrying, this will not be a problem.
 Ancient Mimic Card Ancient Mimic Good if you're really craving for more AGI, as it gives 2 more points than a EoE Agi 3, without any downside.
 Mistress of Shelter Card Mistress of Shelter This is a necessary card for the combo with the Thanatos Tower garment card (Happiness Giver).
 Bathory Card Bathory If like me, you play in a lot of content with Shadow property attacks, you'll take a liking to the Bathory card. Don't forget that under Berserk, you have 0 MDEF, so magic attacks will hurt like a truck. If you can get yourself resilient to them, then your life will be much easier.
Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, and it's pretty cheap ! Very useful for these weapons that get broken by the Rhydo runestone.
Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric I wouldn't usually put this kind of card in the armor, but if you have enough critical rate and damage and you're mostly trying to be more tanky, I'd go for that card in combo with the Raydric Card for that amazing total 30% neutral resistance, as well as that neat 10% ATK.
Hardworking Pitman Card Hardworking Pitman A card very similar to the previous one, you may go for this one if you already got it and do not own the C.Raydric one.
Furious Ninetail Card Angry Nine Tail A very affordable option to grind on critical chance ! It gives +5% Critical chance, +10% Critical damage and another +10% Critical chance if your armor is +10 or more.
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Atlas Weapon [1] Atroce A decent budget choice for Crit RK, as it provides +10% Critical Hit and it's quite heavy so it works well with Crush Strike. Its only weakness is that it's not indestructible, so you might want to put a Golem Card (usually cheap so it should go well with a budget build).
 Crimson Mace [2] Li Me Mang Ryang or Petite or Errende Ebecee or Solider The reason why you would want to go for this weapon is either because you have one with a good elemental advantage (Fire and Holy are great) and refined +7 or more (otherwise you'd probably better off with a Robot's Mech Arm +7~), either it's simply refined past +10 and you wish to make use of it (even if it has a useless element like Poison) because you want to play more defensively with a racial/elemental carded shield that will keep you alive.
 Vicious Mind Mace [1] Immortal Zombie Assault The update to the Vicious Mind weapons actually make them pretty strong now, especially if you can get the weapon to +15 and get specific enchants like +% Boss damage, +% Critical damage; getting perfect enchants could make it rival the Lindy Hop in terms of damage, but the problem is that you have to get Critical hit by other means unlike the Lindy Hop and its Sharp enchants.
 Robot's Mechanical Arm [2] Charleston 3 I already talked about this one previously but I got to where I am currently thanks to this weapon so that's partly the reason why it appears here. Basically it's more or less the same fight as JDR vs Crimson Katar; the crimson weapons give a neat ATK bonus but they're only level 3 weapons (Check the Refinement System for more information on weapon levels). The Mech' Arm is a weapon to surpass Metal Gear a level 4 weapon with quite the correct ATK for a one-handed weapon, has 2 slots and most importantly gives a gigantic +20 Critical Chance bonus. This means you can invest less in LUK and Critical bonus items and cards, and get something else more interesting to further increase your DPS.
 Gigantic Blade [1] Charleston 3 This two-handed sword has a very good weapon ATK and weight, making it quite effective for Spiral Pierce, and it increases % critical damage based on its refine. Its downsides are that big -15% ASPD penalty and the fact that it only has one slot. It has gotten better though, since the arrival of the instance King's Heels and the possibility of enchanting the Charleston weapons with enchants similar to VM weapons.
 Vicious Mind Two-handed Sword [1] Immortal Zombie Assault Same as the VM Mace: if you can get the weapon to +15 and get specific enchants like +% Boss damage, +% Critical damage, it can rival the Lindy Hop in terms of damage, but the problem is that you have to get Critical hit by other means unlike the Lindy Hop and its Sharp enchants. The Ominous Assaulter & Heater combo might be pretty neat here.
 Royal Knight's Broadsword [2] Abyss Glast Heim This new addition to the two-handed swords roster is a pretty good rival to Lindy Hop, and will surpass Vicious Mind in terms of ATK. Unlike this last one who needs a special enchant in order to be unbreakable by itself, this one just needs to be refined to +9 for that. The Broadsword will get enchants later, which might make it worthwhile. Despite its strong bonuses, it has the same problem as the other weapons that the Lindy Hop doesn't suffer from, it's the lack of ASPD, which means you have to compensate in stats or other equipments for that.
 Oriental Sword [2] Ancient Hero A weapon considered rather pretty meme, the Oriental Sword is an autocast 2HS that casts Sonic Wave. Its inconsistency with the autocast and the fact that it relies on a ranged skill makes it difficult to build around it, but it still brings a strong autocasted skill to the table; my suggestion with this weapon is to just build as usual on your RK and not bother with ranged bonuses except if you can freely add some in your build (aka it doesn't prevent you from taking other important mods). I'd recommend upgrading it to the Patent version as soon as you can, if you desire to go down this route.
 Guardian Knight Claymore [2] Glast Heim Challenge Mode A weapon that came out with the late update of Challenge Glast Heim, this weapon is like its update, kind of outdated. It still is decent if properly refined though, and is kind of a more racial hunting oriented version of the Lindy, for Undead and Angel monsters. If you have many Temporal Fragments taking the dust and you're looking for a potential budget option, this may be interesting for you.
 Illusion Death Guidance [2] Illusion of Underwater A new version of the good old Death Guidance has popped out, in a form of a critical weapon boosting up Storm Blast ! It is highly recommended to use it at least refined to +11 for the critical bonuses it provides. While it won't be able to outperform the Claw Sword, it might be a good budget contender against the other weapons if enchanted.
 Lindy Hop [2] Stefan or Immortal Cursed Knight Prior to the arrival of the Claw Sword, it was the wet dream of each Rune Knight. This weapon used to be the most endgame two-handed sword we could get, and had the right to stay at the n1 spot as a weapon for RKs thanks to all the pros it has. It has the most ATK out of all 2HS, has 2 slots, gives ATK% and ASPD% bonuses based on the refine, is indestructible (goodbye Golem Card), and is enchantable twice (Malangdo Enchant. Getting a Lindy past +10 used to be every main Crit RK's goal (You can settle for a +8 if you find it too hard or too expensive to go further in the refine hell).
 Poison Forged Spear [3] Venomous Chimera This is a new weapon from the 16.2 episode Terra Gloria, it has potential because it frees up space on the upper headgear slot if you were using Snake Head Hat, and it has 3 slots even though it's a level 4 weapon ! Thanks to the changes to Turisus and Double Attack, this weapon somehow rose above Lindy Hop in both survivability and DPS on Medium enemies; however Rhydo is still a risky bet since it can still break your weapon, and the Lindy Hop still wins on Large monsters. Beware as it's still weaker than Claw Sword, the weapon is overhyped probably for business reasons.
 Beam Claymore-OS [2] Illusion (17.1) The new two-handed sword contender from 17.1 seems able to overpower the Lindy Hop on specific cases, due to its +11 refine bonus which gives +20% damage against Small and Medium sizes. It has a low crit rate bonus but since we have access to Acute and the new Illusion critical enchants, it's not a big problem. It can also be enchanted pretty good with ATK% and %critical damage. While I heard it can beat higher refine Lindies, I believe that the fact it only has a %size damage increase against Small and Medium but not Large (which are a big part of the MvPs), makes me think it's not that interesting. This weapon got a nice boost thanks to its new combo with the Clark Sidecap, allowing it to compensate its weakness on Large monsters by bringing a huge 4% large size modifier every 2 refines of the weapon.

Whether it is worth replacing a Snake Hat or an ORC, is something I am currently unable to say; we still lack data on the sword as too few people tried refining it, and I'll need someone to lend me one to be able to test. If you were to use this weapon, I'd recommend after checking out the overall bonuses the weapon and the hat give, to discard size modifier cards on your weapon (WK/CW) and go for something such as critical damage or ATK.

 Patent Oriental Sword [2] Ancient Hero The patent version of the Oriental Sword shown higher, which provides us with better bonuses overall than its normal counterpart and also brings us 15 critical rate and 15% critical damage ! Its inconsistency with the autocast and the fact that it relies on a ranged skill makes it difficult to build around it, but it still brings a strong autocasted skill to the table; my suggestion with this weapon is to just build as usual on your RK and not bother with ranged bonuses except if you can freely add some in your build (aka it doesn't prevent you from taking other important mods).
 Claw Sword [2] Einbech Mine 3 The new contender that surpasses Lindy, ladies and gentlemen, here is the ultra expensive Claw Sword ! Comes with +15% ATK and +5 crit by default, has a beautiful 300 weapon ATK (40 lower than Lindy Hop but who cares) and gets huge damage increase on refine stages ! Including an non-exhaustive list of : +25% critical dmg, chance to proc +20% DMG to all sizes for a duration, and +7 crit ! You can also enchant it and go for ATK% or crit dmg% or physical damage against a specific type of monster, or even DEF ignore% !
 Oriental Sword-LT [2] Item Reform The new upgrade after the Patent now available, the LT has become more refined and far less of a meme because of its new spec: the weapon now offers some nice POW, P.ATK and ATK% by default, it's indestructible which will allow us to Crush Strike day and night with it, and the SW% mod per refine has been replaced by critical damage per refine, giving us a more uniform boost on our damage since it'll also boost our basic attacks, Storm Blast (and IB if you got something to autocast it). The SW% mod boost can still be found on several refine stages with a good quantity, and also accompanied by Storm Blast% mods. Refine-wise the bonuses end with a stronger crit rate amount compared to previously (10 more), and the old critical damage bonus has been replaced with Melee & Ranged % mods. As this weapon is level 5, we get access to some very cool bonuses as well on grade C and B : more Melee&Ranged% mods and some nice P.ATK and POW.
 Thanos Greatsword-AD [2] Airship Crash New versions of the Thanatos weapons appeared with the Thanos-AD series, and this weapon is the one for RK. It is a very weird combination of WC and AA, more about that in a bit: It gives a good amount of WC% skill mods and ATK per refine, as well as Melee, Size and more WC mods at specific refine stages. The weapon also weirdly has some Wind Cutter autocast feature when doing AAs. The HP/SP leech effect has sadly disappeared (Gravity probably considered it too powerful on endgame because it'd literally heal you full even with a small % amount) and has been replaced with some flat HP/SP regeneration. The grading on this weapon funnily enough is made for us AA users as it boosts Servant Weapon, thus boosting further our damage. It kinda is a janky fun weapon with its own potential; it helps the AoE clearing capacity of the build that would otherwise rely entirely on Storm Blast, and will also fully pierce DEF proving itself pretty neat if you don't have good DEF pierce for the enemies you're fighting and they have very high DEF.
 Abysmal Knight Card Abysmal Knight A very cheap weapon card choice for MvP hunting, that does not lose to the other cards thanks to its powerful 25% modifier against boss protocol monsters.
 The Paper Card The Paper It does the same effect as Aunoe Card but it drains 1 SP whenever you do normal attacks. This doesn't really change much if you plan on Berserking 100% of the time since we have no need for SP once we're buffed, so it might be a good budget alternative to Aunoe.
 Aunoe Card Aunoe You might want to use this one if you can find it cheaper than WK card. It's not as good but it's made for critical attacks.
 Warrior Lola Card Warrior Lola If you find yourself lacking crits and you don't mind losing a %damage card, you could switch one for a Warrior Lola to get solid crits. Beware though, it only works for maces and it's better the more you refine your weapon (usually goes well with a Crimson Mace).
 Ominous Assaulter Card Ominous Assaulter This is a new option that opened up with Illusion of Abyss, but only for a two-handed sword build. It increases a bit your critical rate, and a lot your critical damage and your ATK depending on your weapon's refine. It comboes with Ominous Heater for even more critical (both chance and damage). It's pretty good if you lack critical damage somehow (if you use Brown Rat instead of Petal Card for example).
 Immortal Cursed Knight Card Sky Fortress An old card previously very rare and now very common thanks to MCA getting more mini-bosses in its list, this card gives an alright 10% ATK bonus and will give you a small 2% chance of autocasting IB. This is a very nice jank meme card, sadly it occupies the gear slot where the main sources of size modifier can be found. Nonetheless it has its strengths and you may combine 2 of them with the Ignition Shadow Set and an Old Rune Circlet for more chances to proc Ignition Break and a ton of mods for this skill.
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is one of the most interesting cards for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies (most of the monsters from the game). If you play mace+shield, you'll want to get at least one WK card to combo with the KK card as it transforms your WK increase from 20% to 35%.
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer This is a better version of the WK card, that came out with the Abyss Glast Heim dungeon. It gives 30% against Medium & Large by itself, so it's better when using a two-handed sword since we can't equip KK cards.
 Greater Special Alnoldi Card Garden Watcher One of the two cards that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, this card blesses us with the mighty Melee modifier, and gives us the indestructible property to our weapon. Considering we now got a very strong melee boost with the new Thanatos Tower cards, I wouldn't recommend it alongside the thanatos combo, except if you do Crush Strikes in which case your weapon could break and this card would prevent it.
 Greater Ruba Papilla Card Greater Ruba Papilla The other card that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, it boosts heavily critical damage based on the refine of the weapon. Due to the large quantity of critical damage everywhere else on the slots and the other better options available (size, melee), it is highly recommended to forget this card and go for the other choices listed before (it is still listed as a possibility per nature of my guide, built to show the many paths available to you as the reader).
 Rekenber Guard Card Rekenber Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; this card is a stronger version of the Greater Special Alnoldi, and it works on a bigger variety of weapons (all swords and daggers). The only weakness within this card that I can see is the lack of the indestructible property that the GSA gives; this is an issue if you plan on using Crush Strike and your weapon isn't indestructible.
 Gan Ceann Card Gan Ceann This very specific card is an optional choice you may opt for since this is a kinda MvP hunting oriented build, the majority of the MvPs you'll kill are going to be Large monsters and this card excels at boosting damage against such size. To make it work to its fullest, you'll want to do the weapon card combo it offers.
 Brutal Murderer Card Brutal Murderer Same as above except this time for Medium enemies.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades. You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK). This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players because of it's 10% DEF pierce bonus. That bonus doesn't work on bosses !
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here.
 Royal Guard Shield [1] Banquet for Heroes This shield is quite rare because nobody bothers trying to get one. It gives you the ability to use Shield Spell Lv 1, which can be used to increase your ATK based on the shield base defense. With this shield it's not extremely good, but why would you refuse a possibly free ATK bonus ? You can always switch after using the ATK buff for another shield (but don't bother with this shield if you aren't looking for any kind of min-maxing, the ATK bonus is not really incredible).
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Alice Card Alice The reason this card is here again, is because as a Critical Rune Knight, you'll probably do a lot of MvPs, and this card will be great for your survival. It's especially good against MvPs with weak monsters or no monsters at all, like in Monster Hunter.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). You'll want to get GSS with full STR enchants; if combined with a Poison Breath hat for the combo and you already have too much critical damage, this set could potentially be better than going for the usual critical garments like a FAW.
 Heroic Backpack [1] Monster Hunter This garment is the most used one, tied with the Giant Snake Skin. It used to be the best one for DPS characters as it gives a nice increase in damage on the offensive stats (STR, DEX, LUK) as long as you have 90 in the stat associated with the bonus you want, and as long as the bag is refined to +7 or +9.
 Illusion Engine Wing A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice and you'll want to get 2 Critical modules as well as one Fast module. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. It can be as good as a +9 FAW with 3 Fatal3 enchants, but only if you equip a pair of Illusion Leg A to get the +10% Critical damage bonus from the combo, which allows it to reach the same critical damage potential as the FAW. In that case, you'll have a better ASPD as well as a better critical rate than with the Fallen Angel Wings.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This is a good mid-game garment, a bit similar to HBP as it gives you a bonus different for each stat you've increased, every 20 base points. The reason why it surpasses HBP, is because you can enchant it 3 times (as long as you got it refine to +9, otherwise it's 2 times at +7 and only once under) with strong enchants like Fatal, and it can go up to Fatal 4 on one enchant. The only problem it has, is that we lose a flat ASPD point and a few %ASPD points too.
 Fallen Warrior Manteau [1] Tomb of the Fallen A very good garment that surpasses the previous choices only when refined past +10 and comboed with a Vicious Mind Aura. Its effects are also similar to the others, it gives us ATK, ASPD%, Crit damage% and some other bonuses. It's an extremely versatile combo !
 Automatic Engine Wing A-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. We still have access to interesting modules like  Automatic Module (Critical) but the new addition that may make you think twice about getting this garment or another is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very welcome Melee% boost.
 Temporal Str Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim Part of one of our recent updates alongside its other stat brothers, the STR manteau is currently BiS for all non-crit physical builds. That garment bombs you with raw ATK, refined ATK% and spicy %size modifiers ! The reason why we got it here on a crit build, is in case you have plans to use that manteau on several characters at the same time as your RK. The difference in damage with a Temporal Agi Manteau is not that big so you may want to go for that one if you play multiple classes. If you plan on just going for a cheaper investment, you will want critical damage% as enchant on the temporal manteau (they usually are cheaper than AGI ones).
 Temporal Agi Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim Here comes our strongest contender of the current times, the Temporal Agi Manteau ! Similar to its brother Str Manteau, it gives critical damage instead of the ATK%, alongside the ATK and the %size. You will want to enchant it with critical damage or ATK% for MOAR POWAH BABE !
 Gray Wolf Manteau [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This manteau is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing A-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a +50 ATK bonus. While it may not surpass the Agi Manteau in damage, it wins in utility. The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be an important source of damage with the Melee% it brings. The second slot we will want the Wolf Orb (Critical) which can provide up to +15 Critical rate and +24% Critical damage. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Str) on this one.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat If you already have a LOT of Critical Damage bonuses, you could theorically go for more ATK as it's better to keep a balance between Critical Damage and ATK, it will also help a lot for ASPD.
 Petal Card Petal It's one of the great stat cards; you will get a 24% critical damage bonus since you have 120 LUK and it gives 2% per 10 base LUK. Definitely a great and cheap asset.
 Happiness Giver Card Happiness Giver Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is sickeningly powerful as it gives at 120 STR a whooping 55% Melee damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Mistress of Shelter card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
 Galensis Card Galensis A complete replacement for Petal Card, this one gives more damage (30% critical) and at the same time provides you with a big source of critical rate, because you get 2 every 10 base LUK points. The only bad side of this card is that you need to reach 125 base LUK for the damage part.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Temporal Boots of Luck [1] Old Glast Heim This used to be, and still is a very good pair of boots for critical builds as it gives a whooping 30% critical damage bonus. The enchants are going to define the price of your boots (if you want to buy them instead of crafting them); what you want at least is to get ASPD4 to have an easier time catching the 193 cap. After that, pretty much any special enchant works for a RK (except Muscular Endurance and Speed of Light).
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit.
  • Lucky Day is easier to proc and doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, MATK, P.Dodge.
  • Speed of Light is an exotic but interesting choice since the arrival of MH2, and even more since we got the new Fall of Glast Heim instance with the insignia enchants. SoL allows you to dodge half the hits thanks to the P.Dodge proc (Perfect Dodge is halved in MH2), giving you an easier time tanking there, as well as lowering a bit the stress and burden on your healer.
  • Hawkeye can be quite useful if you're looking for another way to get max ASPD as it gives you +200 DEX so you'll get quite a few ASPD points and a bit of damage. It doesn't have the downside of draining your HPs like Speed of Light.
  • Runaway Magic gives you +200 INT so you're gonna have a lot of MATK, it will work with Enchant Blade. Don't forget that the bonus ATK from Enchant Blade changes dynamically so you can't cheese the enchant and then switch your boots to something else. To proc Runaway Magic you'll need to cast spells, the most common way to do it is with auto-spells stuffs like CD in Mouth.
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type, and when paired with the Illusion Engine Wing A-type you'll get +10% critical damage. The item by itself doesn't have any %critical damage bonus, but it's not a big loss since we already have a ton of that, and it brings an especially strong enchant that you can slot on it, named Overpower. It gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK swords) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds. Once you proc it and as long as you keep attacking, you can be sure it'll never run out as it procs very often.
 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a stronger combo with the Engine Wing, as well as a big increase on the  Automatic Module (Overpower) module, which got on its 17.2 version a +10% Melee modifier when Overpower procs.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong. If you are overflowing with critical damage and running Temporal Boots of Luck, you might consider switching to these.
 Unknown STR Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of stat boots that was added with Airship Crash, these give a bit of ATK, HP and SP based on the refine of the boots which ain't crazy for lvl 5 boots. The main attraction comes from the potential proc when dealing damage which will grant a whooping +175 STR for 10 seconds, basically permanent when continuously hitting enemies (kinda like the Illusion & Automatic procs). The STR boost can be increased through grading. While this gives no interesting modifier like the other previous boots, the STR boost might come in clutch because of how Storm Blast scales on STR, and also simply because of our usual high STR scaling through Weapon ATK with our big swords.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Overpower) to get some sweet STR for boosting the Storm Blast autocast and the nice Melee% mod as well. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
Matyr Card Matyr A cheap choice that combines survivability (+10% HP) and a tiny +1 AGI bonus, better than nothing.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie This is one of the few offensive cards on the boots card slot, it's only worth it if you refine your boots a lot (something like +9 up to +12).
 Rigid Nightmare Terror Card Rigid Nightmare Terror A pretty good budget card, you can combine it with the Nightmare Terror Card that goes into the Armor slot for a sweet 10% ATK.
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ASPD+5% and ATK+3%; if you already got a lot of critical damage increase equipments, you can get this one instead to increase your ATK (remember, you gotta keep the equilibrium between critical damage and ATK, it works kind of the same as the weapon % cards).
 Geffen Bully Card Geffen Bully This used to be a very good min-maxing card if you want to increase your critical damage; it gives 5% Critical damage and 3% ASPD.
 Geffen Gangster Card Geffen Gangster Similar to Geffen Bully but the numbers are reversed.
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman That card gives us flat ATK based on STR, and it's the new BiS card for the critical build thanks to its amazing combo with the Deep Sea King Dramoh Card that gives you +15% critical damage.
 Arena Bully Card Geffen Night Arena The revised version of the Geffen Bully card, this one will provide us with +10% Critical damage.
 Arena Arhi Card Geffen Night Arena A nice new addition from the revisited Geffen Tournament instance, this card provides us with +5% damage to all sizes, which can be pretty useful if you're low on size modifiers.
 Arena Ifodes Card Geffen Night Arena The other most interesting card from that content is the Arena version of Ifodes Card, bringing us a neat +7% Melee boost.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Luk Glove [1] Eclage You will have to take either one or two of these if you're trying to get more than 90 critical chances and you don't have enough money for expensive items. Since you're going to keep 120 LUK for the boots, this accessory will give you +12 Critical; combine it with an Essence of Evil Luk 3, and you'll get at least +16 Critical (1 more point if you get past a Crit cap on your LUK stat) per glove.
 Pendant of Maelstrom [1] Nightmarish Jitterbug This used to be one of the most offensive-oriented accessories you could get. We're one of the few classes that will benefit from both the effects of the accessory (even though the MATK bonus won't be really noticeable on your damage). Get this one if you're playing on a budget build (the price decreased since the GMT update) and you have a lot of ATK already as the bonus will only get better.
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Since the ASPD update it has become much more interesting; even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus (1% more than PoM) and a big 10% ASPD bonus (this is the most interesting part as %ASPD got much better since the update).
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament Used to be one of the strongest accessories you could get, depending on the 2 enchants you have on it. Could go from 40M with bad enchants, to... 1B with godly enchants (2x 8% critical damage enchants). It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it, making it a better choice than Pendant of Maelstrom.
 Illusion Booster L [1]

 Illusion Booster R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for us Crit RKs, are the Attack Speed and the Fatal modules. It is possible to enchant up to 3 times each accessory, so you can put one ASPD and one Fatal enchant on each of them, providing you a lot of ASPD and critical rate (very useful if you play for example the Royal Knight's Broadsword). The third slot is not as important, you may choose what you want to put on it, it's up to your preferences; I personally like using the drain modules which give you HP & SP leech.
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK (this is pretty huge by itself, compared to that the critical insignia is crap with its small 7% critical damage) and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantments for Crit RK are Strong and Flash:
  • Strong : When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%. This is by far the strongest one for us as it increases the size modifier.
  • Flash : When equipped with Speed of Light, increases critical damage by 30%. While not as good as the Strong one (because size modifier is super interesting and critical damage is something we already have a plethora of), it is a great budget choice and Speed of Light boots work very well for tanking contents such as MH2.
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Fatal) gives us now a nice +10 critical rate instead of the old +4, pretty useful to beat the high critical shield of some enemies; the  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) adds 20 ATK now, and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Brilliant Light Ruby Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one that interests us most is Fatal of course. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to +15 Critical rate and +12% Critical damage per enchant. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR if possible.
 Gold Scaraba Card Antler Scaraba and his other golden friends A card that used to be kinda expensive years ago, it is now a budget choice to fill your accessory slots with a cool 20 ATK.
Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit These cards are here again because when you get to an endgame level, you'll have found other ways to get critical hits besides using EoE Luk 3 on your accessories, so you can get these to finish your possible lack of ASPD and increase further your ATK.
Owl Baron Card Owl Baron Nice for hard-hitting builds like Critical RK, depending on RNGod you might get a good increase in DPS but you might as well feel like it doesn't proc enough.
Ominous Heater Card Ominous Heater A very interesting choice if you choose to skip the Old Rune Circlet and its Acute enchant, it will help a lot for your critical rate. Please note that the set with Ominous Assaulter doesn't work twice, even with 2x the cards.
Chaotic Killer Mantis Card Chaotic Killer Mantis A cheap critical damage thanks to its combo with Angra Mantis, It gives a nice amount of critical damage, but beware you get no critical chance bonus on this one !
 Gigantes Card Gigantes A big flat 40 ATK that is only available on left slot, another way of boosting your damage if you have too much %critical damage mod.
 Void Mimic Card Void Mimic A huge critical damage card giving far more than all its peers with a big 15%. The combo would be nice but it means giving up one of the strong garment cards, not recommended.
 Grey Wolf Card Grey Wolf This card locked to the left slot, arrived with Episode 18 and finally brings us (alongside the card it comboes with) Melee% bonuses on the accessory card slots. The Grey Wolf Card will give you 6% Melee, and an additional 8% Melee if equipped with the Phantom Wolf Card, for a total of 20% Melee on accessory slots.
 Phantom Wolf Card Phantom Wolf The other part of the combo with the Grey Wolf Card, this one does basically the same thing (6% Melee) but is locked on the right slot instead.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can put in one of these essences. Usually you'll end up putting EoE LUK 3 because you need a high critical rate.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 Pretty good if your critical rate is high (around 100-110 is enough to hit most of the time), it's sometimes better or cheaper than some other options (like Gold Scaraba).
 Essence of Evil LUK 3 LUK+4, Critical+4, DEX-4 You'll need this if you're aiming for 100% critical chance (without considering the critical defense of the enemies of course). If you're pretty close to 100 in Critical, you can forget about putting points in DEX as you'll be most of the time doing critical hits, which have perfect hit and aren't affected by your HIT rate (and this also means that the decrease in DEX of the EoE does nothing to you, so it's basically a win-win situation for you).
Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get in shape as it doesn't require any refinement; it provides 4 very interesting bonuses for us which are:
  • ASPD% and flat ASPD temporary buff when casting Enchant Blade based on Shadow Shield refine
  • Small chance to autocast Ignition Break while attacking
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness, and most importantly a lot of stat reduction for our VCT !
  • +50% DEF Pierce on Normal Monsters : When you get closer to endgame and start entering areas such as Einbech Mine 3, you'll have quite the hard time trying to one shot these monsters, the reason being they have high DEF. 50% pierce is not perfect but it helps a lot !

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears. Also, this DEF pierce does not work on boss protocol monsters so beware !

 Force Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears Part of the early batch we got with MH2, this set will fill the remaining slots when using an armor/shield/shoes set. It'll provide us with a bunch of extra ATK and ATK%, so this is a nice addition considering we don't need DEF pierce.
 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
 Mammoth Shadow Plate Sub Stat Shadow Gears A very basic but helpful shadow armor, this plate gives +10 Critical rate by default and you'll get up to 5 more upon refining it to the max. This will help you solve some build planning issues with newer gears that do not provide as much crit rate as before, or because of custom content with very high critical shield.
 Blitz Shadow Buckler Sub Stat Shadow Gears Same as above except you get only +5 by default.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, which will help cover the weaknesses some weapon types have, helping us catch up to spear users with Dragon Training. For the most common weapon being 2HS, it'll raise back up the size penalty on Small and Medium monsters.
 Ignition Shadow Set 3-1 Class Sets This IB oriented set is actually very interesting for us as it includes IB autocasting in it, as well as some general DEF pierce thanks to its all races pierce that can go up to 60% with the combo with the Rune Knight Shield. It fits very well on a build that runs the Old Rune Circlet since it boosts IB as well.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Melee Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Broken Warehouse Manager
  • Middle: Angelgolt (Pink)
  • Lower: Sharp Magic
 This set of stone will boost up your Melee % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot. Feel free to go for it if you are already well stocked on Critical damage.
 Critical Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Contaminated Raydric
  • Middle: Rigid Kaho
  • Lower: Ancient Robot
 This set of stone will boost up your Critical damage modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot although you might want to fill it with the Critical Onyx like explained below. Feel free to go for it if you are already well stocked on Melee damage or need the critical rate.
 Double Attack Onyx [G] Onyx Shop A seemingly basic stone that actually promotes our damage a lot, this stone gives us Double Attack at level 3, which is a 21% chance of doubling our basic attack damage. If you are not running anything that gives Double Attack (like PFS or Racing Cap), then I highly recommend to go for this stone.
 Critical Onyx [G] Onyx Shop The Critical Onyx is a pretty strong stone by itself already with its 20% Critical damage bonus, but it also brings up a combo with the Critical Amber Set, offering a +10 Critical rate bonus; this is especially useful when you already have your build set up to have enough critical rate but want to discard some gear pieces that were giving a lot of it for example to swap accessories to the Sinful/Brilliant Light ones, since they do not offer any crit rate.
 Guillotine Cross Onyx II [G] Onyx Shop An unusual choice that is available to us is to go for other classes' stones. The most interesting one so far is the second set of Guillotine Cross which offers 15% Critical damage, which doesn't seem all that interesting at first compared to the Critical Onyx; but you can combo it with the Assassin Cross Onyx II [U] for an additional 5% ATK and 15% Critical damage (thus reaching a total of 30% Critical damage with just 2 stones).

Wind Cutter

WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH WOOSH

If you're starting out as an RK, this is most likely the build you've been suggested. I recommend seeking out the Peuz's set as soon as you're 3rd class and can use the Wind Cutter skill, as the armor set is extremely powerful once you assemble it.

Stats

Here are the stats I use for my WC RK:

  • STR 120
  • AGI 90+
  • VIT 120
  • INT 50+
  • DEX 90+
  • LUK 1+

When leveling, you should quickly aim to have 90 STR, AGI and DEX: 90 STR is easy to get and will allow you to dish enough damage for a while. 90 AGI will allow you to reach quickly the ASPD cap, especially if your ACD reduction is low (which means the ASPD cap is low too). 90 DEX is a must to be able to hit your enemies, because of their FLEE. LUK is not a priority because WIND CUTTER DOES NOT CRIT GUYS !


Strategy

Smash that Wind Cutter button and watch your allies cry in despair over your strong DPS, that's all you gotta do to win ! Since the new 2021 job improvement rework, if you want your spin to win to work properly, you need 185 ASPD and 40% ACD to spam like the wind !

Don't forget that Wind Cutter is a swiss army knife, it changes depending on the weapon you are using, it can have 3 different ways of working :

  • With a two-handed sword : 2 hits instead of 1 hit, at a 1250% per hit skill modifier, and the skill will pierce DEF
  • With a spear weapon : the damage is considered ranged instead of melee, with a 2000% skill modifier
  • With other weapons : nothing specific, with a 1500% skill modifier

Swapping to a spear can prove to be really helpful in situations where you go into an area with lots of monsters with the ability to reflect; this will allow you to bypass it entirely, at the cost of a weaker WC (because you lose the DEF pierce a 2HS provides with the skill). You will be able to escape a lot of deaths, and avoid spending money in Golden X to bypass the reflect.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the Wind Cutter build. Don't forget that you can always take a look again at the General Equipment list, if some items here do not suit you or they are too expensive for you. I've also dropped some interesting cards for MH2 since I know a lot of you are reading this guide for its strong capabilities on that content.

Sets
Set Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Peuz's set
  • Armor dropped by Raydric
  • Accessory dropped by Skogul and Frus
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 So this set which was pretty underwhelming at first, it ended up being extremely good with the new Wind Cutter rework because of its +100% bonus on the skill. You get an absurd increase in damage with it, and it's super cheap, making the build very cost effective for beginners. You'll lack ACD in the beginning though so the spam will be a bit slow, but it'll quickly get better. You can keep using this set while you improve the remaining gear slots, which will allow you to fill other damage modifiers and also take care of the ACD reduction.
 Illusion Sprint set Illusion of Twins The Illusion Sprint combo between the Mail and the 2 accessories (Ring and Glove) is actually a very interesting underdog option. The armor by itself offers 12% ACD and a few VIT points as well as 2 Nive slots on which you can put Powerful Nives for up to +14% damage to all races, and can be comboed with the 2 accessories for a whooping +15% max HP/SP ! The Illusion Sprint Ring comboes with the Mail for 10% more ACD reduction, and comboes with the Illusion Sprint Glove for 5% more ACDr (the Glove itself giving 3% ACDr). The accessories cannot have Nives but they can be enchanted with some stats; this cheap 3-pieces set will bring you a total of 30% ACD which will help you reaching high amounts of ACDr early on. You can then combo these pieces with the Shoes as well, which will bring a lot to the table as well: +10% ATK, +70 ATK, +25% damage against bosses when comboing the Mail and the Shoes, then with the Shoes and the accessories you will get some on-hit chances to gain the gigantic +150 STR and +150 AGI buffs ! Beweare though, the combo of the shoes with the accessories will continuously drain your HP and SP, so you might want to have some swap equipment to avoid losing HP&SP when not fighting, and bring some leech effects if you plan on using this combo so you can regenerate in the middle of the fight.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
Beginner top hats
 Rideword Hat [1] Upper Custom Headgear Quests The basic farming hat, if you feel like you die too quickly against monsters and an Incubus/Succubus is not enough for regeneration, feel free to take out your dusty Rideword Hat and grind hard !
 Heart Wing Headband [1] Upper Master of Coin This hat gives a lot of ACD% reduction and SP cost reduction, which makes it a very good alternative to Rideword Hat, especially if you play with the Peuz set and you lack a lot of ACD reduction.
Mid-endgame top hats
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat. It can be interesting if you already have it on hand or got too much of skill modifiers.
 Black Ribbon [1] Top Master of Coin A very strong hat made for Wind Cutter, it increases the skill's damage by 50% and gives bonus ATK based on your AGI. If you don't need regen anymore (like for example in MH2), you should totally go for this hat, a +7 will do as we have no need for the +9 effect on this build. Beware, in MH2 this hat only gives +15% Wind Cutter damage !
 Clark Sidecap [1] Top Master of Coin From a recent hat update bringing lots of combos regarding the OS weapons from episode 17.1, this hat is pretty interesting even for Wind Cutter because of what it brings : it gives 20 ATK every 2 refines, and 2 great boosts at refines +9 and +11: at +9 we get the extremely rare melee modifier with a whooping +15% (Melee modifier works the same as ranged%, it acts as a final modifier so it's very interesting to have) and at +11 we get a +15% size modifier to Small and Medium.
 Illusion Goibne Helm [1] Top Illusion of Luanda Similar to its other Illusion counterparts, this hat can be enchanted and you'll want to go for STR runes like explained above. The reason why you would go for this hat, outside of any reason concerning a specific kind of content like MH2, is that you lack ACD. This top hat is a huge source of ACD, as it can provide +12% ACD reduction when refined to +9. Combined with the all races bonus thanks to the runes of strength, it is a very powerful contender BUT it will get beaten by a Black Ribbon in terms of raw damage. Now we only require 40% ACD, so it's not recommended.
 Illusion Hot-blooded Headband [1] Top Illusion of Teddy Bear The answer of the community to counter the MH2 nerf of Black Ribbon, this hat provides a ton of bonuses based on the refine of the hat : +10% damage against against wind, water, earth and neutral monsters at +7, +15% damage against small and large monsters at +9. It can also be enchanted, the most recommended enchant for us is the Powerful Nive which, depending on its level, gives a bonus of STR at a specific refine and an all races% bonus at a higher refine.
 Tiger King Doll Hat-LT [1] Top Master of Coin An improved version of the White Drooping Eddga, this one provides a lot of bonuses even outside of the transformation: +2 STR,DEX,POW,CON and 10% ASPD and damage against Brute monsters by default, up to +25% Melee mods and +10% ATK through refines, as well as up to 5% ATK, +3 POW and +9 P.ATK through grading. For the transformation part, we get gifted with amazing boosts: +35 ATK per refine and +20 P.ATK if the hat is refined at least to +10 !
Beginner middle hats
 Monocle [1] Middle Owl Marquis & Owl Viscount The cheapest slotted middle hat, that is the hat you wanna go for in case you really want to use a card in hat slot and you can't use the top slot.
Midgame middle hats
 New Wave Sunglasses Middle New Wave Sunglasses One of your main sources of ACDr, it is the BiS equipment as it contributes a whooping 10% ACD reduction. You definitely need it if you play with the Peuz set since none of the pieces of the set contribute to that stat. You might want to slot it if you have a headgear card which gives you an edge and you don't need as much ACD (you'll lose 5% off the unslotted version though !).
Endgame middle hats
 Magical Booster [1] Middle Magical Booster An alternative to the NWS, this one can either provide as much ACD as the slotted NWS or get other offensive enchants.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD% and we can get further more ACD% reduction through enchants.
Beginner lower hats
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good budget option as it directly increases your physical damage by 1%.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin. If you have enough ACD %reduction for some reason (like for example you're in MH2), going for that hat as well as a GSS full of STR will give you a good increase in damage, resilience and attack speed.
Midgame lower hats
 Blood Sucker Lower Nova Shop One very interesting midgame hat you might want to keep using even in endgame, this hat provides you with some small HP leech % chance based on your damage, at the cost of losing your natural HP&SP recovery (This isn't actually disabling your recoveries but giving you -100%, you can get some regen back if you have just a tiny bit of HP/SP % recovery; this isn't really necessary though if you plan on using leech).
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary in Mouth quest This is pretty interesting as a lower hat for its all stats and ATK bonuses.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary in Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, one could argue the +2 all stats is better than the +1 version with 5 ATK; as it directly depends on the rest of your gears and the difference is really small, it's something you have to test by yourself.
Endgame lower hats
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory A rare lower hat which works only when in combo with the Fallen Warrior Manteau: the main reason behind it, is the great amount of ACD reduction it gives based on your VIT. You get 4% every 30 VIT base points.
 Silver Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Melee damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Golden Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory Same as the previous one, this is only useful if you plan on optimizing a ranged WC build with a spear, as it gives Ranged% damage.
Midgame cards
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This new card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you should go for an EoE STR 3.
Endgame cards
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A pretty strong hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus. Despite that, considering we don't really care about HP with our sky high HP pool, you shouldn't bother and should just put an offensive card on the shoes.
 Engkanto Card Card Engkanto This card increases the damage dealt to Poison property monsters, it should be your go-to card in case you want to farm Garanth/Garronath on MH2. Beware though, its effect is halved in there, which means it only increases your damage by 15% (and not 30% like usually).
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Excellion Suit Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from the instances Charleston Crisis and King's Heels This armor can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki. It also provides you with a nice amount of ACD reduction (20%) when combined with the Excellion Wing, so it's a good budget alternative if you are on a tight budget.
Midgame gears
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the LLSuit and the YSF01 Plate thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants and you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction, that's a really good contender to max out our ACD% reduction cap. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it good for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races. Be careful as this armor doesn't provide ACD reduction, so you need to find how to fill the gap on other slots if you go for this armor.
 Peuz's set
  • Armor dropped by Raydric
  • Accessory dropped by Skogul and Frus
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 I took the liberty of putting again the Peuz's set here as a quick reminder of its potency; its main drawback was the lack of ACD with the set, and with the job improvement rework that lowered the ACD required to 40%, it becomes pretty easy to reach that cap even with a Peuz's set, as a result its early steroid buff for Wind Cutter shouldn't be underestimated. (The only place where it will not be performing good though is MH2 where its combo effect is halved).
Endgame gears
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new contender from 17.2 ! This armor can be enchanted with a variety of different enchants, the interesting ones for us are  Automatic Module (Attacker Force) for the rare melee modifier it provides and  Automatic Module (Delay After Skill) for the ACD it provides just like its Illusion counterpart. You may go for  Automatic Module (Power) if you are looking for a cheaper option instead of the Attacker Force module.
 Illusion Sprint Mail [1] Illusion of Twins Alongside the Sprint Shoes you'll see later in the Shoes section, this armor was released to combo with all the Illusion Sprint parts. In our case it'll be interesting to use if we go for the shoes as you get through the combo everything you would normally find on an Illusion/Automatic armor : ATK, ATK%, Melee/Ranged% and ACD% reduction. On top of that you even get damage against bosses, isn't that neat ?
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. Also we now get access to other skills through these enchants, including Wind Cutter with the Wolf Orb (Cutter Break) enchant which gives a huge 60% WC boost !. The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the huge amount of ATK, ATK% and Melee% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Beginner gears
 Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, and it's pretty cheap !
Mid-endgame gears
 Hardworking Pitman Card Hardworking Pitman A good ATK% card which will also help you beat on these high FLEE monsters since it gives +5% ATK as well as +10 HIT.
 Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric For me it's clearly the optimal choice for mixing survivability and damage thanks to its combo with the Raydric Card for that amazing total 30% neutral resistance, as well as that neat 10% ATK.
 Mistress of Shelter Card Mistress of Shelter This is a necessary card for the combo with the Thanatos Tower garment card (Happiness Giver).
Weapons

If you're not familiar enough with how the Wind Cutter skill works based on the weapon you choose, I'd recommend that you go back to the skills section and read what I wrote about it there, as it is pretty important to choose what weapon you'll use for the contents you will encounter.

Item Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Death Guidance [2] Amdarais A 200 ATK two-handed sword with some potential for survivability: it gives you +20 Perfect Dodge and the possibility to do an AoE life steal when you physically attack. Watch out for the Hell Power that you can sometimes autocast on yourself, it'll prevent you from being resurrected for several minutes. It can be enchanted.
 Thanatos Great Sword [1] Ghost Palace This two-handed sword is really nice for survival because it gives you a chance to regenerate a small part of the damage you do on a attack, including AoE attacks. If you have a Rideword Hat and a Hunter Fly Card in your weapon you'll regenerate lots of HP quite often with this weapon, making it one of the strongest sustain weapons. Since the new Ghost Palace update, you can also enchant your Thanatos weapon, you can get nice effects like an elemental enchantment (they're similar to Vicious Mind enchantments).
Midgame gears
 Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Great Demon Baphomet in Sealed Shrine This weapon more commonly known as the TGL is the most interesting solo-wise, because you benefit from 20% ACD reduction and 20% SP cost reduction; the fact that it's a two-handed sword makes up for its small lack of damage with a full DEF ignore because of WC's properties with a 2HS equipped. You may also enchant it for bonus ATK (Fighting Spirit).
 Illusion Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Illusion of Labyrinth The illusion version of its counterpart, it's very similar but mostly is about buffing DB builds, the only interesting part for us is that we can get a supplementary 5% ACD reduction on it with the enchants; if you don't need these last 5%, don't bother getting the illusion version and stay on the normal one which gives overall more ATK thanks to its proc effect and the Malangdo enchants.
 Lindy Hop [2] Stefan or Immortal Cursed Knight This weapon is extremely good damage-wise, but it has neither ACD reduction nor leeching ability, so beware. It has the most ATK out of all 2HS, has 2 slots, gives ATK% and ASPD% bonuses based on the refine, is indestructible (goodbye Golem Card), and is enchantable twice (you need to aim for Fighting Spirit enchants for the WC build).
 Claw Sword [2] Einbech Mine 3 The new contender that surpasses Lindy, ladies and gentlemen, here is the ultra expensive Claw Sword ! Comes with +15% ATK by default, has a beautiful 300 weapon ATK (40 lower than Lindy Hop but its bonuses compensate for that) and gets huge damage increase on refine stages ! Including an non-exhaustive list of : chance to proc +20% DMG to all sizes for a duration, 20% ACD reduction ! You can also enchant it and go for ATK% or physical damage against a specific type of monster, or even DEF ignore% !
Endgame gears
 Hypocrisy Edge [2] Broken Warehouse Manager or Greater Aries This weapon may not necessarily look like much but its %Wind Cutter bonuses on several refine levels give it an edge in damage that can surpass the Claw Sword. It can be enchanted and potentially get %Melee damage, which could push its potential even further. The biggest downside to this weapon is the loss of 10% ACD compared to other options like Tae Goo Lyeon or the Claw Sword; ACD reduction stays to this day the biggest factor in the DPS you'll deal.
 Thanos Greatsword-AD [2] Airship Crash New versions of the Thanatos weapons appeared with the Thanos-AD series, and the RK weapon is oriented for WC luckily for us. It gives a good amount of WC% skill mods and ATK per refine, as well as Melee, Size and more WC mods at specific refine stages. The weapon also weirdly has some Wind Cutter autocast feature when doing AAs, this may prove to come in clutch if you ever end up silenced and do not have Nosiege runes nor Green Potions thanks to that autocast (I have no idea about the % chance though). The HP/SP leech effect has sadly disappeared (Gravity probably considered it too powerful on endgame because it'd literally heal you full even with a small % amount) and has been replaced with some flat HP/SP regeneration. The grading on this weapon is clearly not interesting for us at it boosts Servant Weapon, hinting at a use for autoattacking. This weapon will become much stronger later on when we get access to Thanos Warrior Helmet (which will put it above the Vivatus Fides weapon described below).
 Adulter Fides Two-Handed Sword [2] Villa of Deception One of 4 new RK/DK weapons in the Episode 18, this weapon is surprisingly a classic level 4 weapon released post 4th job patch. It boasts a pretty high weapon ATK (300), WC skill mods, Melee%, ACD% and some ATK based on refine rate, and you can enchant it. It's not stronger than the Thanos Greatsword because of its lack of P.ATK per refine, but its big brother (down below) is the more interesting one for us.
 Vivatus Fides Two-Handed Sword [2] Villa of Deception This 2HS is the upgraded version of the Adulter Fides one; it has the same stats and boosts per refine, except it's a level 5 weapon; this means P.ATK per refine (which is huge) and some pretty neat Grading bonuses. It will later on get stronger through the Helm of Faith combo. Like the Adulter version, it's possible to enchant it, and if you want your weapon to be versatile, you may want to aim for ACD% reduction or the Melee% enchants.
Alternative
 Crimson Spear [2] Stem Worm or Naga One of the famous crimson weapons. The base ATK is low but it'll get much stronger thanks to the special ATK bonus that increases each time you refine it, up to +15.
 Hunting Spear [1] Kraken or Leak or Fallen Bishop or Boitata The Hunting Spear, a weapon of choice usually for Spiral Pierce but it's also listed here because it's a strong contender amongst the one-handed spears. It's also pretty good against Brute monsters because it allows you to pierce their DEF, making it pretty similar to the ability of 2HS on Wind Cutter to ignore DEF, but at the same time you get access to long range modifiers.
 Thanatos Spear [1] Ghost Palace A very classic weapon with incorporated leech in it, if you are leveling in an area with lots of Reflect Shield monsters, this weapon will do very good.
 Thanatos Long Spear [1] Ghost Palace Same as the one above except it's a two-handed spear with stronger weapon ATK; if tankiness is none of your concern, then you might want to drop your shield and go for that.
 Vicious Mind Spear [1] Sky Fortress The better version of the Crimson Spear, the specific enchants might make it worthwhile for specific places to grind, where there is a common element or race among the monsters (for example Magma 3 where there's reflect, go for dmg against neutral element).
 Royal Knight's Lance [2] Abyss Glast Heim A two-handed spear which brings a lot of ranged mods per refine as well as a neat 15% all races bonus at +9, if you find one for dirt cheap it can be a very good midgame weapon.
 Illusion Zephyrus [3] Illusion of Underwater Probably one of our current best options for ranged WC, it's one of these very rare 3 slots level 4 weapons, which allows for a great variety of card combinations. It brings a lot of ranged% as well as flat ATK based on refinement, and you get also 20% Spiral damage at +7 and +10% size modifier against medium and large monsters. Keep in mind that this is a lance thus two-handed spear, and you will have to get your DEF pierce through other means (like shadow gears perhaps).
Beginner gears
 Abysmal Knight Card Abysmal Knight A very cheap weapon card choice for MvP hunting, that does not lose to the other cards thanks to its powerful 25% modifier against boss protocol monsters.
 Hunter Fly Card Hunter Fly If you don't care about doing a ton of damage but you want to survive, then this is the way to go. Hunter Fly Card allows you to regenerate health based on the damage you deal, at a low chance. Hitting more monsters means you're repeating the probability several times, and it ramps up the chance of making the card proc; add this card to a Thanatos Weapon and use a Rideword and you'll notice you get full health in no time while killing monsters, basically making you unstoppable machine that does not need a support or potions.
Midgame gears
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is one of the most interesting cards for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies (most of the monsters from the game).
 Brain Sucker Card Brain Sucker From Airship Crash arrived a new card that can replace Hunter Fly thanks to its huge 20% HP leech rate, however it comes with a huge disadvantage: -15% Max HP. I think that if you're looking for survivability it's probably better to just stick to Hunter Fly and avoid that drop in HP.
 Greater Special Alnoldi Card Garden Watcher One of the two cards that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, this card blesses us with the mighty %Melee modifier, and gives us the indestructible property to our weapon. Considering we now got a very strong melee boost with the new Thanatos Tower cards, I wouldn't recommend it alongside the thanatos combo, except if you do Crush Strikes in which case your weapon could break and this card would prevent it.
Endgame gears
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer This is a better version of the WK card, that got out with the Abyss Glast Heim dungeon. It gives 30% against Medium & Large by itself, so it's better for two-handed swords since we can't equip KK cards. If you go with a one-handed weapon like a spear though, get at least one WK card if you plan to use the KK card.
 Rekenber Guard Card Rekenber Guard A card that appeared with the last content update on Bioresearch Laboratory; this card is a stronger version of the Greater Special Alnoldi, and it works on a bigger variety of weapons (all swords and daggers), but without the indestructible effect.
 Gan Ceann Card Gan Ceann This very specific card is an optional choice you may opt for. It only gets to its fullest effect if you do the weapon card combo it offers.
 Brutal Murderer Card Brutal Murderer Same as above except this time for Medium enemies.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
Midgame gears
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades. You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK).
