This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players because of it's 10% DEF pierce bonus. That bonus doesn't work on bosses !
Mid-endgame gears
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here.
Beginner gears
 Hodremlin Card Hodremlin This card gives a 15% reduction against all sizes so it's great if you only want to keep one shield. It's a budget version of the next card.
 Gaster Card Gaster If you're playing an AoE farming build, you'll mostly fight against lots of normal monsters, which makes this card pretty good in this situation because it reduces the damage you receive from all kinds of non-MvP monsters.
Alice Card Alice The reason this card is here again is because as a Rune Knight you'll probably do a lot of MvPs, and this card will be great for your survival.
Endgame gears
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). If you don't have any, you might want to get one of the cheapest for starters. The +10 MDEF is really neat and if you get a pair of Temporal Boots (any of the boots, even the basic ones should work), you'll also get a +15% HP and +5% SP set bonus. Try getting eventually a more expensive GSS with several STR enchants. You can also combo this garment with the Poison Breath hat for lots of neat effects. Beware as you might be lacking ACD reduction with this kind of garment !
 Excellion Wing [1] Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from the instances Charleston Crisis and King's Heels This garment is usually only used in combination with the Excellion Suit you've seen before, for the aforementioned combo of 10% ACD it provides, it's a very budget choice. You can enchant it 3 times like the suit, the enchants which will interest you are a combination in any way you want of those 3 enchants : HP/DEF/ATK (you can put up to 3 of any of these 3 enchants).
Midgame gears
 Illusion Engine Wing B-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice; you'll want to get 2 Fast modules as well as one Above All module. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. The B-type's combo with the Illusion Armor A gives 10% more ACD reduction, which is the reason we go for this one.
Endgame gears
 Fallen Warrior Manteau [1] Tomb of the Fallen A very good garment that surpasses the other choices only when refined past +10 and comboed with a Vicious Mind Aura. It gives us ATK, a lot of ASPD% and ACD% and some other less important bonuses. It's what you should go for once you've obtained everything else, and want more damage and ACD.
 Automatic Engine Wing B-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. The new addition that may make you think twice about choosing another garment is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very attractive %Melee boost.
 Temporal Str Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim The STR manteau, as many originally cash shop items, is a very powerful option for all non-crit physical builds. That garment bombs you with raw ATK, refined ATK% and spicy %size modifiers ! You'll want to put ACD% enchant on the garment, or ATK% if you somehow already got too much ACD% (but that shouldn't happen until the next RK rework).
 Gray Wolf Muffler [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The muffler is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing B-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a 10% ACDr bonus. While it may not surpass the Str Manteau in both ACD% reduction and damage, it wins in utility (and ultimately damage, you will see why). The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be our main enchant source of damage upgrade with the Melee% it brings. The second slot (which is the most interesting one I believe) can be enchanted with Wolf Orb (Guide Attack), which can bring up to 24 Perfect Hit rate ! This is extremely important for us on Wind Cutter as our main counter is very high FLEE which some monsters boast thanks to using the skill Agi Up. Perfect Hit will allow us to hit while ignoring FLEE, much like a Critical hit. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Str) on this one.
Beginner gears
Wakwak Card Wakwak This is one of the first garment stat cards, it will increase your ATK based on your STR. You get +5 ATK every 10 base STR points.
 Raydric Card Raydric Increases your resistance to neutral property attacks by 20%. This one is really good because all monsters hit physically with neutral attacks, so you reduce most of the damage from monsters by 20%. This is really great for grinding solo or doing tough monsters. It also comboes with the Contaminated Raydric to add 10% more neutral resistance as well as 5% more ATK.
Midgame gears
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat This card will help you reach a good amount of ATK and ASPD in case you're lacking in these areas.
 Happiness Giver Card Happiness Giver Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is sickeningly powerful as it gives at 120 STR a whooping 55% Melee damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Mistress of Shelter card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
Midgame gears
 Temporal Boots of Strength [1] Old Glast Heim These boots are amongst the best ones, but they need to combo with an expensive accessory for that, and are generally both expensive. The enchants are going to define the price of your boots (if you want to buy them instead of crafting them); what you want at least is to get ASPD4 to have an easier time catching the ASPD cap we're looking for. Then, you'll have to make your choice between these 2 special enchants :
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit.
  • Speed of Light is an exotic but interesting choice since the arrival of MH2, and even more since we got the new Fall of Glast Heim instance with the insignia enchants. SoL allows you to dodge half the hits thanks to the P.Dodge proc (Perfect Dodge is halved in MH2), giving you an easier time tanking there on the 1-star mode, as well as lowering a bit the stress and burden on your healer.
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type. The item brings an especially strong enchant that you can slot on it, named Overpower. It gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK swords) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds. Once you proc it and as long as you keep attacking, you can be sure it'll never run out as it procs very often.
Endgame gears
 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a big increase on the  Automatic Module (Overpower) module, which got on its 17.2 version a +10% Melee modifier when Overpower procs. You can also add the Firing Shot module for more HIT once the DEX boost triggers.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong.
 Unknown STR Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of stat boots that was added with Airship Crash, these give a bit of ATK, HP and SP based on the refine of the boots which ain't crazy for lvl 5 boots. The main attraction comes from the potential proc when dealing damage which will grant a whooping +175 STR for 10 seconds, basically permanent when continuously hitting groups of enemies (kinda like the Illusion & Automatic procs). The STR boost can be increased through grading. While this gives no interesting modifier like the other previous boots, the STR boost is quite phenomenal; I'd recommend checking with a calculator if this would be stronger for you than Illusion Sprint Shoes as usually multiplcative modifiers tend to do better.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Overpower) to get some STR and the nice Melee% mod as well. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
Beginner gears
 Matyr Card Matyr A cheap choice that combines survivability (+10% HP) and a tiny +1 AGI bonus, better than nothing.
 White Porcellio Card White Porcellio A new budget possibility that gives flat ATK, you can combine it with Porcellio Card for greater effects.
 Rigid Nightmare Terror Card Rigid Nightmare Terror A pretty good budget card, you can combine it with the Nightmare Terror Card that goes into the Armor slot for a sweet 10% ATK.
Midgame gears
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ASPD+5% and ATK+3% from the get-go, usually BiS since it helps us reach an OK ASPD and it helps increasing our damage again.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie This is one of the few offensive cards on the boots card slot, it's only worth it if you refine your boots a lot (something like +9 up to +12).
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman That card gives us flat ATK based on STR, it may or may not better than previous options depending on the quantity of ATK and ATK% you currently have.
 Arena Arhi Card Geffen Night Arena A nice new addition from the revisited Geffen Tournament instance, this card provides us with 5% damage to all sizes, which can be pretty useful if you're low on size modifiers.
 Arena Ifodes Card Geffen Night Arena The other most interesting card from that content is the Arena version of Ifodes Card, bringing us a neat 7% Melee boost.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus and a big 10% ASPD bonus. It's a great cheap accessory choice.
 Pendant of Maelstrom Nightmarish Jitterbug A little bit weaker than the previous option, but it provides you with a card slot. Correct budget option.
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it; you'll want to get ATK% enchants.
Midgame gears
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for us, are the Attack Speed and the Drain modules. It is possible to enchant up to 3 times each accessory, so you can put one ASPD and one Drain enchants on each of them, providing you a lot of ASPD and leech. For the third slot, it's up to you.
 Sarah's Right Earring Sarah and Fenrir This accessory eliminates the need of Fly Wings or a Creamy card, and you can enchant it to get ACD reduction, up to a neat 10% reduction. While the accessory is easy to get (because you only need to complete the instance once), you need Shards of Gigantes to enchant the earring, which you can get from the instance or on the market. You can get more accessories by spending 1 Shard of Gigantes for each accessory, and you can also get a Left Earring if you want to have 2 of them at the same time.
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantment for a Wind Cutter build is Strong: "When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%."
Endgame gears
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Drain Life) gives 1% more leech (better than nothing I guess), the  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) adds 20 ATK now and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus, and you will also get a tiny but sweet ACDr% bonus.
 Brilliant Light Ruby Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus, and you will also get a tiny but sweet ACDr% bonus.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one that interests us most is Fighting Spirit of course. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to 10% Melee damage and 5 Perfect Hit, so pretty much with 2 accessories with 2 perfect enchants each, that means 40% Melee and 20 P.HIT ! This is very helpful in order to solve our troubles trying to hit high FLEE enemies. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR if possible.
Beginner gears
 Gold Scaraba Card Antler Scaraba and his other golden friends A card that used to be kinda expensive years ago, it is now a budget choice to fill your accessory slots with a cool 20 ATK.
 Broken Cleaner Card Beta Cleaner A or Beta Cleaner B If you're looking for a way to boost your HP pool to get tankier, or you plan to do some hybrid WC/DB action, this card is exactly what you need !
Midgame gears
 Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit You can get these to finish your possible lack of ASPD and increase further your ATK, still one of the best choices today.
Endgame gears
 Gigantes Card Gigantes A big flat 40 ATK that is only available on left slot, pretty interesting if your other accessory slot is busy or you're simply missing one (because you're using a sarah earring for example).
 Grey Wolf Card Grey Wolf This card locked to the left slot, arrived with Episode 18 and finally brings us (alongside the card it comboes with) Melee% bonuses on the accessory card slots. The Grey Wolf Card will give you 6% Melee, and an additional 8% Melee if equipped with the Phantom Wolf Card, for a total of 20% Melee on accessory slots.
 Phantom Wolf Card Phantom Wolf The other part of the combo with the Grey Wolf Card, this one does basically the same thing (6% Melee) but is locked on the right slot instead.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can put in this essence.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 It's free real ATK ( ). Joke aside, it's pretty good to replace cards like Gold Scaraba/Gigantes or occupy slots which usually have expensive cards.
Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get, it provides 2 nice bonuses for us which are:
  • ASPD% and flat ASPD temporary buff when casting Enchant Blade based on Shadow Shield refine
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears.

 Reload Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears One of the important stats and not always easy to fetch, is the After Cast Delay reduction. This set allows us to get 15% more reduction of it, without changing any of our gears, which is a big asset because it allows us to focus more on damage in equipments. You will need to refine the whole set to +9 to benefit from the big ACD% bonus. Don't forget to transform the Reload Shadow Armor into its version 2 to get slightly more ACD reduction as well as some VIT.
 Force Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears Part of the early batch we got with MH2, this set will fill the remaining slots when using an armor/shield/shoes set, just like the Reload set. It'll provide us with a bunch of extra ATK and ATK%, so this is a nice addition considering we don't need DEF pierce.
 Ancient Shadow Vest Sub Stat Shadow Gears The shadow armor slot is not very generous with damage boost choices, but there are also utility-oriented gears we can look at. This vest is one of them, bringing us up to +20 HIT, which will help us fight against high FLEE targets.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, which will help cover the weaknesses some weapon types have, helping us catch up to spear users with Dragon Training. For the most common weapon being 2HS, it'll raise back up the size penalty on Small and Medium monsters.
 Auto Spell Shadow Plate Auto Spell Shadow Gears This unexpected shadow gear is actually helpful for us to fight high FLEE targets as it provides +5 Perfect Hit when refined to +9.
For Ranged WC only
 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Melee Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Broken Warehouse Manager
  • Middle: Angelgolt (Pink)
  • Lower: Sharp Magic
 This set of stone will boost up your Melee % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot. Feel free to go for it if you are already well stocked on Critical damage.
 Reload Onyx Set Onyx Shop An alternative to damage if once again you are lacking ACD for maximum spammability, you may go for this option to get the few remaining % you need.
 SP Absorb Onyx [G] Onyx Shop If you need to fill the remaining slot in case you went for the Melee or Reload sets, you may get this utility onyx that will help you triggering some SP leech when necessary.

Ignition Break

Looking for a stomping, popular build that crushes everything ? Want to obliterate everything that moves ? Ignition Break can do that, but be prepared for a huge budget investment to be able to reach the damage of those Rune Knights that impressed you.

Stats

Here are the stats I'd use for an IB build:

  • STR 120
  • AGI 30+
  • VIT 90+
  • INT 30+
  • DEX 120
  • LUK 120

We're of course putting 120 STR in this build because it relies heavily in ATK. Not much AGI needed, since Ignition Break isn't fully spammable. You could get some though if you're planning on getting a high FLEE, but mob trains virtually destroy your FLEE so it's not that worth it. Only start getting some AGI once you get the CD reduction gears for IB. The 90 VIT is there to help build up your natural HP pool, and also proc the effect of the Heroic Backpack. This build is all about skill-spamming, so of course we're going to invest a bit of INT to get enough time for the Rideword to regen your HP and SP. DEX is there at 120 for the cast of Ignition Break; this skill has only variable cast so you can reduce it a lot with stat reduction (Remember, int+dex*2=530 => Instant Cast IB). LUK should be set at 120 for the critical chance, as well as the damage you get from investing into it with crit gears.

Skills

So the skills you'll probably need as an IB RK, are approx the same as the Critical build except you get Ignition Break, the mounting skills from both LK and RK skill trees (speed is important when doing mob trains).

Strategy

If you want to level your char with the IB build and by doing mob trains, there are several things you need to know:

  • Don't face the mobs head on; always keep your distance, use Ignition Break before they get close to you so it hits and staggers them right before they hit you (that's called kiting).
  • You need to ALWAYS keep Concentration up (for the Endure effect). It will decide if you'll be able to get away from the monsters after getting attacked, or if the train stomps on you because you get stun-locked by the many monster hits.).
  • If you feel like you don't regen enough with the HP/SP leech equipments you got, you can try combining a Succubus/Incubus pet with more leech gears to further increase the chances of replenishing your HP/SP.
  • If you die too much with mob trains, try getting a Priest friend or slave to use Kyrie Eleison on you. That way you can survive longer and train your kiting strategy.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the Ignition Break build.

Sets
Set Way to obtain Notes
Beginner gears
 Grace Knight set Eden Academy A fairly new set that is available through a custom beginner content, this practically free set will boost you in many ways: ATK, IB skill mod, critical damage... If you have no gears yet, going for this set will help you get more easily into midgame. My only issue with it if you're starting out is that it provides basically no critical rate, so you'll have to rely on other sources like your base LUK, buffs or manage to set in your stuff some crit rate equipments/cards.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Rideword's Hat [1] Top Custom Headgear Quests This is a really strong hat as it gives you a chance to convert your damage as HP and/or SP. It should proc often with IB against mob trains.
 Ancient Gold Ornament [1] Top Wolfchev's Laboratory A good budget hat since the Bio5 update which boosts your ATK by 8%, you might find it for a cheap price on the market.
 Fox Ear Ribbons [1] Top Nova Shop This hat gives 10% aspd bonus, and when you physically attack, you have a chance of transforming into Moonlight Flower: it gives you a %ranged damage bonus, and +100% critical chance. Since Ignition Break will now crit with the November 7th RK update, I thought why not with this hat ! Considering the fact that you'll do mob trains, the ribbon should proc quite often. A budget option similar to the bio hat but without the big IB damage increase and the critical damage bonus.
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat. It can be interesting if you already have it on hand or got too much of skill modifiers.
 Black Ribbon [1] Top Master of Coin An interesting middle-budget choice, it gives +30% damage on IB at +9 and bonus ATK based on your AGI at +7.
 Old Rune Circlet [1] Top Tomb of the Fallen Currently the strongest hat for its refine bonuses and enchants, but also the hardest to get. Every 2 refines, you have 20% bonus damage on Ignition Break, and 15% on Hundred Spears. On the Ignition Break build, you may use the Mettle enchantment, which gives ATK+3% and HIT+3 every level, or get Acute, for 3 CRIT and 15% critical damage per level.
 Goral Crown [1] Top Goral Crown One of the latest hats pre-4th classes, it offers a pretty good boost at high refine without the need to invest into an annoying RNG enchant system. Its biggest use comes from the combo with the Volar which gives a lot of skill mod per refine of the weapon; beware though, running this hat instead of the ORC will give you some trouble for compensating on critical rate.
 Angel Spirit Middle Nova Shop ATK and MATK+2%, STR+2. Similar to Ancient Gold Ornament, it's great if you want to keep increasing your ATK; but you won't have a slot on this hat.
 Wing of Diablo [1] Middle Evil Wing Ears & Spiritual Auger from Nova Shop If you're looking for a cheap critical option, get these ears alongside an EoE LUK 3. You may also go for the Angel Wing Ears if you prefer.
 Fafnir Skin Middle Weakened Fafnir's quest This hat gives +3% Critical chance and comboes with the Fafnir Mask, they give together a total of +5% Critical chance as well as +5% Critical damage (as a combo). Beware of the -100% HP regeneration debuff this hat gives !
 Magical Booster [1] Middle Magical Booster quest This new hat allows us to get good bonuses such as critical rate, raw ATK and ATK%, while having an available card slot. As an IB RK, you'll want to get critical rate and ATK%.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD%, but what interests us the most is the enchant part since we can get up to 6 critical rate through that, while keeping a card slot.
 Deep Blue Sunglasses [1] Middle Ancient Juperos An alternative to the Victory Wing Ears, this one purely gives VCT% reduction instead. If you wish to reduce IB's cast time completely through percentage, then this is a very powerful option since you can get up to 15% VCTr in total with the enchants added, while keeping a slot available.
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good choice if you have a lot of ATK (usually because you have a two-handed weapon like a Lindy or a crimson weapon). A cheaper choice would be otherwise go for a Bandit Scarf.
 Fafnir Mask Lower Weakened Fafnir's quest It gives +2% Critical chance and combos with the Fafnir Skin shown before. If you're really in need of critical rate, that's a good source you can get.
 Blood Sucker Lower Nova Shop One very interesting midgame hat you might want to keep using even in endgame, this hat provides you with some small HP leech % chance based on your damage, at the cost of losing your natural HP&SP recovery (This isn't actually disabling your recoveries but giving you -100%, you can get some regen back if you have just a tiny bit of HP/SP % recovery; this isn't really necessary though if you plan on using leech).
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, you could use it as it gives a bit of STR and LUK (2 LUK = 0.66 critical rate).
 Silver Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Melee damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Angra Mantis Card Card Angra Mantis It only gives 3% critical damage since we're not a Thief class, but you'll want to put this in case you get the Chaotic Killer Mantis Card for a bonus 5% critical damage.
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This new card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you could go for an EoE STR 3.
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A new hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus but considering our build is not concerned by HP, you shouldn't bother and just put an offensive card on the shoes.
 Deep Sea King Dramoh Card Card Deep Sea King Dramoh This card is able to overcome the Purple Ferus Card thanks to its combo with Deep Sea Merman Card (check out the shoes section to learn more about it). The card by itself though brings just a bit of ATK% based on the refine of your hat, so if you don't plan on using the combo set, it is recommended to stay on the Purple Ferus Card as it's better in that case. Also in case you were worried about your health pool, there's another combo with the normal King Dramoh Card that brings +15% HP, effectively canceling the con of that card and bringing at the same time 10% more HP.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Engraved Armor [1] In the hidden room of Old Glast Heim Engraved Armor is really nice because it'll give you a big +25 MDEF and it has one of the highest DEF rates. It's very useful since the MATK formula update for monsters, to lessen the pain you get from the monsters who use strong magic (Golden Scaraba... oof). Since you'll be mobbing a lot, if they all cast magic at the same time... I don't want to think about it.
 Abusive Robe [1] You can craft it with 600 Honor Tokens, these are obtainable in the Banquet for Heroes quests. This is the most common armor for physical builds against Demi-Humans, Undeads and Demons since you get a %defense bypass on them per refine, as well as the skill Attention Concentrate at level 1. The reason why it's commonly used and refined to +7 is also because of the enchants you can apply on it. Go for the STR enchants (Powerful Nive).
 Excellion Suit Craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis This is a good budget armor you can get for offensive purposes, as you can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK). Going for the Unfrozen blueprint might be nice too to prevent mistakes (monsters who cast Frost Diver for example ?). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki.
 Lava Leather Suit [1] Magma Dungeon F3 A very good choice for pure damage, it is pretty much the physical version of the Flattery Robe once you get it +7, since it gives +150 ATK at this refine (only +100 before +7). Getting the armor +9 is not a bad idea as it gives +10% critical damage, which is useful since Ignition Break now crits.
 Lava Leather Armor [1] Magma Dungeon F3 A more defensive choice compared to the LLSuit shown before, instead of getting +50 ATK at +7, you get a +100 DEF bonus. Stacking DEF is a good choice to mitigate the damage you'll receive from the mob trains if you get hit; a possibility to consider and ponder on since RKs have a naturally low DEF.
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the LLSuit and the YSF01 Plate thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants at least, and if you wanna use that armor on other classes like SS Ranger, you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Luk Soutane [1] Odin's Past The Luk Soutane is an interesting choice for its gigantic amount of critical rate : we get critical rate, damage and LUK per refine. At +12 the armor gives +18 Crit rate, +20 LUK which gives also +6 Crit rate, and 24% Critical damage. The special Luk enchant gives us +10 LUK, +15% Crit damage, +10 Crit rate and +12% DMG against all sizes. So in total you get : +37 Critical rate, 39% Critical damage and +12% against all sizes. The only downside of this armor is the lack of ATK bonuses, so it's really a compromise you need to decide on.
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it pretty strong for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races.
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new armor that I don't even need to name, the one you are seeking with its special enchant if you've been following the IB meta. It has modules like the Illusion equipments in 17.1, except there are Skill modules. Amongst them is the most expensive (as of writing this) module which is the  Automatic Module (Wave Break). This module boosts the damage of both Sonic Wave and Ignition Break like other damage spell modules, but the reason for its huge price is the fact that it reduces IB's cooldown by 0.25s. Considering IB's cooldown has a base of 2 seconds, gets reduced to 1 second with a Volar; it means that putting 2 of these modules reduce your cooldown to 0.5s, effectively halving your cooldown again, and doubling your DPS. You'll want to put on the third slot either a  Automatic Module (Attacker Force) or a  Automatic Module (Critical Force) to further boost your damage. On another note, if you just seek pure damage output per hit on IB, going with  Automatic Module (Attacker Force) and  Automatic Module (Power) modules will provide more than the uber expensive WB modules.
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. The Wolf Orb (Cutter Break) enchant will give us a 60% IB boost, but sadly less cooldown reduction (0.3s) than with the Automatic Module (Wave Break). The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the huge amount of ATK, ATK% and Melee% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Evil Druid Card Evil Druid Evil Druid Card will enchant your armor with the Undead property, you'll get immunity to status effects like Stone Curse and Frozen. But be careful if you play in a party, you cannot be resurrected if you have undead property. This shouldn't be a problem because usually when you farm, you do it alone.
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF. A super cheap choice.
Earth Deleter Card Earth Deleter It disables your SP regeneration, but it allows you to regenerate 10 SP each time you kill a monster with a physical attack, which means you'll be most of the time full on your SP pool since it'll regen much more than the SP cost of IB if you make big mob trains.
Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, and it's pretty cheap ! Might be interesting if you pick a weapon that can be destroyed and you use the Rhydo runestone.
Hardworking Pitman Card Hardworking Pitman A new and much better choice overall for armor than the old usual cards, this one adds 5% ATK, that's 1/3 of an Amdarais Card ! It also gives +10 HIT, it will contribute towards a tailored HIT stuff for high FLEE monster mobbing.
Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric It's the same as the one before but without the HIT part, except it has a combo with the Raydric Card, which will make you much tankier : +10% Neutral Resistance (Raydric already gives +20%) and +5% more ATK. The ATK part of the combo is pretty neat because it compensates for the loss of a damage card on the garment slot like Brown Rat Card or Wakwak Card.
Furious Ninetail Card Angry Nine Tail A new possibility that opened as IB can now crit ! It gives +5% Critical chance, +10% Critical damage and another +10% Critical chance if your armor is +10 or more.
 Mistress of Shelter Card Mistress of Shelter This is a necessary card for the combo with the Thanatos Tower garment card (Happiness Giver).
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Solar Sword Pharaoh This weapon is a bit peculiar and will force you to keep on farming because it consumes 15 SP every 10 seconds. What is neat about it, is that it ALWAYS steals 1% of the damage you do to convert it into HP, which will regen a lot of HP since IB hurts so much; what's more it's naturally Fire enchanted ! Quite the good cheap weapon for farming anything which isn't Shadow/Fire/Water.
 Twin Edge of Naght Seiger [3] Naght Seiger This sword is currently one of the best one-handed choices possible for a skill build with Bio5 cards as it is the level 4 weapon with 3 slots that has the highest weapon ATK in its category, and it can even be Malangdo enchanted.
 Long Horn [1] Cornus and Fallen Bishop This holy spear is one of the greatest budget weapons you can get for early IB farming where you take advantage of the Holy element, like at Geffenia for example. It's indestructible so there's no fear of breaking it. Its ATK is ok for a one-handed weapon, but it's its element which makes it stand out among the others.
 Crimson Spear [2] Stem Worm or Naga Same business as the Crimson Two-handed Sword, but the spear allows you to wield a shield on which you can put a racial/size resistance card; if you plan on mobbing a lot, it's a safe bet. Get a mount to remove size penalty.
 Crimson Lance [2] Owl Duke or Anacondaq or Gryphon Pretty much the same as the other Crimson weapons, but this one is two-handed and has more weight; it's rather more offensive-oriented since you can't use a shield and it has more ATK. If you get a mount with a spear or a lance, you won't have any size penalty problem as you would normally, which makes it the strongest of the Crimson weapons for RK in terms of damage, but you lose the possibility of having Parrying with a two-handed sword or simply a shield with a spear; up to you !
 Vicious Mind Spear [1] Sky Fortress The better version of the Crimson Spear, the specific enchants might make it worthwhile for specific places to grind, where there is a common element or race among the monsters.
 Poison Forged Spear [3] Venomous Chimera As I said before on the Critical build: it's a spear, so you don't have any size penalty on a Peco Peco/Dragon. We recently got Bio Labs 5 content, Seyren Windsor card increases IB damage and the spear is level 4 and has 3 slots; this means +180% damage on Ignition Break if you manage to get a +10 Poison Forged Spear !
 Crimson Two-handed Sword [2] Tamruan or Baroness of Retribution or Abysmal Knight or Egnigem Cenia Crimson weapons are interesting cheap weapons for giving a ton of ATK when overrefined (exactly what we want for IB which is a big steroid ATK skill).
 Death Guidance [2] Amdarais from Old Glast Heim A 200 ATK two-handed sword that give you a lot of survival capacity; it gives you +20% Perfect Dodge and the possibility to do an AoE life steal when you physically attack. Watch out for the Hell Power that you can sometimes cast on yourself, it'll prevent you from being resurrected for several minutes. It's quite useful for beginners on the IB build as it gives you 20 Perfect Dodge: perfect to avoid some attacks of the mob train and prevent getting staggered, which often means your death.
 Krasnaya [3] Drake A 200 ATK two-handed sword with a rare capacity of 3 slots and gives you a small ATK bonus (+20) if you have 96 STR or more. This could prove to be a good alternative to other 2HS because of the versatility of the 3 slots; you could put a Hunter Fly card or more for life stealing and still mix it with ~10-20% damage cards (like Hydra, Skeleton Worker, White Knight).
 Thanatos Great Sword [1] Ghost Palace This two-handed sword is really nice for survival because it gives you a chance to regenerate a small part of the damage you do on a attack, including AoE attacks. If you have a Rideword Hat and a Hunter Fly Card in your weapon you'll regenerate lots of HP quite often and never run out of SP too. Since the new Ghost Palace update, you can also enchant your Thanatos weapon, you can get nice effects like an elemental enchantment (they're a bit similar to Vicious Mind enchantments).
 Royal Knight's Broadsword [2] Abyss Glast Heim monsters This new addition to the two-handed swords roster is a pretty good rival to Lindy Hop, and will surpass Vicious Mind in terms of ATK. Unlike this last one who needs a special enchant in order to be unbreakable by itself, this one just needs to be refined to +9 for that. The Broadsword will get enchants later, which might make it worthwhile.
 Lindy Hop [2] Stefan or Immortal Cursed Knight Prior to the arrival of the Claw Sword, it was the wet dream of each Rune Knight. This weapon used to be the most endgame two-handed sword we could get, and had the right to stay at the n1 spot as a weapon for RKs thanks to all the pros it has. It has the most ATK out of all 2HS, has 2 slots, gives ATK% and ASPD% bonuses based on the refine, is indestructible (goodbye Golem Card), and is enchantable twice (Malangdo Enchant. Getting a Lindy past +10 used to be every main Crit RK's goal (You can settle for a +8 if you find it too hard or too expensive to go further in the refine hell). You should aim for Sharp enchants.
 Guardian Knight Claymore [2] Glast Heim Challenge Mode A weapon that came out with the late update of Challenge Glast Heim, this weapon is like its update, kind of outdated. It still is decent if properly refined though, and is kind of a more racial hunting oriented version of the Lindy, for Undead and Angel monsters. If you have many Temporal Fragments taking the dust and you're looking for a potential specific budget option, this may be interesting for you.
 Claw Sword [2] Einbech Mine 3 The new contender that surpasses Lindy, ladies and gentlemen, here is the ultra expensive Claw Sword ! Comes with +15% ATK and +5 crit by default, has a beautiful 300 weapon ATK (40 lower than Lindy Hop but who cares) and gets huge damage increase on refine stages ! Including an non-exhaustive list of : +25% critical dmg, chance to proc +20% DMG to all sizes for a duration, and +7 crit ! You can also enchant it and go for ATK% or crit dmg% or physical damage against a specific type of monster, or even DEF ignore% !
 Volar [2] Bioresearch Laboratory This two-handed sword shines above other weapons for Ignition Break as it reduces its cooldown by 1 second, and the special enchant Seyren's memory increases the damage of Ignition Break by 5% every 3 refines. If at the same time you have already an overrefined Old Rune Circlet, it is recommended you go for something else other than Seyren Windsor Card if you already have a lot of IB %damage increase, to get the greatest damage combination (for example Contaminated Wanderer cards).
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is the second most interesting card for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies by 20% (most of the monsters from the game).
Hunter Fly Card Hunter Fly Since you'll be mobbing a lot, you'll often proc the life leech with Ignition Break. And since it hits hard, you'll probably regen a big chunk of your HPs.
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer This is a better version of the WK card, that got out with the Abyss Glast Heim dungeon. It gives 30% against Medium & Large by itself, so it's better for two-handed swords since we can't equip KK cards.
 Seyren Windsor Card Tomb of the Fallen This card is awesome for Ignition Break as it increases up to 60% its damage, depending on several conditions. You start with +20%, get another 20% if your weapon is level 4 and another 20% if your weapon is +10 or more. This is a very good contender you can get for an IB build.
 Greater Special Alnoldi Card Garden Watcher One of the two cards that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, this card blesses us with the mighty Melee modifier, and gives us the indestructible property to our weapon. Considering we now got a very strong melee boost with the new Thanatos Tower cards, I wouldn't recommend it alongside the thanatos combo, except if you do Crush Strikes in which case your weapon could break and this card would prevent it.
 Greater Ruba Papilla Card Greater Ruba Papilla The other card that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, it boosts heavily critical damage based on the refine of the weapon. Due to the large quantity of critical damage everywhere else on the slots and the other better options available (size, melee), it is highly recommended to forget this card and go for the other choices listed before (it is still listed as a possibility per nature of my guide, built to show the many paths available to you as the reader).
 Rekenber Guard Card Rekenber Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; this card is a stronger version of the Greater Special Alnoldi, and it works on a bigger variety of weapons (all swords and daggers). The only weakness within this card that I can see is the lack of the indestructible property that the GSA gives.
 Gan Ceann Card Gan Ceann This very specific card is an optional choice you may opt for if hunting MvPs, since the majority of the MvPs you'll kill are going to be Large monsters and this card excels at boosting damage against such size. To make it work to its fullest, you'll want to do the weapon card combo it offers.
 Brutal Murderer Card Brutal Murderer Same as above except this time for Medium enemies.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades. You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK). This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players.
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop The CK's shield is now most of the time the BiS, for all builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. A +0 should be more than enough though !
 Royal Guard Shield [1] Banquet for Heroes This shield is quite rare because nobody bothers trying to get one. It gives you the ability to use Shield Spell Lv 1, which can be used to increase your ATK based on the shield base defense. With this shield it's not extremely good, but why would you refuse a possibly free ATK bonus ? You can always switch after using the ATK buff for another shield (but don't bother with this shield if you aren't looking for any kind of min-maxing, the ATK bonus is not really incredible).
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Gaster Card Gaster If you plan on mobbing only, that means you'll be facing 90% of the time normal monsters. Gaster Card is perfect for that, since it reduces the damage of ALL the non-boss type monsters by 25%.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). If you don't have any, you might want to get one of the cheapest for starters. The +10 MDEF is really neat and if you get a pair of Temporal Boots (any of the boots, even the basic ones should work), you'll also get a +15% HP and +5% SP set bonus. Try getting a GSS with several STR enchants for our IB build. If you're trying to push your critical rate but with a low budget, you can try getting a Green Maiden Card since it'll give you a lot of critical rate as your GSS will most likely be +10 or more, because they are dropped already refined up to +12 in the Faceworm's Nest instance.
 Nidhoggur's Shadow Garb [1] Nidhoggur Shadow This one might be a bit complicated to obtain if you're new, but it can be a really good alternative to GSS if you plan on playing Dragon Breath or Ignition Break build and you need a bit of survivability: this garment gives you a +7% resistance to ALL elements and a 1% chance to regenerate 1% of your damage dealt on one attack (AoE attacks like IB work). Combine this with a Cursed Knight's Shield and you have 14% resistance to all elements ! Quite the underrated garment in my opinion.
 Excellion Wing Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis If you want to go full ATK, you can always pick the wing and put 3 ATK enchants on it; the combo with the Excellion Suit will also increase your survivability with some P.Dodge. But beware, the after cast delay reduction won't work on Ignition Break, as the skill has a cooldown that you can't reduce with current gears (and no after cast delay).
 Valkyrian Manteau [1] Valkyrie Randgris The Valkyrian Manteau won't help much in terms of defense but you'll get a +% reflect based on your refine so it can be nice to help proc some bonuses that work on physical attacks dealt to the enemies. Also, if you combine it with an Abusive Robe, you'll get a great ATK% bonus thanks to the set effect as well as a HP% bonus, based on the refine of the Abusive Robe. Perfect for Ignition Break !
 Heroic Backpack [1] Monster Hunter I brought back from abyss the Backpack, as it still is a very good multi-purpose option and because IB can now crit. The 90+ VIT bonus which gives neutral resistance will synergize well with a Raydric combo, and you'll get nice buffs from the STR and the LUK bonuses too.
 Clergy Manteau [1] Odin's Past The Clergy manteau can be a possible option to reach very high amounts of critical rate, because it can be enchanted up to three times, with among the possibilities, crit enchants that give between 5 and 10 each, for a potential maximum of +30 critical rate on the equipment.
 Illusion Engine Wing A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice and you'll want to get 2 Critical modules as well as one Above All module. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. It can be as good as a +9 FAW with 3 Fatal3 enchants, but only if you equip a pair of Illusion Leg A to get the +10% Critical damage bonus from the combo, which allows it to reach the same critical damage potential as the FAW. You'll get as well more critical rate than FAW with this one.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This is our go-to, not too expensive garment for raw damage, a bit similar to HBP as it gives you a bonus different for each stat you've increased, every 20 base points. The reason why it surpasses HBP, is because you can enchant it 3 times (as long as you got it refine to +9, otherwise it's 2 times at +7 and only once under) with strong enchants like Fatal, and it can go up to Fatal 4 on one enchant.
 King Schmidt's Manteau [1] Fall of Glast Heim This garment is a more expensive option which is similar to the Clergy's Manteau as it solely focuses on critical rate through its 3 enchants (but this time it's Sharp enchants), it will be a good steroid option to skyrocket your critical rate. While you can keep it not refined, it will also give you a sweet damage bonus to Fire and Shadow monsters depending on the refine of your garment, and even possibly a damage increase against Dragon and Formless monsters when reaching +11.
 Temporal Agi Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim Here comes our strongest contender of the current times, the Temporal Agi Manteau ! Similar to its brother Str Manteau, it gives critical damage instead of the ATK%, alongside the ATK and the %size. You will want to enchant it with critical damage for MOAR POWAH BABE ! Beware that even though this garment brings the most damage boost, it does not provide any critical rate !
 Temporal Luk Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim A compromise between the IB build and the Agi Manteau, this one gives you crit rate and crit damage depending on the refine. The nice thing with this option is that you can actually for once benefit of the Temporal Manteau combo, allowing you to pierce heavily the DEF of Brute and Demon monsters.
 Automatic Engine Wing A-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. We still have access to interesting modules like  Automatic Module (Critical) but the new addition that may make you think twice about getting this garment or another is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very welcome %Melee boost.
 Gray Wolf Manteau [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This manteau is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing A-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a +50 ATK bonus. While it may not surpass the Agi Manteau in damage, it wins in utility. The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be an important source of damage with the Melee% it brings. The second slot we will want the Wolf Orb (Critical) which can provide up to +15 Critical rate and +24% Critical damage. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Dex) on this one if you're playing with stats for cast reduction, or go for Wolf Orb (Str) if you don't need it or play VCT% reduction.
 Green Maiden Card Chung E This super extra-tight budget card will save your ass if you're really lacking critical rate and you're using a high refined garment such as a +10 GSS.
 Raydric Card Brown Rat If you think you need more resistance, then feel free to take the Raydric Card ! 20% reduction of the damage coming from the monsters, hell yes.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat This is the card that gives the highest ATK on garment. Your best bet if you want a card that increases both damage and attack speed on that slot.
 Petal Card Petal It's one of the great stat cards; you will get a 24% critical damage bonus since you have 120 LUK and it gives 2% per 10 base LUK.
 Happiness Giver Card Happiness Giver Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is sickeningly powerful as it gives at 120 STR a whooping 55% Melee damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Mistress of Shelter card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Temporal Boots of Strength Old Glast Heim The Temporal STR Boots are usually not super expensive, and provide a great ATK bonus; if you refine it at +3 (safe refine) and you have 120 STR, you'll get 57 ATK thanks to these boots. You get +50 ATK by having 120 points in STR, and you get +7 ATK every 3 refines.
  • Lucky Day is easier to proc and doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, MATK, P.Dodge. Probably your safest bet on an IB build !
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit. I kept it here because it's really strong, but keep in mind that if you get too much strong monsters hitting you, yes you'll proc it, but you will also probably die staggered by the mobs. It's fine for farming lower level areas like Juperos though !
 Temporal Boots of Luck [1] Old Glast Heim A pretty good pair of boots for critical builds as it gives a whooping 30% critical damage bonus. The enchants are going to define the price of your boots (if you want to buy them instead of crafting them); what you want for basic enchant is FS7, or go for ASPD4
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit.
  • Lucky Day is easier to proc and doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, MATK, P.Dodge.
  • Speed of Light is an exotic but interesting choice, and even more since we got the new Fall of Glast Heim instance with the insignia enchants. SoL allows you to dodge 100% of the normal hits thanks to the +100 P.Dodge proc.
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type, and when paired with the Illusion Engine Wing A-type you'll get +10% critical damage. The item by itself doesn't have any %critical damage bonus, but it's not a big loss since we already have a ton of that, and it brings an especially strong enchant that you can slot on it, named Overpower. It gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK swords) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds.
 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a big increase on the  Automatic Module (Overpower) module, which got on its 17.2 version a +10% Melee modifier when Overpower procs. On the Automatic Leg you can put Legendary enchants on all slots so you can also use  Automatic Module (Firing Shot) for the DEX it provides for your cast time, and  Automatic Module (Fatal Flash) for the Critical damage.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong. If you are overflowing with critical damage and running Temporal Boots of Luck, you might consider switching to these.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs,and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Overpower) to get some sweet STR and the nice Melee% mod as well, or go for Wolf Orb (Firing Shot) if you're in dire need of DEX. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie It does the same as Ifodes (possibly better depending on the refine) and it's cheaper. The downside is that your HP gets reduced (The ASPD% of Ifodes is not a big deal for us).
 Chaotic Baphomet Jr. Card Chaotic Baphomet Junior An interesting budget card for crit rate, it'll help you achieve some ok amount of crit rate since IB requires so much, for a little investment.
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ATK+3% and ASPD+5%; usually cheaper than Geffen Bully and the ATK% increase is great for a footgear card.
 Rigid Nightmare Terror Card Rigid Nightmare Terror A pretty good budget card, you can combine it with the Nightmare Terror Card that goes into the Armor slot for a sweet 10% ATK.
 Geffen Bully Card Geffen Bully This used to be a very good min-maxing card if you want to increase your critical damage; it gives 5% Critical damage and 3% ASPD.
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman That card gives us flat ATK based on STR, and it's the new BiS card for the critical build thanks to its amazing combo with the Deep Sea King Dramoh Card that gives you +15% critical damage.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Sheriff's Left Badge Rock Ridge's main quest For what it does, this accessory is pretty strong. It suits every build you could play as a RK since it increases your ATK by 3%, your HP by 1000 and your ranged damage by 3% if you leveled up your stats to at least 90. (respectively STR, VIT and DEX). To get it, you only need to do the main quest of Rock Ridge (Fistful of Zeny), which is mostly speaking to NPCs and you only need to be level 100 to do it.
 Peuz's Seal Skogul or Frus This is a RK-only accessory, it gives 20 ATK and 20 SP. It's also possible to enchant it; it's a good ATK budget accessories.
 Luk Glove [1] Eclage You will have to take either one or two of these if you're trying to get more than 90 critical chances and you don't have enough money for expensive items. If you're going to keep 120 LUK for the boots, this accessory will give you +12 Critical; combine it with an Essence of Evil Luk 3, and you'll get at least +16 Critical (1 more point if you get past a Crit cap on your LUK stat) per glove.
 Pendant of Maelstrom [1] Nightmarish Jitterbug This used to be one of the most offensive-oriented accessories you could get. We're one of the few classes that will benefit from both the effects of the accessory (even though the MATK bonus won't be really noticeable on your damage). Get this one if you're playing on a budget build (the price decreased since the GMT update) and you have a lot of ATK already as the bonus will only get better.
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus (1% more than PoM) and 10% ASPD.
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament Used to be one of the strongest accessories you could get, depending on the 2 enchants you have on it. Could go from 40M with bad enchants, to... 1B with godly enchants (2 critical damage enchants for example). It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it, making it a better choice than Pendant of Maelstrom. Try to get 2 critical damage enchants on it.
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for the IB RK, are the Fatal and the Drain modules. The last slot is up to you !
 Royal Guard Ring [1] Friday A very versatile accessory that can gives %HP/SP. It has access to a large amount of enchants, including one very interesting for us which is Sharp ! This goes very well hand-in-hand with the next accessory as both can only be equipped on a specific slot (this one being locked to the right accessory slot), and both can get enchanted with Sharp, which will help us reach great amounts of critical rate.
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK (this is pretty huge by itself, compared to that the critical insignia is crap with its small 7% critical damage) and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantments for IB RK are (like Crit RK since IB now crits) Strong and Flash:
  • Strong : When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%. This is by far the strongest one as it increases the size modifier.
  • Flash : When equipped with Speed of Light, increases critical damage by 30%. While not as good as the Strong one (because size modifier is super interesting and critical damage is something we already have a plethora of), it is a great budget choice and Speed of Light boots work very well for doing mobtrains with the 100 PDodge bonus.
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Fatal) gives us now a nice +10 critical rate instead of the old +4, pretty useful to beat the high critical shield of some enemies; the  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) adds 20 ATK now, and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one that interests us most is Fatal of course. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to +15 Critical rate and +12% Critical damage per enchant. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR if possible.
Gold Scaraba Card Gold Scaraba This is the second card that gives the most flat ATK on the accessory slot (Gigantes gives the double). Not very used nowadays, you should be abl to find it for cheap.
Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit With this card combo you can get 7% ATK, to finish your stuff in beauty.
Gigantes Card Gigantes This is the highest ATK card you can get on accessory, you can only equip it on the left accessory though. The best thing to do is to combine it with the Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card which is equipped on the right slot, and adds 4% ATK and 4 STR.
Ominous Heater Card Ominous Heater A very interesting choice as it will help a lot for your critical rate. Please note that the set with Ominous Assaulter doesn't work twice, even with 2x the cards.
Chaotic Killer Mantis Card Chaotic Killer Mantis A cheap card for pure critical damage thanks to its combo with Angra Mantis, It gives a big amount of critical damage, but beware you get no critical chance bonus on this one !
 Void Mimic Card Void Mimic A huge critical damage card giving far more than all its peers with a big 15%. The combo would be nice but it means giving up one of the strong garment cards, not recommended.
 Grey Wolf Card Grey Wolf This card locked to the left slot, arrived with Episode 18 and finally brings us (alongside the card it comboes with) Melee% bonuses on the accessory card slots. The Grey Wolf Card will give you 6% Melee, and an additional 8% Melee if equipped with the Phantom Wolf Card, for a total of 20% Melee on accessory slots.
 Phantom Wolf Card Phantom Wolf The other part of the combo with the Grey Wolf Card, this one does basically the same thing (6% Melee) but is locked on the right slot instead.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can put in this essence.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 It's sometimes better or cheaper than some other options (like Gold Scaraba).
Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get in shape as it doesn't require any refinement; it provides 2 very interesting bonuses for us which are:
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness, and most importantly a lot of stat reduction for our VCT !
  • 50% DEF Pierce on Normal Monsters : When you get closer to endgame and start entering areas such as Einbech Mine 3, you'll have quite the hard time trying to one shot these monsters, the reason being they have high DEF. 50% pierce is not perfect but it helps a lot !

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears. Also, this DEF pierce does not work on boss protocol monsters so beware !

 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
 Almighty Shadow Focus

 Almighty Shadow Brooch

Nightmare Toy Factory & Thanatos Tower (Hard) 2 popular shadow gears that actually do not combo together, these will only give bonuses through refines. You get +1 to All Stats every refine of the shadow gear, meaning with both you can reach +20 All Stats; this is extremely interesting for solving the issue of IB's cast time with the great amount of DEX and INT we'll get through these accessories.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, which will help cover the weaknesses some weapon types have, helping us catch up to spear users with Dragon Training. For the most common weapon being 2HS, it'll raise back up the size penalty on Small and Medium monsters.
 Mammoth Shadow Plate Sub Stat Shadow Gears A very basic but helpful shadow armor, this plate gives +10 Critical rate by default and you'll get up to 5 more upon refining it to the max. This will help you solve some build planning issues with newer gears that do not provide as much crit rate as before, or because of custom content with very high critical shield.
 Blitz Shadow Buckler Sub Stat Shadow Gears Same as above except you get only +5 by default.
 Ignition Shadow Ring Zaedronath (MH) The One Ring as some might say, this shadow gear actually is so strong it can occupy the spot of BiS shadow ring as it provides CD reduction for Ignition Break.
