When refined and combined with Volar and a double Wave Break Automatic Armor, one will be able to spam IB without any kind of delay, thus making this skill exponentially strong, even way more than what it already was.
 Ignition Shadow Set Zaedronath (MH) The full set that includes the Ignition Shadow Ring seen above, is pretty good and versatile but might not be the very best for those that seek perfection. It gives a bit more of IB skill mod which an RK usually already has plenty of, and will provide DEF pierce on all races by at least 40% depending on the refines of your set. The issue with this is that it's not a full DEF pierce, and also you lose the slots for the Almighty accessories.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Melee Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Broken Warehouse Manager
  • Middle: Angelgolt (Pink)
  • Lower: Sharp Magic
 This set of stone will boost up your Melee % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot. Feel free to go for it if you are already well stocked on Critical damage and skill mods.
 Critical Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Contaminated Raydric
  • Middle: Rigid Kaho
  • Lower: Ancient Robot
 This set of stone will boost up your Critical damage modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot although you might want to fill it with the Critical Onyx like explained below. Feel free to go for it if you are already well stocked on Melee damage and skill mods or need the critical rate.
 Critical Onyx [G] Onyx Shop The Critical Onyx is a pretty strong stone by itself already with its 20% Critical damage bonus, but it also brings up a combo with the Critical Amber Set, offering a +10 Critical rate bonus; this is especially useful when you already have your build set up to have enough critical rate but want to discard some gear pieces that were giving a lot of it for example to swap accessories to the Sinful/Brilliant Light ones, since they do not offer any crit rate.
 Rune Knight Onyx II [G] Onyx Shop This stone is more focused on our build as it provides direct IB skill mods; you will get 15% from that stone itself, and also 10% more if you combo it with the Lord Knight Onyx II [M].
 Guillotine Cross Onyx II [G] Onyx Shop An unusual choice that is available to us is to go for other classes' stones. The most interesting one so far is the second set of Guillotine Cross which offers 15% Critical damage, which doesn't seem all that interesting at first compared to the Critical Onyx; but you can combo it with the Assassin Cross Onyx II [U] for an additional 5% ATK and 15% Critical damage (thus reaching a total of 30% Critical damage with just 2 stones).

Spiral Pierce

Some of you have been asking for it, and here it is ! An unpopular yet efficient single-target ranged skill, that can actually go high in terms of DPS. Stay true to your Lord Knight roots and make Seyren proud !

Stats

Here are the stats for Spiral Pierce :

  • STR 120
  • AGI 120~
  • VIT 90~
  • INT 90~
  • DEX 120
  • LUK 1

We're of course putting 120 STR in this build because it relies heavily in ATK. Close to 120 base AGI is necessary because we're looking for maximum spammability on this build. The 90 VIT is there to help build up your natural HP pool, eliminate the stun possibility and also proc the effect of the Heroic Backpack. Since this is all about skill-spamming, so of course we're going to invest a lot of INT to get enough time for the Rideword to regen your HP and SP, as well as helping reduce VCT. We got 120 DEX to reduce the most possible the cast as well as eliminate FCT thanks to Temporal Dex Boots. LUK should get the remaining points for a small ATK bonus.


Skills

So this could be simply played like other skill-focused builds where you only focus on a single skill (which here is Spiral Pierce of course), but you may also level other 3rd class ranged skills like Sonic Wave, Hundred Spear and Dragon Breath. Another good addition would be Brandish Spear since it's ranged since the skill rework, and scales off STR.

Strategy

It is mostly going to revolve around spamming Spiral Pierce, so I'd recommend setting your Spiral Pierce hotkey on Smartcast mode in NovaExt. If you don't know how to do that, you might want to read the tutorial here. If you feel like you don't regen enough with the HP/SP leech equipments you got, you can try getting a Succubus/Incubus pet to further increase the chances of resplenishing your HP/SP.

Spiral Pierce is a skill that requires 86% ACD for maximum spam.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the Spiral Pierce build.

Sets
Set Way to obtain Notes
 Illusion Sprint set Illusion of Twins The Illusion Sprint combo between the Mail and the 2 accessories (Ring and Glove) is actually a very interesting underdog option. The armor by itself offers 12% ACD and a few VIT points as well as 2 Nive slots on which you can put Powerful Nives for up to +14% damage to all races, and can be comboed with the 2 accessories for a whooping +15% max HP/SP ! The Illusion Sprint Ring comboes with the Mail for 10% more ACD reduction, and comboes with the Illusion Sprint Glove for 5% more ACDr (the Glove itself giving 3% ACDr). The accessories cannot have Nives but they can be enchanted with some stats; this cheap 3-pieces set will bring you a total of 30% ACD which will help you reaching high amounts of ACDr early on. You can then combo these pieces with the Shoes as well, which will bring a lot to the table as well: +10% ATK, +70 ATK, +25% damage against bosses when comboing the Mail and the Shoes, then with the Shoes and the accessories you will get some on-hit chances to gain the gigantic +150 STR and +150 AGI buffs ! Beweare though, the combo of the shoes with the accessories will continuously drain your HP and SP, so you might want to have some swap equipment to avoid losing HP&SP when not fighting, and bring some leech effects if you plan on using this combo so you can regenerate in the middle of the fight. Feel free as well to swap the Powerful Nives on armor and shoes for Dexterous Nives if you have some issues with Cast Time.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Rideword's Hat [1] Top Custom Headgear Quests This is a really strong hat as it gives you a chance to convert your damage as HP and/or SP. It might be necessary to fight the SP consumption of Spiral Pierce.
 Ancient Gold Ornament [1] Top Wolfchev's Laboratory Awesome hat for our build, it boosts our ATK by 8%, and gives an all stat +2 bonus, great for cast time. A good budget hat since the Bio5 update, you might find it for a cheap price on the market.
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat. It can be interesting if you already have it on hand or got too much of skill modifiers.
 Heart Wing Headband [1] Top Master of Coin Looking for even MOAR spammability ? Look no further, Heart Wing Headband is there for you ! It reduces your ACD by 5% and your SP consumption by 10%, then reduces both by 3% every 3 refines ! Truly great for skill-spamming builds.
 Old Rune Circlet [1] Top Tomb of the Fallen Currently the strongest hat for its refine bonuses and enchants, but also the hardest to get. Every 2 refines, you have 20% bonus damage on Ignition Break, and 15% on Hundred Spears. For Spiral Pierce, you'll want the Mettle enchantment, which gives ATK+3% and HIT+3 every level; it could help a lot in case you're trying to hit high Flee enemies.
 Temporal Circlet (Rune Knight) [1] Top Glast Heim Challenge Mode A new option that tops off the Bio hat, as you can get Mettle at the same time as a Temporal Jewel Str enchant which gives flat ATK, hit rate and ATK% based on the hat's refine.
 Goral Crown [1] Top Goral Crown One of the latest hats pre-4th classes, it offers a pretty good boost at high refine without the need to invest into an annoying RNG enchant system, which is a huge advantage for me. If you are playing with a Vernan, you'll also benefit from 10% ACD with the hat combo (sadly no Spiral mods for us on this one).
 Tiger King Doll Hat-LT [1] Top Master of Coin An improved version of the White Drooping Eddga, this one provides a lot of bonuses even outside of the transformation: +2 STR,DEX,POW,CON and 10% ASPD and damage against Brute monsters by default, up to +25% Melee mods and +10% ATK through refines, as well as up to 5% ATK, +3 POW and +9 P.ATK through grading. For the transformation part, we get gifted with amazing boosts: +35 ATK per refine and +20 P.ATK if the hat is refined at least to +10 ! It's more of a raw ATK hat that is not really tailored for Spiral, but it provides a lot of damage steroid by itself when it triggers, and you can also get 0.5s FCT reduction through the grading, which can allow for a better boots choice.
 Sigrun's Wings Middle Nova Shop It's basically a cheap trade-off: by getting this flat +1 ASPD you'll be able to invest less AGI on your build, meaning more DEX in your stats (Points past 120 are expensive, watch out !).
 Angel Spirit Middle Nova Shop ATK and MATK+2%, STR+2. Similar to Ancient Gold Ornament, it's great if you want to keep increasing your ATK; but you won't have a slot on this hat.
 New Wave Sunglasses Middle Custom Headgear Quests The current middle hat trend for skill-spam builds. Its 10% ACD bonus is awesome for the slot it occupies, and should definitely be your first choice if you have the money or the time to farm the crafting items.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD% reduction, which we can increase even more through enchants while keeping a card slot.
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good budget choice thanks to its +1% physical damage bonus. If you're looking for something cheaper, go for a Bandit Scarf.
 Well-chewed Pencil Lower Nova Shop A very good choice as it is quite cheap, and actually gives you a good stat bonus for a lower hat (DEX+2), as well as HIT to help you clear these pesky and agile enemies.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin.
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest This pretty interesting all-stats lower hat can be obtained by doing a small but rewarding quest.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, which is in our case more interesting thanks to the +2 all stats bonus it gives instead of +1 for our Instant Cast goal.
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory The most expensive and rare lower hat, it is also the BiS hat to get ACD reduction when in combo with the Fallen Warrior Manteau: the main reason behind it, is the great amount of ACD reduction it gives based on your VIT. You get 4% every 30 VIT base points.
 Golden Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Ranged damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This new card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you should go for an EoE DEX or STR 3.
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A new hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus but considering our build is not concerned by HP, you shouldn't bother and just put an offensive card on the shoes.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Abusive Robe [1] You can craft it with 600 Honor Tokens, these are obtainable in the Banquet for Heroes quests. This is the most common armor for physical builds against Demi-Humans, Undeads and Demons since you get a %defense bypass on them per refine, as well as the skill Attention Concentrate at level 1. The reason why it's commonly used and refined to +7 is also because of the enchants you can apply on it.

Thanks to the DEX enchants, you can get much more easily Instant Cast with this armor. You'll trade damage you could have with Lava Leather/Excellion for spammability if you don't want to invest too much on DEX elsewhere.

 Excellion Suit Craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis This used to be one of the best budget armors you can get for offensive purposes, as you can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK) and it gives you ACD reduction. Going for the Unfrozen blueprint might be nice too to prevent mistakes (monsters who cast Frost Diver for example ?). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki. Spiral Pierce is a skill that has ACD, so getting this set will improve a lot your spammability.
 Lava Leather Suit [1] Magma Dungeon F3 An old armor which gives a lot of flat ATK, it is pretty much the physical version of the Flattery Robe once you get it +7, since it gives +150 ATK at this refine (only +100 before +7).
 Lava Leather Armor [1] Magma Dungeon F3 A more defensive choice compared to the LLSuit shown before, instead of getting +50 ATK at +7, you get a +100 DEF bonus. A possibility to consider and ponder on since RKs have a naturally low DEF.
 YSF01 Plate [1] Werner Laboratory This bad boy Seyren has allowed us to wear his awesome armor, which will totally power us up ! His plate gives a huge ATK% bonus, based on your STR (if it reaches 125) and the refine of the armor. Definitely top tier for our build, especially with the combo with the manteau that you'll see in the Garments section ! It is now kinda outdated, you can get it for cheap nowadays.
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the other armors thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants at least, and if you wanna use that armor on other classes like SS Ranger, you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it pretty strong for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races. The big downside to it is the lack of ACD.
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new contender from 17.2 ! This armor can be enchanted with a variety of different enchants, the interesting ones for us are  Automatic Module (Hundred Spiral) for the skill modifier it provides and  Automatic Module (Delay After Skill) for the ACD it provides just like its Illusion counterpart. You may also go for  Automatic Module (Power) and/or  Automatic Module (Range Force) if you want a more generic armor.
 Illusion Sprint Mail [1] Illusion of Twins Alongside the Sprint Shoes you'll see later in the Shoes section, this armor was released to combo with all the Illusion Sprint parts. In our case it'll be interesting to use if we go for the shoes as you get through the combo everything you would normally find on an Illusion/Automatic armor : ATK, ATK%, Melee/Ranged% and ACD% reduction; and it will also solve the FCT issue through a whooping 0.7s FCT reduction bonus. On top of that you even get damage against bosses, isn't that neat ?
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. Sadly there's still no Spiral Pierce module, so we have to stick with Wolf Orb (Angle Shot) which provides +40% Ranged. The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the huge amount of ATK, ATK% and Melee% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF. A super cheap budget choice.
Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, and it's pretty cheap ! Might be interesting if you pick a weapon that can be destroyed and need to use Rhydo.
Hardworking Pitman Card Hardworking Pitman A new and much better choice overall for armor than the old usual cards, this one adds 5% ATK, that's 1/3 of an Amdarais Card ! It also gives +10 HIT, it will contribute towards a tailored HIT stuff for high flee monster mobbing; nothing as frustrating as missing all your hits with Spiral...
Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric It's the same as the Pitman one but without the HIT part, except it has a combo with the Raydric Card which will make you much tankier : +10% Neutral Resistance (Raydric already gives +20%) and +5% more ATK. The ATK part of the combo is pretty neat because it compensates for the loss of a damage card on the garment slot like Brown Rat Card or Wakwak Card.
Dame of Sentinel Card Observation This card by itself does not do much aside from giving us a bit more DEX for instant cast, but it's an important part for a combo with of the strongest garment cards for us (Empathizer).
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Death Guidance [2] Amdarais from Old Glast Heim A 200 ATK two-handed sword that give you a lot of survival capacity; it gives you +20 Perfect Dodge and the possibility to do an AoE life steal when you physically attack. Watch out for the Hell Power that you can sometimes cast on yourself, it'll prevent you from being resurrected for several minutes.
 Thanatos Spear [1] Ghost Palace A very classic weapon with incorporated leech in it, if you are leveling in an area with lots of Reflect Shield monsters, this weapon will do very good.
 Thanatos Long Spear [1] Ghost Palace Same as the one above except it's a two-handed spear with stronger weapon ATK; if tankiness is none of your concern, then you might want to drop your shield and go for that.
 Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Great Demon Baphomet in Sealed Shrine The TGL is an awesome weapon for ACD as it reduces your cast delay between skills by 20%, same thing for your SP consumption. You'll even be able to enchant it with %ranged damage twice (Expert Archer enchantment). The only downside is that it's not a very heavy weapon, so you will lose on one of the big factors that increase the damage of the skill.
 Hunting Spear [1] Kraken or Leak or Fallen Bishop or Boitata This contestant is playing alone in his category as it is pretty much the best (and only worth it) one-handed spear you could find for Spiral Pierce, with its mighty 420 (No, I'm not saying it) weight. It pierces the defense of Brute monsters, is level 4 and can even be Malangdo enchanted !
 Cardo [1] Kraken or Nidhoggr's Shadow One of those old weapons of pre-renewal for Spiral Pierce, still a viable budget choice today ! With its stomping 560 weight, prepare to crush monsters of your level like they were flies ! And guess what good news Renewal brought ? It can be enchanted twice with Expert Archer. Definitely not to be underestimated when starting out on the build.
 Giant Lance Bio Labs 3/Wolfchev Laboratory So that lance is hands down the fattest Spiral Pierce weapon because of its enormous 2000 weight. The big problem though, is that it adds to Spiral Pierce a 20 seconds long cooldown, meaning you can't spam the skill at all. It could be used in specific cases like maybe PvP/BG for the memes ? Or when you need to OS some big monsters but you can still survive fine with other skills like Sonic Wave for example. It's not really played because the CD is horrid but it's still a possible option !
 Royal Knight's Broadsword [2] Abyss Glast Heim monsters This new addition to the two-handed swords roster is a pretty good rival to Lindy Hop, and will surpass Vicious Mind in terms of ATK and weight. Unlike this last one who needs a special enchant in order to be unbreakable by itself, this one just needs to be refined to +9 for that. The Broadsword will get enchants later, which might make it worthwhile if it includes ACD. The date we get these enchants is indefinitely pushed back until the staff gets more information on how they work.
 Royal Knight's Lance [2] Abyss Glast Heim A two-handed spear which brings a lot of ranged mods per refine as well as a neat 15% all races bonus at +9, if you find one for dirt cheap it can be a very good midgame weapon.
 Illusion Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Illusion of Labyrinth This is the new upgraded version of the Tae Goo Lyeon, which even with its moderate weight, is a very strong contender. It gives 2% ranged damage every refine, and gives you 20% ACD at +9. It's possible to get a 5% ACD enchantment on it, which is what you'll want to go for.
 Lindy Hop [2] Stefan or Immortal Cursed Knight The wet dream of each Rune Knight. This weapon is currently the most endgame two-handed sword we can get, and has the right to stay at the n1 spot as a weapon for RKs thanks to all the pros it has. It has the most weapon ATK out of all 2HS, has 2 slots, gives ATK% and ASPD% bonuses based on the refine, is indestructible (goodbye Golem Card), and is enchantable twice (Malangdo Enchant). You should aim for Expert Archer enchants.
 Claw Sword [2] Einbech Mine 3 The new contender that surpasses Lindy in versatility, ladies and gentlemen, here is the ultra expensive Claw Sword ! Comes with +15% ATK by default, has a beautiful 300 weapon ATK and gets huge damage increase on refine stages ! You can also enchant it and go for ATK% or physical damage against a specific type of monster, or even DEF ignore% ! It comes here as one of the best options because it gives you 20% ACD which is huge and pretty much replaces the Tae Goo Lyeon, it's kind of the fusion of a Lindy Hop and a TGL.
 Vernan [2] Bioresearch Laboratory This two-handed sword is the new best-in-slot weapon damage-wise for Spiral Pierce thanks to its amazing +30% damage on the skill and its HUGE weight of 650 in its weapon category. It also gives some ATK% and %ranged damage based on refine, and it also boosts a lot Sonic Wave by decreasing its CD by 1.5 seconds and increasing its damage by 30%, which means your Spiral Pierce build doubles as a Sonic Wave build ! It can also be enchanted with Seyren's Memory which adds more damage to both skills.
 Illusion Zephyrus [3] Illusion of Underwater A new contender to the scene as well as the best two-handed spear for Spiral Pierce (not too difficult as there aren't many good two-handed ones), this new lance doesn't joke with its 3 slots ! It's one of these very rare 3 slots level 4 weapons, which allows for a great variety of card combinations. It brings a lot of ranged% as well as flat ATK based on refinement, and you get also 20% Spiral damage at +7 and +10% size modifier against medium and large monsters. Its features brings it to the second place of the podium below Vernan.
 Adulter Fides Two-Handed Sword [2] Villa of Deception One of 4 new RK/DK weapons in the Episode 18, this weapon is surprisingly a classic level 4 weapon released post 4th job patch. It boasts a pretty high weapon ATK (300), Melee%, ACD% and some ATK based on refine rate, and you can enchant it.
 Adulter Fides Lance [2] Villa of Deception A new two-handed spear from Episode 18, just like the Adulter Fides 2HS it's a level 4 weapon with fairly high weapon ATK, ATK per refine and Ranged%, which can be enchanted with some more Ranged% or ACD%. Sadly it lacks the ACD% reduction that the 2HS offers.
 Vivatus Fides Two-Handed Sword [2]

 Vivatus Fides Lance [2]

Villa of Deception These are the upgraded versions of the Adulter Fides ones; they have the same stats and boosts per refine, except they're level 5 weapons; this means P.ATK per refine (which is huge) and some pretty neat Grading bonuses. Like the Adulter version, it's possible to enchant them, and if you want your weapon to be versatile, you may want to aim for ACD% reduction or Ranged% enchants.
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is the most interesting card for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies (most of the monsters from the game).
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer The current strongest size modifier card for weapons ! They give 10% more than WK cards, so you should aim for these for an endgame build. If you can use a shield somehow though, you will want to use a WK to combo with the KK card as it is stronger (you can only use the combo once).
 Greater Research Assistant Bot Card Greater Research Assistant Coming from the 17.2 update, this will only work if you are using a spear, it will give you a quantity of ranged% modifier based on refine.
 Rekenber Senior Guard Card Rekenber Senior Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; just like the GRAB this will only work if you are using a spear and it will give you more ranged% damage based on refine.
 Gan Ceann Card Gan Ceann This very specific card is an optional choice you may opt for. It only gets to its fullest effect if you do the weapon card combo it offers.
 Brutal Murderer Card Brutal Murderer Same as above except this time for Medium enemies.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades. You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK). This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players.
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here.
 Royal Guard Shield [1] Banquet for Heroes This shield is quite rare because nobody bothers trying to get one. It gives you the ability to use Shield Spell Lv 1, which can be used to increase your ATK based on the shield base defense. With this shield it's not extremely good, but why would you refuse a possibly free ATK bonus ? You can always switch after using the ATK buff for another shield (but don't bother with this shield if you aren't looking for any kind of min-maxing, the ATK bonus is not really incredible).
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). If you don't have any, you might want to get one of the cheapest for starters. The +10 MDEF is really neat and if you get a pair of Temporal Boots (any of the boots, even the basic ones should work), you'll also get a +15% HP and +5% SP set bonus. You could look for a cheap GSS with a combination of DEX and INT if you want to get easy IC.
 Excellion Wing Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis If you want to go full ATK, you can always pick the wing and put 3 ATK enchants on it; the combo with the Excellion Suit will also increase your survivability with some P.Dodge. Spiral Pierce is a skill that only has ACD, so getting this set will improve a lot your spammability.
 Valkyrian Manteau [1] Valkyrie Randgris The Valkyrian Manteau won't help much in terms of defense but you'll get a +% reflect based on your refine so it can be nice to help proc some bonuses that work on physical attacks dealt to the enemies. Also, if you combine it with an Abusive Robe, you'll get a great ATK% bonus thanks to the set effect as well as a HP% bonus, based on the refine of the Abusive Robe.
 Heroic Backpack [1] Monster Hunter Although the HBP doesn't give any ACD reduction, it still is a solid choice for the versatility it has : ATK, ASPD and ranged damage bonuses. If you feel like other garments kill too much your ASPD, you may go for this one as it does indeed not have any ACD reduction but it improves your attack speed and your damage overall, so you're not losing too hard on DPS.
 YSF01 Manteau [1] Werner Laboratory Next in the badass set of Seyren, we got the manteau ! Although it requires us having 125 VIT for its big 10% ACD reduction at +0, the fact that we get even more reduction from both the refine of the garment and from the combo with the armor, makes it a very powerful choice. Definitely something you'll want at +9 otherwise the garment is not worth wasting your stat points on it.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This garment has a very good %ranged damage potential with the enchants on it and will beat the Engine Wing from 17.1, but it lacks ACD reduction, so beware of the spammability.
 Illusion Engine Wing B-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice and you'll want to get 2 Fast modules. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. Since it's the B-type, when combined with the A-type armor we'll get 10% ACD so it's pretty strong for us, especially if you don't use a weapon that gives ACD like the TGL.
 Automatic Engine Wing B-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. We still have access to interesting modules like  Automatic Module (Fast) but the new addition that may make you think twice about getting this garment or another is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very welcome %Ranged boost.
 Temporal Str Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim The STR manteau, as many originally cash shop items, is a very powerful option for all non-crit physical builds. That garment bombs you with raw ATK, refined ATK% and spicy %size modifiers ! You'll want to put ACD% enchant on the garment, or Ranged% if you somehow already got too much ACD%.
 Gray Wolf Muffler [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The muffler is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing B-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a 10% ACDr bonus. While it may not surpass the Str Manteau in both ACD% reduction and damage, it wins in utility (and ultimately damage, you will see why). The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be our main enchant source of damage upgrade with the Melee% it brings. The second slot (which is the most interesting one I believe) can be enchanted with Wolf Orb (Guide Attack), which can bring up to 24 Perfect Hit rate ! This is extremely important for us on Spiral Pierce as our main counter is very high FLEE which some monsters boast thanks to using the skill Agi Up. Perfect Hit will allow us to hit while ignoring FLEE, much like a Critical hit. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Str) on this one or (Dex) if you need to reduce your cast time.
 Raydric Card Raydric If you think you need more resistance, then feel free to take the Raydric Card ! 20% reduction of the neutral damage coming from the monsters' basic attacks, hell yes.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat This gives a nice amount of ATK on garment, as well as a bit of ASPD%. If you feel like you're lacking too much attack speed, you might want to go for that one.
 Menblatt Card Menblatt One of the few cards in garment that give %ranged damage, this is a good cheap option even up to endgame.
 Empathizer Card Empathizer Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is pretty strong because at 120 DEX it gives 55% Ranged damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Dame of Sentinel card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Temporal Boots of Dexterity Old Glast Heim This is pretty much the only boots you want to go for as they eliminate the FCT of Spiral Pierce once you put 120 points in DEX.
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit. I kept it here because it's really strong, but keep in mind that if you get too much strong monsters hitting you, yes you'll proc it, but you will also probably die staggered by the mobs.
  • Lucky Day doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, HIT, P.Dodge. Probably your safest bet !
  • Hawk eye procs faster than Lucky Day and will increase your ASPD by a few points, but you'll suffer a SP drain
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type. It brings 2 strong enchants that will interest us :
    • Overpower which gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK swords) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds
    • Firing Shot which gives +50 DEX and +10% Ranged damage.

While Overpower will usually give you more damage, you need to think about your cast time and your ASPD, which Firing Shot will take care of. Up to you to find the one that fits the most with the equipments you chose !

 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a stronger combo with the Engine Wing, as well as the usual  Automatic Module (Overpower) and  Automatic Module (Firing Shot) modules.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong. You may also go for DEX nives if you need the stats for cast reduction, with lower damage boost. Beware also that those boots have no FCT reduction, you will have to find how to take care of Spiral's FCT somewhere else (for example go for the Illusion Sprint Mail for the combo !).
 Unknown STR Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of stat boots that was added with Airship Crash, these give a bit of ATK, HP and SP based on the refine of the boots which ain't crazy for lvl 5 boots. The main attraction comes from the potential proc when dealing damage which will grant a whooping +175 STR for 10 seconds, basically permanent when continuously hitting groups of enemies (kinda like the Illusion & Automatic procs). The STR boost can be increased through grading. While this gives no interesting modifier like the other previous boots, the STR boost is quite phenomenal; I'd recommend checking with a calculator if this would be stronger for you than Illusion Sprint Shoes as usually multiplcative modifiers tend to do better. Same as above, these boots do not have integrated FCT reductions so you will need something else to take care of it, like the Casting Onyx costume enchant for example.
 Unknown DEX Boots [1] Airship Crash Another pair of stats boots just like above, this one is an interesting alternative for us because of the huge quantity of DEX it brings, and there's a bit of strategy tied to it: You can exploit this to completely disregard the need of stacking DEX in your gears, only relying on your base 120 DEX (which with this setup, is not even needed to be kept that high except for HIT reasons) because getting that 175 bonus DEX will allow you to clear completely your VCT through stats. Yes you'll have a dirty cast time when the boots do not proc and that will make it awful to proc, but what if I told you there's an alternate way to deal with that ? If you possess a Vernan, you can simply spam Sonic Wave pretty fast since the skill has no cast time and you have the reduced CD and more than enough ACD% reduction; you will thus manage to easily proc the big DEX boost, and can safely switch back to Spiral Pierce. Neat huh ?
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Firing Shot) to get some DEX to clear cast time and for more HIT, as well as some Ranged%. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). You could also get the Wolf Orb (Fixed Casting) but we have a lot of other ways to get that nowadays so I wouldn't recommend it. The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie It's a cheaper choice than Ifodes, the downside is that your HP gets reduced and you don't get that neat ASPD bonus. You can though get a bigger ATK% if your boots are heavily refined.
 White Porcellio Card White Porcellio Another budget choice if you're planning to go cheap, this card gives you some flat ATK, and more if you refine your shoes or combo it with the Porcellio Card.
 Rigid Nightmare Terror Card Rigid Nightmare Terror This card is underestimated and allows you to get 10% ATK for a budget investment by putting a Nightmare Terror Card in your armor. Definitely something to look for if you don't wanna invest in the pricier options down there.
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ATK+3% and ASPD+5%; a bit expensive but the ATK% increase is great for a footgear card.
 Odoric Card Odoric Here we have a card that fits more the ranged bill as it improves your ranged damage by 5% and your ASPD by 3%. It is a mix between Ifodes and Blut Hase, perhaps something you'll be interested in if you're lacking ASPD.
 Blut Hase Card Blut Hase That card is a pretty good damage-oriented card you could ever get for boots as it gives +3% ATK as well as +5% ranged damage. Its price is also the highest of the non-mvp/miniboss cards, it's usually twice or thrice the price of an Ifodes.
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman A newer option that appears here actually as a mid-tier choice, it gives you a bunch of ATK depending on your base STR.
 Arena Arhi Card Geffen Night Arena A nice new addition from the revisited Geffen Tournament instance, this card provides us with +5% damage to all sizes, which can be pretty useful if you're low on size modifiers.
 Arena Blut Hase Card Geffen Night Arena The new updated version of the Blut Hase, this version provides instead 5% ATK and 7% Ranged.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Sheriff's Left Badge Rock Ridge's main quest For what it does, this accessory is pretty strong. It suits every build you could play as a RK since it increases your ATK by 3%, your HP by 1000 and your ranged damage by 3% if you leveled up your stats to at least 90. (respectively STR, VIT and DEX). To get it, you only need to do the main quest of Rock Ridge (Fistful of Zeny), which is mostly speaking to NPCs and you only need to be level 100 to do it.
 Pendant of Maelstrom [1] Nightmarish Jitterbug This used to be one of the most offensive-oriented accessories you could get, it has an all stats bonus so another good addition for your cast time ! Get this one if you're playing on a budget build (the price decreased since the GMT update).
 Broken Chip 1 [1]

 Broken Chip 2 [1]

Last Room They used to be a no-brainer back when bragi gave 100% ACD reduction because getting the 2 accessories give you +12 STR and +12 INT, and they're slotted, making them the best accessories for reducing VCT by stats. Now it's a little more delicate as we have to get ACD as well since Bragi got nerfed.
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus (1% more than PoM) and 10% ASPD. A well-spent investment if the only thing you lack is ASPD.
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament A good accessory, but not exactly the best for Spiral. Could go from 5M with bad enchants, to... a very high price with godly enchants. It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it, making it a better choice than Pendant of Maelstrom damage-wise. Try to get 2 ATK% enchants on each ring.
 Expert Ring [1] Ragged Zombie or Prison Breaker A very budget choice compared to Sarah Earrings, that gives half the performance but allows you to put a card on the accessory. The only downside is the SP consumption increase.
 Sarah's Left Earring

 Sarah's Right Earring

Sarah and Fenrir Another slot-less accessory which is quite popular because it's a very affordable spam-enabler accessory since you can reach up to 10% ACD reduction and I highly recommend getting the perfect enchant as it's not very hard. It is account-bound so you'll have to make them yourself.
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for the Spiral RK, are the ASPD, Expert Archer and the Drain modules.
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK (this is pretty huge by itself, compared to that the critical insignia is crap with its small 7% critical damage) and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantments for Crit RK are Strong and Flash:
  • Strong : When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%. This is by far the strongest one as it increases the size modifier, which is kinda the rarest modifier you can get.
  • Hawkeye : When equipped with Hawkeye, increases ATK by 10%. It's a more affordable but weaker option compared to the Strong enchant, still might be worthwhile !
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) adds 20 ATK now, the  Automatic Module (Expert Archer) has now a HIT bonus which is very welcome for us, and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus. I recommend using the Sinful set over the Brilliant Light one because it gives 0.3 FCT rather than 0.2, effectively reducing entirely the FCT on Spiral Pierce; this allows you to remove FCT gears elsewhere.
 Brilliant Light Ruby Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus. This only gives 0.2 FCT with the combo but if you're running already FCT elsewhere, this won't be an issue for you.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one which interests us the most is Expert Archer. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to +10% Ranged damage and +20 HIT, so pretty much with 2 accessories with 2 perfect enchants each, that means +40% Ranged and +80 HIT ! This is very helpful in order to solve our troubles trying to hit high FLEE enemies. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR or DEX if possible.
Gold Scaraba Card Gold Scaraba This is the second card that gives the most flat ATK on the accessory slot (Gigantes gives the double).
Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit The combo of the 2 Buffalo cards will help improving your ASPD as well as getting a bit more damage with their great +7% ATK and +7 AGI.
 Gigantes Card Gigantes A big flat 40 ATK that is only available on left slot, pretty interesting if your other accessory slot is busy and you can't use the buffalo combo, or you're simply missing one (because you're using a sarah earring for example).
 Sharp Magic Card /  Magic Poisoned Sanare Card /  Sewage Cramp Card /  Sewage Cramp Card /  Sewage Venenum Card 17.2 Cards These new options that came from 17.2 are listed here as possible options to further help on your cast time since they all give a combination of stats that include DEX, and they give a nice %HP boost as well, which will help you survive more.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can usually put in this essence.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 It's sometimes better or cheaper than some other options (like Gold Scaraba).
 Essence of Evil DEX 3 DEX + 4 Hit + 8 LUK - 4 It's actually core if you want to spam the most possible by reaching Instant Cast with stat reduction.

Feel free to optimize your build with these if you need to reduce the amount of DEX you got in your stats.

Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get in shape as it doesn't require any refinement; it provides 4 very interesting bonuses for us which are:
  • ASPD% and flat ASPD temporary buff when casting Enchant Blade based on Shadow Shield refine
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness, and most importantly a lot of status reduction for our VCT !
  • +50% DEF Pierce on Normal Monsters : When you get closer to endgame and start entering areas such as Einbech Mine 3, you'll have quite the hard time trying to one shot these monsters, the reason being they have high DEF. 50% pierce is not perfect but it helps a lot !

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears. Also, this DEF pierce does not work on boss protocol monsters so beware !

 Reload Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears One of the important stats and not always easy to fetch, is the After Cast Delay reduction. This set allows us to get 15% more reduction of it, without changing any of our gears, which is a big asset because it allows us to focus more on damage in equipments. You will need to refine the whole set to +9 to benefit from the big ACD% bonus. Don't forget to transform the Reload Shadow Armor into its version 2 to get slightly more ACD reduction as well as some VIT.
 Force Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears Part of the early batch we got with MH2, this set will fill the remaining slots when using an armor/shield/shoes set, just like the Reload set. It'll provide us with a bunch of extra ATK and ATK%, so this is a nice addition considering we don't need DEF pierce.
 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
 Almighty Shadow Focus

 Almighty Shadow Brooch

Nightmare Toy Factory & Thanatos Tower (Hard) 2 popular shadow gears that actually do not combo together, these will only give bonuses through refines. You get +1 to All Stats every refine of the shadow gear, meaning with both you can reach +20 All Stats. This will help us remove further the cast time of Spiral Pierce, as well as helping on the ASPD with the bonus AGI which synergizes well with 2HQ.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 Ancient Shadow Vest Sub Stat Shadow Gears The shadow armor slot is not very generous with damage boost choices, but there are also utility-oriented gears we can look at. This vest is one of them, bringing us up to +20 HIT, which will help us fight against high FLEE targets.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, which will help cover the weaknesses some weapon types have, helping us catch up to spear users with Dragon Training. For the most common weapon being 2HS, it'll raise back up the size penalty on Small and Medium monsters.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Ranged Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Chaotic Hunter Fly
  • Middle: Abyssman/Toxious
  • Lower: Deep Sea Swordfish
 This set of stone will boost up your Ranged % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot. This is your main damage option.
 Reload Onyx Set Onyx Shop An alternative to damage if once again you are lacking ACD for maximum spammability, you may go for this option to get the few remaining % you need.
 SP Absorb Onyx [G] Onyx Shop If you need to fill the remaining slot in case you went for the Ranged or Reload sets, you may get this utility onyx that will help you triggering some SP leech when necessary.
 Casting Onyx [G] Onyx Shop A great garment onyx which will remove the fixed cast time of Spiral Pierce, this will allow us to disregard the usual shoes options that take care of that part.
 Lord Knight Onyx II [U] Onyx Shop One of the three specific costume enchants for us, this one gives % ranged damage based on the learnt level of Spiral Pierce.
 Lord Knight Onyx [M] Onyx Shop This fairly straightforward Onyx boosts Spiral Pierce's damage by 15%.
 Lord Knight Onyx II [L] Onyx Shop The last Spiral Pierce oriented costume enchant, this one boosts Spiral by 20% instead. Considering the low quantity of Spiral mods available, it's recommended to get this one as well.

Sonic Wave

You've been looking for a ranged build because you've tasted too much melee reflect ? You still wanted to use a critical build because stacking HIT with Spiral Pierce ain't your cup of tea ? Look no further, Sonic Wave is here to fill that void in your heart !

Stats

Here's an average stat setup for SW that you can use:

  • STR 120
  • AGI 90+
  • VIT 90+
  • INT 40+
  • DEX 1
  • LUK 120

Yes you may think it is very similar to the Critical AA build if you've played it, which means it is totally compatible as a build swap !


Skills

Skill-wise, we find yet again the usual buffs any physical RK will want:

The reason why we want Enchant Blade here even if it doesn't bring any damage bonus to skills, is if you wanna one day use the Rune Knight Shadow Shield for the attack speed bonus it provides temporarily when casting Enchant Blade.

Strategy

Here we get the same usual buff routine for physical RKs like the other builds:

Auto Berserk > Berserk Potion > Enchant Blade > Two-Hand Quicken > Aura Blade > Turisus Runestone > Asir Runestone > Concentration > Parrying > Magnum Break

RK is a class that becomes a powerhouse all thanks to its buffs, so never forget them !

Sonic Wave is a skill which requires 50% ACD for maximum spam when using a Vernan to remove most of the cooldown, otherwise it's not necessary to get ACD.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the SW build. Don't forget that you can always take a look again at the General Equipment list, if some items here do not suit you or they are too expensive for you.

Sets

I keep together the set pieces (currently only one) that are only worth running together here.

Set Way to obtain Notes
 Peuz's set
  • Armor dropped by Raydric
  • Accessory dropped by Skogul and Frus
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 The famous beginner set for Wind Cutter, should also not be forgotten for Sonic Wave, as its 100% bonus also applies for our build ! While you will most certainly lack critical rate at first, this set will make up for it and help you build a good amount of damage when starting out. Since it also buffs WC, do not hesitate to use it when you get swarmed by monsters, it might save you on several occasions !
 Grace Knight set Eden Academy A fairly new set that is available through a custom beginner content, this practically free set will boost you in many ways: ATK, ASPD, critical damage... If you have no gears yet, going for this set will help you get more easily into midgame. My only issue with it if you're starting out is that it provides basically no critical rate, so you'll have to rely on other sources like your base LUK, buffs or manage to set in your stuff some crit rate equipments/cards, just like the Peuz set.
 YSF01 Seyren's set YSF01 Seyren The YSF01 set is pretty good if you get every piece +9, for content with sky-high DEF thanks to its DEF pierce ability. It provides also a good amount of ATK% and %Critical damage if you get the stat requirements (125 STR and 125 LUK respectively), which is not that big of a deal for us on SW.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Fox Ear Ribbons [1] Top Nova Shop This hat gives 10% aspd bonus, and when you physically attack, you have a chance of transforming into Moonlight Flower: it gives you a 5% ranged damage bonus (+1% every refine after +6), and +100% critical chance. It's a really interesting budget hat as you're guaranteed to crit on the majority of the content when you transform
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat. It can be interesting if you already have it on hand or got too much of skill modifiers.
 Black Ribbon [1] Top Master of Coin Another very cheap contender for the build, this hat brings you 50% SW skill damage at +0 ! Beware, in MH2 this hat only gives +15% damage !
 Illusion Hot-blooded Headband [1] Top Illusion of Teddy Bear A strong endgame hat that stands tall and high even on critical builds thanks to its bonuses. If you aren't lacking in critical hit, this hat provides a ton of bonuses based on the refine of the hat : +10% damage against against wind, water, earth and neutral monsters at +7, +15% damage against small and large monsters at +9. It can also be enchanted, the most recommended enchant for us is the Powerful Nive which, depending on its level, gives a bonus of STR at a specific refine and an all races% bonus at a higher refine.
 Old Rune Circlet [1] Top Tomb of the Fallen Currently one of the strongest hats for its special enchant, but also hard to get. On the Critical build, you'll want the Acute enchantment, which gives Crit+3 and Critical Damage+10% every level.
 Temporal Circlet (Rune Knight) [1] Top Glast Heim Challenge Mode A new option that tops off the Bio hat, as you can get Acute at the same time as a Temporal Jewel Luk enchant which gives critical damage, critical rate and ATK% based on the hat's refine.
 Goral Crown [1] Top Goral Crown One of the latest hats pre-4th classes, it offers a pretty good boost at high refine without the need to invest into an annoying RNG enchant system, which is a huge advantage for me. If you are playing with a Vernan, you'll also benefit from 10% ACD with the hat combo and a big Sonic Wave boost per refine. Definitely a must-have if you're playing with a Vernan.
 Tiger King Doll Hat-LT [1] Top Master of Coin An improved version of the White Drooping Eddga, this one provides a lot of bonuses even outside of the transformation: +2 STR,DEX,POW,CON and 10% ASPD and damage against Brute monsters by default, +10% ATK through refines, as well as up to 5% ATK, +3 POW and +9 P.ATK through grading. For the transformation part, we get gifted with great boosts: +35 ATK per refine and +20 P.ATK if the hat is refined at least to +10 !
 Wing of Diablo [1] Middle Evil Wing Ears & Spiritual Auger from Nova Shop If you're fine on both critical and ASPD, you can then opt for ATK items. Get these ears alongside an EoE STR 3. You may also go for the Angel Wing Ears if you prefer.
 Fafnir Skin Middle Weakened Fafnir's quest This hat gives +3% Critical chance. Currently a very good combo with the Fafnir Mask, they give together +5% Critical chance as well as +5% Critical damage (as a combo).
 New Wave Sunglasses Middle New Wave Sunglasses One of your main sources of ACDr, it is a pretty good midgame equipment as it contributes a whooping 10% ACD reduction.
 Magical Booster [1] Middle Magical Booster quest This hat allows us to get good bonuses such as critical rate, raw ATK and ATK%, while having an available card slot. As a Critical RK, you'll want to get critical rate (or raw ATK if you already got too much critical rate) and ATK%.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD%, but what interests us the most is the enchant part since we can get up to 6 critical rate through that, while keeping a card slot.
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good budget option as it directly increases your physical damage by 1%.
 Fafnir Mask Lower Weakened Fafnir's quest It gives +2% Critical chance and combos with the Fafnir Skin shown before.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin. Going for that hat as well as a GSS full of STR will give you a good increase in damage, resilience and attack speed. It's a nice budget alternative.
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest This is pretty interesting as a lower hat for its all stats and ATK bonuses.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, giving +2 all stats instead of all the other bonuses.
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory A rare lower hat which only works when in combo with the Fallen Warrior Manteau. It brings effects similar to the Heroic Backpack, bringing us ATK, ASPD and critical damage based on our stat investment.
 Golden Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Ranged damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Phylla Card Card Phylla Before the Bio5 update I used this to get past the 100 critical cap as it procs often enough with high ASPD (Vanberk is not worth it as the chance is too low, here it's ok to get a smaller bonus since we already have critical from everywhere else). Stacking 2 Phylla cards will make it proc quite often.
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you should go for an EoE STR 3.
 Angra Mantis Card Card Angra Mantis It only gives 3% critical damage since we're not a Thief class, but you'll want to put this in case you get the Chaotic Killer Mantis Card for a bonus 5% critical damage.
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A very good ATK hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus but considering our build is not concerned by HP, you shouldn't bother and just put an offensive card on the shoes.
 Deep Sea King Dramoh Card Card Deep Sea King Dramoh This card is able to overcome the Purple Ferus Card thanks to its combo with Deep Sea Merman Card (check out the shoes section to learn more about it). The card by itself though brings just a bit of ATK% based on the refine of your hat, so if you don't plan on using the combo set, it is recommended to stay on the Purple Ferus Card as it's better in that case. Also in case you were worried about your health pool, there's another combo with the normal King Dramoh Card that brings +15% HP, effectively canceling the con of that card and bringing at the same time 10% more HP.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Excellion Suit Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from the instances Charleston Crisis and King's Heels This used to be a very good armor you could get for offensive purposes, as you can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki. This armor is great if you have a weapon with low ATK. It is now outmatched by the Lava Leather Suit, but if you're trying to get a budget build, the excellion might be interesting for you.
 Lava Leather Suit [1] Magma Dungeon F3 A new challenger for our old armors ! This armor increases your ATK by a lot, and if you manage to get it +9, you'll even benefit from its neat critical damage bonus. It provides more ATK when it's +7 than a +7 Excellion Suit with STR ATK ATK blueprints.
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the LLSuit and the YSF01 Plate thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants at least, and if you wanna use that armor on other classes like SS Ranger or WC RK, you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Luk Soutane [1] Odin's Past The Luk Soutane is an interesting choice in case you're going to MH2, as you need a gigantic amount of critical rate, and this armor gives us a ton of it : we get critical rate, damage and LUK per refine. At +12 the armor gives +18 Crit rate, +20 LUK which gives also +6 Crit rate, and 24% Critical damage. The special Luk enchant gives us +10 LUK, +15% Crit damage, +10 Crit rate and +12% DMG against all sizes. So in total you get : +37 Critical rate, 39% Critical damage and +12% against all sizes. The only downside of this armor is the lack of ATK bonuses, so it's really a compromise you need to decide on.
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it very strong for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races.
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new armor that comes with 17.2, it has modules like the Illusion equipments in 17.1, except there are Skill modules. Amongst them is the most expensive (as of writing this) module which is the  Automatic Module (Wave Break). This module boosts the damage of both Sonic Wave and Ignition Break like other damage spell modules, but the reason for its huge price is the fact that it reduces IB's cooldown by 0.25s. I'd recommend staying off from that enchant for now except if you have a huge budget or plan on farming for it, as the damage upgrade is not worth killing your purse because of the expensive IB part of the module. If you go for it nonetheless, you'll want to put on the third slot either a  Automatic Module (Range Force) or a  Automatic Module (Critical Force) to further boost your damage, or a  Automatic Module (Delay After Skill). The other, more appropriate budget-wise option, is putting  Automatic Module (Power) mods.
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. We will go for the Wolf Orb (Hundred Wave) module for a cool +60% bonus on Sonic Wave. The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the big amount of ATK, ATK% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF, a possible budget choice. It emphasizes again on the all-out strategy where you don't care about your defense.
 Bathory Card Bathory If you play in a lot of content with Shadow property attacks, you'll take a liking to the Bathory card. Don't forget that under Berserk, you have 0 MDEF, so magic attacks will hurt like a truck. If you can get yourself resilient to them, then your life will be much easier.
Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible ! Very useful when you play in content where you get often your stuff broken.
Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric I wouldn't usually put this kind of card in the armor, but if you have enough critical rate and damage and you're mostly trying to be more tanky, I'd go for that card in combo with the Raydric Card for that amazing total 30% neutral resistance, as well as that neat 10% ATK.
Furious Ninetail Card Angry Nine Tail A new addition to the Critical RK build, and currently the It gives +5% Critical chance, +10% Critical damage and another +10% Critical chance if your armor is +10 or more.
Dame of Sentinel Card Observation This card by itself does not do much aside from giving us a bit more DEX for instant cast, but it's an important part for a combo with of the strongest garment cards for us (Empathizer).
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Crimson Spear [2] Stem Worm or Naga One of the famous crimson weapons. The base ATK is low but it'll get much stronger thanks to the special ATK bonus that increases each time you refine it, up to +15. The reason why you would want to go for this weapon is either because you have one with a good elemental advantage (Fire and Holy are great) and refined +7 or more, either it's simply refined past +10 and you wish to make use of it (even if it has a useless element like Poison) because you want to play more defensively with a racial/elemental carded shield that will keep you alive. The fact that it's a spear also synergizes well if you're using a mount for the 100% size on all sizes.
 Royal Knight's Broadsword [2] Abyss Glast Heim This new addition to the two-handed swords roster is a pretty good rival to Lindy Hop, and will surpass Vicious Mind in terms of ATK. Unlike this last one who needs a special enchant in order to be unbreakable by itself, this one just needs to be refined to +9 for that. The Broadsword will get enchants later, which might make it worthwhile. Despite its strong bonuses, it has the same problem as the other weapons that the Lindy Hop doesn't suffer from, it's the lack of ASPD, which means you have to compensate in stats or other equipments for that.
 Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Great Demon Baphomet in Sealed Shrine This early weapon more commonly known as the TGL is interesting solo-wise, because you benefit from 20% ACD reduction and 20% SP cost reduction. You may also enchant it for bonus ATK (Fighting Spirit).
 Illusion Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Illusion of Labyrinth The illusion version of its counterpart, it's very similar but mostly is about buffing DB builds, the only interesting part for us is that we can get a supplementary 5% ACD reduction on it with the enchants; if you don't need these last 5%, don't bother getting the illusion version and stay on the normal one which gives overall more ATK thanks to its proc effect and the Malangdo enchants.
 Lindy Hop [2] Stefan or Immortal Cursed Knight Prior to the arrival of the Claw Sword, it was the wet dream of each Rune Knight. This weapon used to be the most endgame two-handed sword we could get, and had the right to stay at the n1 spot as a weapon for RKs thanks to all the pros it has. It has the most ATK out of all 2HS, has 2 slots, gives ATK% and ASPD% bonuses based on the refine, is indestructible (goodbye Golem Card), and is enchantable twice (Malangdo Enchant. Getting a Lindy past +10 used to be every main Crit RK's goal (You can settle for a +8 if you find it too hard or too expensive to go further in the refine hell). You'll want to get Sharp enchants on this one, except if you're already set crit-wise, in that case you may go for Expert Archer enchants.
 Guardian Knight Claymore [2] Glast Heim Challenge Mode A weapon that came out with the late update of Challenge Glast Heim, this weapon is like its update, kind of outdated. It still is decent if properly refined though, and is kind of a more racial hunting oriented version of the Lindy, for Undead and Angel monsters. If you have many Temporal Fragments taking the dust and you're looking for a potential budget option, this may be interesting for you.
 Claw Sword [2] Einbech Mine 3 The new contender that surpasses Lindy, ladies and gentlemen, here is the ultra expensive Claw Sword ! Comes with +15% ATK and +5 crit by default, has a beautiful 300 weapon ATK (40 lower than Lindy Hop but who cares) and gets huge damage increase on refine stages ! Including an non-exhaustive list of : +25% critical dmg, chance to proc +20% DMG to all sizes for a duration, and +7 crit ! You can also enchant it and go for ATK% or crit dmg% or physical damage against a specific type of monster, or even DEF ignore% !
 Vernan [2] Bioresearch Laboratory This two-handed sword is the new best-in-slot weapon damage-wise for Sonic Wave because it decreases its CD by 1.5 seconds and increasing its damage by 30%, resulting in a super fast spam ! It can also be enchanted with Sharp or Expert Archer, and Seyren's Memory which adds more damage to the skill.
 Abysmal Knight Card Abysmal Knight A very cheap weapon card choice for MvP hunting, that does not lose to the other cards thanks to its powerful 25% modifier against boss protocol monsters.
 The Paper Card The Paper It does the same effect as Aunoe Card (shown below) but it drains 1 SP whenever you attack.
 Aunoe Card Aunoe You might want to use this one if you can find it cheaper than WK card. It's not as good but it's made for critical attacks.
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is one of the most interesting cards for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies (most of the monsters from the game). If you play mace+shield, you'll want to get at least one WK card to combo with the KK card as it transforms your WK increase from 20% to 35%
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer This is a better version of the WK card, that got out with the Abyss Glast Heim dungeon. It gives 30% against Medium & Large by itself, so it's better for two-handed swords since we can't equip KK cards.
 Ominous Assaulter Card Ominous Assaulter This is a new option that opened up with Illusion of Abyss, but only for a two-handed sword build. It increases a bit your critical rate, and a lot your critical damage and your ATK depending on your weapon's refine. It comboes with Ominous Heater for even more critical (both chance and damage). It's pretty good if you lack critical chance somehow.
 Greater Ruba Papilla Card Greater Ruba Papilla The other card that came out with 17.2 for two-handed sword RKs, it boosts heavily critical damage based on the refine of the weapon. Due to the large quantity of critical damage everywhere else on the slots and the other better options available (size, melee), it is highly recommended to forget this card and go for the other choices listed before (it is still listed as a possibility per nature of my guide, built to show the many paths available to you as the reader).
 Greater Research Assistant Bot Card Greater Research Assistant An unusual choice from the 17.2 update, this will only work if you are somehow using a spear, it will give you a quantity of ranged% modifier based on refine.
 Rekenber Senior Guard Card Rekenber Senior Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; just like the GRAB this will only work if you are somehow using a spear and it will give you more ranged% damage based on refine.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades.
