You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK). This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players because of it's 10% DEF pierce bonus. That bonus doesn't work on bosses !
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here.
 Royal Guard Shield [1] Banquet for Heroes This shield is quite rare because nobody bothers trying to get one. It gives you the ability to use Shield Spell Lv 1, which can be used to increase your ATK based on the shield base defense. With this shield it's not extremely good, but why would you refuse a possibly free ATK bonus ? You can always switch after using the ATK buff for another shield (but don't bother with this shield if you aren't looking for any kind of min-maxing, the ATK bonus is not really incredible).
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Alice Card Alice The reason this card is here again, is because as a Critical Rune Knight, you'll probably do a lot of MvPs, and this card will be great for your survival. It's especially good against MvPs with weak monsters or no monsters at all, like in Monster Hunter.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). You'll want to get GSS with full STR enchants; if combined with a Poison Breath hat for the combo and you already have too much critical damage, this set could potentially be better than going for the usual critical garments like a FAW.
 Heroic Backpack [1] Monster Hunter This garment is the most used one, tied with the Giant Snake Skin. It used to be one of the best for DPS characters as it gives a nice increase in damage on the offensive stats (STR, DEX, LUK) as long as you have 90 in the stat associated with the bonus you want, and as long as the bag is refined to +7 or +9. Even up to today, it still is a very good cheap garment as it provides you with ASPD, ranged damage and critical damage.
 Illusion Engine Wing A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice and you'll want to get 2 Critical modules as well as one Fast module. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. It can be as good as a +9 FAW with 3 Fatal3 enchants, but only if you equip a pair of Illusion Leg A to get the +10% Critical damage bonus from the combo, which allows it to reach the same critical damage potential as the FAW. In that case, you'll have a better ASPD as well as a better critical rate than with the Fallen Angel Wings.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This is a good garment, a bit weaker than the HBP in terms of damage since you'll mostly only find it enchanted with either only EA or Fatal enchants, it's only great for buffing only one type of damage.
 Fallen Warrior Manteau [1] Tomb of the Fallen A very good garment that surpasses the other choices only when refined past +10 and comboed with a Vicious Mind Aura. It gives us ATK, ASPD%, Crit damage% and ACD%. It's a very interesting garment for solo play as you'll most likely be looking for ACD.
 Violet Halo [1] Dante's shop One of the most interesting garments for a skill based on both ranged and critical, it scales up very hard depending on its refine, and goes even further beyond thanks to its possible combos with many hats, offering you lots of possibilities depending on your needs, whether it is ACD, critical damage or ranged damage !
 Temporal Agi Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim Here comes our strongest contender of the current times, the Temporal Agi Manteau ! Similar to its brother Str Manteau, it gives critical damage instead of the ATK%, alongside the ATK and the %size. You will want to enchant it with ranged damage for MOAR POWAH BABE !
 Automatic Engine Wing B-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. We still have access to interesting modules like  Automatic Module (Critical) but the new addition that may make you think twice about getting this garment or another is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very welcome %Ranged boost.
 Gray Wolf Muffler [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The muffler is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing B-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a 10% ACDr bonus. While it may not surpass the Str Manteau in both ACD% reduction and damage, it wins in utility (and ultimately damage, you will see why). The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be one good source of damage with the Ranged% it brings. The second slot can be enchanted with Wolf Orb (Critical), which can bring up to +15 Critical Rate and +24% Critical Damage. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Str) on this one.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat If you already have a LOT of Critical Damage bonuses, you could theorically go for more ATK as it's better to keep a balance between Critical Damage and ATK, it will also help a lot for ASPD if you're not going for an overrefined Lindy Hop (Even more helpful if you go for FAW instead of HBP and lack these last points of ASPD).
 Menblatt Card Menblatt A good card which gives +% ranged damage. An interesting choice in case you have already too much critical damage%.
 Petal Card Petal It's another one of the great stat cards; you will get a 24% critical damage bonus since you have 120 LUK and it gives 2% per 10 base LUK. Definitely core on this build.
 Empathizer Card Empathizer Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is pretty strong because at 120 DEX it gives 55% Ranged damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Dame of Sentinel card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Temporal Boots of Luck [1] Old Glast Heim This used to be, and still is a very good pair of boots for critical builds as it gives a whooping 30% critical damage bonus. The enchants are going to define the price of your boots (if you want to buy them instead of crafting them); what you want at least is to get ASPD4 if you're lagging behind on your ASPD, or EA4 for raw damage. After that, pretty much any special enchant works for a RK (except Muscular Endurance and Runaway Magic).
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit.
  • Lucky Day is easier to proc and doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, MATK, P.Dodge.
  • Speed of Light is an exotic but interesting choice since the arrival of MH2, and even more since we got the new Fall of Glast Heim instance with the insignia enchants. SoL allows you to dodge half the hits thanks to the P.Dodge proc (Perfect Dodge is halved in MH2), giving you an easier time tanking there, as well as lowering a bit the stress and burden on your healer.
  • Hawkeye can be quite useful if you're looking for another way to get max ASPD as it gives you +200 DEX so you'll get quite a few ASPD points and a bit of damage. It doesn't have the downside of draining your HPs like Speed of Light.
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type, and when paired with the Illusion Engine Wing A-type you'll get +10% critical damage. The item by itself doesn't have any %critical damage bonus, but it's not a big loss since we already have a ton of that, and it brings an especially strong enchant that you can slot on it, named Overpower. It gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK swords) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds. Once you proc it and as long as you keep attacking, you can be sure it'll never run out as it procs very often.
 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a stronger combo with the Engine Wing, and can get the trinity of legendary enchants, aka  Automatic Module (Overpower),  Automatic Module (Fatal Flash) and  Automatic Module (Firing Shot) modules. Once they all proc, they will surpass all other shoes options.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong. If you are overflowing with critical damage and running Temporal Boots of Luck, you might consider switching to these.
 Unknown STR Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of stat boots that was added with Airship Crash, these give a bit of ATK, HP and SP based on the refine of the boots which ain't crazy for lvl 5 boots. The main attraction comes from the potential proc when dealing damage which will grant a whooping +175 STR for 10 seconds, basically permanent when continuously hitting enemies (kinda like the Illusion & Automatic procs). The STR boost can be increased through grading. While this gives no interesting modifier like the other previous boots, it is simply interesting because of our usual high STR scaling through Weapon ATK with our big weapons.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Firing Shot) to get some Ranged% mod. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
 Matyr Card Matyr A cheap choice that combines survivability (+10% HP) and a tiny +1 AGI bonus, better than nothing.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie This is one of the few offensive cards on the boots card slot, it's only worth it if you refine your boots a lot (something like +9 up to +12).
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ASPD+5% and ATK+3%; if you already got a lot of critical damage increase equipments, you can get this one instead to increase your ATK (remember, you gotta keep the equilibrium between critical damage and ATK, it works kind of the same as the weapon % cards).
 Geffen Bully Card Geffen Bully This used to be a very good min-maxing card if you want to increase your critical damage; it gives 5% Critical damage and 3% ASPD.
 Geffen Gangster Card Geffen Gangster Similar to Geffen Bully but the numbers are reversed.
 Odoric Card Odoric Here we have a card that fits more the ranged bill as it improves your ranged damage by 5% and your ASPD by 3%. It is a mix between Ifodes and Blut Hase, perhaps something you'll be interested in if you're lacking ASPD.
 Blut Hase Card Blut Hase That card is a very good ranged-oriented card you could ever get for boots as it gives +3% ATK as well as +5% ranged damage.
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman That card gives us flat ATK based on STR, and it's the new BiS card for the critical build thanks to its amazing combo with the Deep Sea King Dramoh Card that gives you +15% critical damage.
 Arena Bully Card Geffen Night Arena The revised version of the Geffen Bully card, this one will provide us with +10% Critical damage.
 Arena Arhi Card Geffen Night Arena A nice new addition from the revisited Geffen Tournament instance, this card provides us with +5% damage to all sizes, which can be pretty useful if you're low on size modifiers.
 Arena Blut Hase Card Geffen Night Arena The new updated version of the Blut Hase, this version provides instead 5% ATK and 7% Ranged.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Luk Glove [1] Eclage You will have to take either one or two of these if you're trying to get more than 90 critical chances and you don't have enough money for expensive items. Since you're going to keep 120 LUK for the boots, this accessory will give you +12 Critical; combine it with an Essence of Evil Luk 3, and you'll get at least +16 Critical (1 more point if you get past a Crit cap on your LUK stat) per glove.
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus and a big 10% ASPD bonus.
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament An old alternative you can get, depending on the 2 enchants you have on it. Could go from 40M with bad enchants, to... 1B with godly enchants (2x 8% critical damage enchants). It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it.
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for us Crit RKs, are the Attack Speed and the Fatal modules. It is possible to enchant up to 3 times each accessory, so you can put one ASPD and one Fatal enchant on each of them, providing you a lot of ASPD and critical rate (very useful if you play for example the Royal Knight's Broadsword). The third slot is of course reserved for the Expert Archer module !
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK (this is pretty huge by itself, compared to that the critical insignia is crap with its small 7% critical damage) and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantments for Crit RK are Strong and Flash:
  • Strong : When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%.
  • Flash : When equipped with Speed of Light, increases critical damage by 30%. While not as good as the Strong one (because size modifier is super interesting and critical damage is something we already have a plethora of), it is a great budget choice.
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Fatal) gives us now a nice +10 critical rate instead of the old +4, pretty useful to beat the high critical shield of some enemies; you still want as usual the  Automatic Module (Expert Archer), and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Brilliant Light Ruby Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the two that interest us the most are Fatal and Expert Archer. Depending on the level you obtain those enchants at, you can either have up to +15 Crit rate and +12% Crit damage, or up to 10% Ranged with the EA one. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR if possible.
 Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit These cards are here again because when you get to an endgame level, you'll have found other ways to get critical hits besides using EoE Luk 3 on your accessories, so you can get these to finish your possible lack of ASPD and increase further your ATK.
 Ominous Heater Card Ominous Heater A very interesting choice if you choose to skip the Old Rune Circlet and its Acute enchant, it will help a lot for your critical rate. Please note that the set with Ominous Assaulter doesn't work twice, even with 2x the cards.
 Chaotic Killer Mantis Card Chaotic Killer Mantis A good card for pure critical damage thanks to its combo with Angra Mantis, It gives a big amount of critical damage, but beware you get no critical chance bonus on this one !
 Gigantes Card Gigantes A big flat 40 ATK that is only available on left slot.
 Void Mimic Card Void Mimic A huge critical damage card giving far more than all its peers with a big 15%. The combo would be nice but it means giving up one of the strong garment cards, not recommended.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can put in one of these essences. Usually you'll end up putting an EoE LUK 3 because you need a high critical rate.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 Pretty good if your critical rate is high (around 100-110 is enough to hit most of the time), it's sometimes better or cheaper than some other options (like Gold Scaraba).
 Essence of Evil LUK 3 LUK+4, Critical+4, DEX-4 You'll need this if you're aiming for 100% critical chance (without considering the critical defense of the enemies of course). If you're pretty close to 100 in Critical, you can forget about putting points in DEX as you'll be most of the time doing critical hits, which have perfect hit and aren't affected by your HIT rate (and this also means that the decrease in DEX of the EoE does nothing to you, so it's basically a win-win situation for you). Keep in mind also that Sonic Wave has no cast, so you won't be bothered by having a low DEX.
Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get in shape as it doesn't require any refinement; it provides 4 very interesting bonuses for us which are:
  • A bunch of SW% skill mod based on the shadow weapon refine
  • ASPD% and flat ASPD temporary buff when casting Enchant Blade based on Shadow Shield refine
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness, and most importantly a lot of status reduction for our VCT !
  • +50% DEF Pierce on Normal Monsters : When you get closer to endgame and start entering areas such as Einbech Mine 3, you'll have quite the hard time trying to one shot these monsters, the reason being they have high DEF. 50% pierce is not perfect but it helps a lot !

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears. Also, this DEF pierce does not work on boss protocol monsters so beware !

 Reload Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears One of the important stats and not always easy to fetch, is the After Cast Delay reduction. This set allows us to get 15% more reduction of it, without changing any of our gears, which is a big asset because it allows us to focus more on damage in equipments. You will need to refine the whole set to +9 to benefit from the big ACD% bonus. Don't forget to transform the Reload Shadow Armor into its version 2 to get slightly more ACD reduction as well as some VIT.
 Force Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears Part of the early batch we got with MH2, this set will fill the remaining slots when using an armor/shield/shoes set, just like the Reload set. It'll provide us with a bunch of extra ATK and ATK%, so this is a nice addition considering we don't need DEF pierce.
 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
 Sonic Shadow Set 3-1 Class Sets This set gives us ranged damage as well as Sonic Wave skill mods and DEF pierce based on the refinement it gets. Although the DEF pierce is not 100% it is a nice versatile option, and this set works partially without the gauntlet and thus you could swap it completely (or temporarily for a specific content) for one of the weapon pierce sets mentioned above, or simply get an armor pierce set.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, which will help cover the weaknesses some weapon types have, helping us catch up to spear users with Dragon Training. For the most common weapon being 2HS, it'll raise back up the size penalty on Small and Medium monsters.
 Mammoth Shadow Plate Sub Stat Shadow Gears A very basic but helpful shadow armor, this plate gives +10 Critical rate by default and you'll get up to 5 more upon refining it to the max. This will help you solve some build planning issues with newer gears that do not provide as much crit rate as before, or because of custom content with very high critical shield.
 Blitz Shadow Buckler Sub Stat Shadow Gears Same as above except you get only +5 by default.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 SP Absorb Onyx [G] Onyx Shop If you need to fill the remaining slot in case you went for the Melee or Reload sets, you may get this utility onyx that will help you triggering some SP leech when necessary.
 Ranged Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Chaotic Hunter Fly
  • Middle: Abyssman/Toxious
  • Lower: Deep Sea Swordfish
 This set of stone will boost up your Ranged % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot.
 Reload Onyx Set Onyx Shop An alternative to damage if once again you are lacking ACD for maximum spammability, you may go for this option to get the few remaining % you need.
 Critical Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Contaminated Raydric
  • Middle: Rigid Kaho
  • Lower: Ancient Robot
 This set of stone will boost up your Critical damage modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot although you might want to fill it with the Critical Onyx like explained below. Feel free to go for it if you need the critical rate.
 Critical Onyx [G] Onyx Shop The Critical Onyx is a pretty strong stone by itself already with its 20% Critical damage bonus, but it also brings up a combo with the Critical Amber Set, offering a +10 Critical rate bonus; this is especially useful when you already have your build set up to have enough critical rate but want to discard some gear pieces that were giving a lot of it for example to swap accessories to the Sinful/Brilliant Light ones, since they do not offer any crit rate.
 Guillotine Cross Onyx II [G] Onyx Shop An unusual choice that is available to us is to go for other classes' stones. The most interesting one so far is the second set of Guillotine Cross which offers 15% Critical damage, which doesn't seem all that interesting at first compared to the Critical Onyx; but you can combo it with the Assassin Cross Onyx II [U] for an additional 5% ATK and 15% Critical damage (thus reaching a total of 30% Critical damage with just 2 stones).

Dragon Breath

You feel like RK is not naturally bulky enough ? You want to leave all the job to your dragon while you chill hard ? You wanna take a shower of monsters and still not give a damn ? Then this might be for you !

Stats

Here's an average stat setup for DB that you can use:

  • STR 30+
  • AGI 30+
  • VIT 120
  • INT 120
  • DEX 120
  • LUK 1+

It is interesting to get just a bit of STR to increase your maximum weight for carrying pots and farming. You will want a little bit of AGI for faster animation when getting fairly well geared, this is not a priority at all though. VIT and INT are necessary for the damage of Dragon Breath since it is based on HP and SP. DEX is there of course to reduce heavily the cast time. LUK won't bring much benefit to us, so leave it alone except if you wanna push it to 90ish and get close to Curse immunity, but you probably won't have enough points for that.

Skills

These are the skills we want to pick as DB RK:

Strategy

Dragon Breath by default only has access to Fire and Water elements, but thanks to the update on the runes, you can now get several different elements through them. Dragon Breath (Fire) can become Holy through Turisus, and Shadow with Lux Anima. Dragon Breath Water can become Ghost with Asir, and Neutral with Lux Anima. Please remember that Lux Anima will overwrite both Turisus and Asir, so this is kind of a weakness this rune has for us DB users as sometimes we will be forced to not use it in order to hit some elemental monsters.

One easy path when starting on this build is to heavily stack sources of HP and SP leech, in order to proc them on packs of monsters with the AoE of Dragon Breath; this will allow you to survive even longer on top of your already sky high health pool.

Dragon Breath is a skill with a long ACD of 3 seconds for which we need a reduction of 96% for maximum spam; this is however hindered by the fact that DB has a hard animation delay, which prevents you from spamming faster even with the reduction amount reached. The only counter measure to this is to perform "dancing" (aka animation cancel by moving) or to get swarmed by monsters to get your animation cancelled by their hits.

One more thing to remember: thanks to Dragonic Aura as a Dragon Knight, the 3rd class skill Dragon Breath gets a big boost from POW and P.ATK, so Level 5 weapons have a stronger impact than you might think if you refine them high because of the P.ATK added every refine.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the DB build. Don't forget that you can always take a look again at the General Equipment list, if some items here do not suit you or they are too expensive for you.

Sets
Keep in mind every piece of this set could be used separately if you want, as they are even by themselves fairly strong when refined and enchanted.
Set Way to obtain Notes
 Grace Breath set Eden Academy A fairly new set that is available through a custom beginner content, this practically free set will boost you in many ways : %HP, ACD, Dragon Breath skill mod and also 0.5s FCT reduction. If you have no gears yet, going for this set will help you get more easily into midgame.
 Illusion Goibne set Illusion of Luanda This set was some time ago a staple in both tanking and DB builds, it still works wonderfully today. This will give you everything you want on such a build: ACD, FCT reduction and HP. All these bonuses appear when the set is heavily refined, and you'll absolutely want to enchant each piece of the set with Stamina/Dexterous Nives (Lv2 if possible) to get a huge HP/ranged bonus at +11; it is possible to get two on each piece.
 Illusion Sprint partial set Illusion of Twins The Illusion Sprint combo between the Mail and the 2 accessories (Ring and Glove) is actually a very interesting underdog option. The armor by itself offers 12% ACD and a few VIT points as well as 2 Nive slots (So possibly 2 Stamina Nives Lv2, +14 VIT and +14% MHP or Dexterous Nives if you need some Ranged% and DEX for the cast time), and can be comboed with the 2 accessories for a whooping +15% max HP/SP ! The Illusion Sprint Ring comboes with the Mail for 10% more ACD reduction, and comboes with the Illusion Sprint Glove for 5% more ACDr (the Glove itself giving 3% ACDr). The accessories cannot have Stamina Nives but they can be enchanted with some DEX to help us with cast time reduction. This cheap 3-pieces set will bring you a total of 30% ACD which will help you reaching high amounts of ACDr early on.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Ship Captain Hat [1] Top Nova Shop This hat is an ok budget investment, will give you some % ranged mod which you'll be lacking a lot early on.
 Dark Knight Mask [1] Top Master of Coin An interesting alternative to more typical choices, this hat gives a bit of HP and brings a whooping 15% ACD when refined to +11; making it effectively the hat with the most ACD% reduction source. There is also now a combo with 3 different accessories taking the same slot with Thanatos Tower which will give you 0.5s FCT reduction as well as several other bonuses, so it's a good idea to use the set together.
 Temporal Circlet (Rune Knight) [1] Top Glast Heim Challenge Mode The new core hat for Dragon Breath, this hat heavily boosts it through refines; you can also get a bunch of HP through it thanks to the Temporal Jewel Vit enchant and the Adamantine (which will also stacks you hard on MDEF). Please note that the Temporal Jewel Dex is not a good idea as the ranged damage in it only works for bow users.
 New Wave Sunglasses Middle New Wave Sunglasses One of your main sources of ACDr, it is a pretty good midgame equipment as it contributes a whooping 10% ACD reduction.
 Magical Booster Middle Magical Booster An alternative to the NWS, this one can either provide as much ACD as the slotted NWS or get other offensive enchants.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD% reduction, which we can increase further through enchants.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin. Going for that hat as well as a GSS will give you a good increase in damage, resilience and attack speed. It's a nice budget option.
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest This is pretty interesting as a lower hat for its all stats and ATK bonuses.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, giving +2 all stats instead of all the other bonuses; this version is prefered as it gives more VIT, INT and DEX, which are important stats for us.
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory A rare lower hat which brings us ASPD, ACD and neutral resist based on our stat investment when paired with a Fallen Warrior Manteau.
 Golden Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us 5% Ranged damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Bungisngis Card Card Bungisngis This card will give you a few %HP per refine of your hat; this must go in your top slot.
 Rigid Sky Deleter Card Card Rigid Sky Deleter This one goes well in combo with Bungisngis as it goes up to 10% HP, it's intended to go on the middle slot.
 Melted Poring Card Card Melted Poring A new replacement for both Bungisngis and Rigid Sky Deleter, this card needs no combo and gives 10% HP by itself.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Glorious Suit Glorious Blacksmith This unexpected PvP gear is actually a very nice early budget option for a DB RK as it gives straight out of the box 20% HP. You can buy it with the Valor Badges you get from dailies, so it is basically free.
 Excellion Suit Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from the instances Charleston Crisis and King's Heels This used to be a nice armor for offensive and tankiness purposes, as you can get several refine-based %HP modules on it, as well as get ACD% with the garment combo. Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki.
 Vit Soutane [1] Odin's Past The VIT version of the soutanes, this armor is one of the top contenders for HP increase as long as you refine it and get the proper enchants on it. We will of course want to go for the VIT blessing as it gives us even more health and a bit of %ACD, and try to get double VIT enchants as well (or DEX if you'd prefer to adjust better your stats to get instant cast).
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new armor that comes with 17.2, it has modules like the Illusion equipments in 17.1, except there are Skill modules. The interesting modules for us are the  Automatic Module (Dragonic Breath) and  Automatic Module (Delay After Skill).
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. So we will want to get the Wolf Orb (Dragonic Breath), and then the most interesting enchants for us will be if possible Wolf Orb (Delay after skill) since it brings a lot of ACD% reduction, or otherwise you can go for Wolf Orb (Shooter) for the Ranged% it provides, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be. The last slot will not be able to receive the ACD one so it'll be either Shooter or Physical Defense (or perhaps Magical Defense ?).
Peco Peco Card Peco Peco If you feel like you have not enough HP (even though you're a natural meat bag), you can opt for this neat 10% HP bonus.
 Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, might come in handy.
 Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric This is a tank option if paired with a Raydric Card to stack up on Neutral resist.
 Ominous Solider Card Ominous Solider If you want to go all the way on HP, this is as of 17.2 the best non-MVP card for that purpose in the armor slot up until level 200; you'll also get some decent amount of DEF for more tankiness.
Dame of Sentinel Card Observation This card by itself does not do much aside from giving us a bit more DEX for instant cast, but it's an important part for a combo with of the strongest garment cards for us (Empathizer).
Amitera Card Amitera A new HP% card contender for 4th classes, this one will beat the Ominous Solider by offering up to 20% HP, as long as you're at least level 200.
Weapons
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Thanatos Great Sword [1] Ghost Palace This two-handed sword is really nice for survival because it gives you a chance to regenerate a small part of the damage you do on a attack, including AoE attacks. If you have a Rideword Hat and a Hunter Fly Card in your weapon you'll regenerate lots of HP quite often with this weapon, making it one of the strongest sustain weapons. DB is made for cleaning groups of monsters so this is a very interesting option early on.
 Solar Sword Pharaoh A very unexpected choice not many know about, this junk of a weapon is actually a great artifact thanks to its ability to convert 1% of your physical damage to health, on every attack. For Dragon Breath this is actually incredible as we have a nice AOE that can be spammed fairly well, and with high enough damage and enough monsters you can basically keep your health full at all times. The disadvantages of this weapon are that it drains SP continuously and has not slot to equip cards (thus can't do the 17.2 DB card set); however this is slightly compensated by the fact it can be enchanted twice with ranged mods.
 Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Great Demon Baphomet in Sealed Shrine This early weapon more commonly known as the TGL is interesting solo-wise, because at +9 you benefit from 20% ACD reduction and 20% SP cost reduction. You may also enchant it with Expert Archer for more ranged damage.
 Illusion Tae Goo Lyeon [2] Illusion of Labyrinth The illusion version of the TGL, it's very similar but gives HP and SP%, and buffs DB when comboed with the Illusion Boots ! And we can also get a supplementary 5% ACD reduction on it through the enchants.
 Dragonic Slayer [2] Ancient Hero One of two Ancient Hero weapons made for RK, this one is focused on the DB build. You'll get HP/SP% and DB% skill mods per refine as well as some ACD% reduction, this is a pretty good weapon when heavily refined; but I'd not recommend it considering the price difference compared to an Illusion TGL which will work very fine early on. It'd be wiser to aim for the next upgrades of this weapon, which can be found later in this section. The combo with the boots isn't really worth it.
 Metal Stick [3] Spider Chariot This weapon originally meant for RG, can actually be used as RK and is pretty useful as it is a spear with 3 slots and 15% ACD; it is a fairly balanced weapon and may help you reach that very high ACD reduction cap.
 Pike [4] Wormtail or Caramel A very cheap weapon that actually is used for endgame purposes, since we don't care about ATK on DB, we can make use of cheap and easy to refine weapons with 4 slots to fill with several refine based cards. This setup actually brings out the most damage thanks to the huge amount of ranged; the only weakness of it is that you get no ACD with that weapon.
 Spear [4] Taffy Same as the Pike but is lighter.
 Patent Dragonic Slayer [2] Ancient Hero The upgrade to the Dragonic Slayer, this version gives more HP/SP per refine than its predecessor, and also gives more ACD% reduction in total at +11.
 Dragonic Slayer-LT [2] Item Reform Another upgrade to the Dragonic Slayer and currently the last one, compared to the previous weapon it gives some HP/SP% bonuses by default and offers more DB% skill mod per refine. It also brings a very sweet 15% all size reduction at +9, which synergizes well with the new DK passive Two Hand Defending (it gives some additional size resistance). Since this is a level 5 weapon it has grades, and very interesting ones at grades C and B: %ranged damage is always welcome, the new RES & MRES stats will help you stay alive against future difficult contents, and the bonus size reduction will be a nice addition to DK's bulkiness.
 Hunter Fly Card Hunter Fly If you don't care about doing a ton of damage but you want to survive, then this is the way to go. Hunter Fly Card allows you to regenerate health based on the damage you deal, at a low chance. Hitting more monsters means you're repeating the probability several times, and it ramps up the chance of making the card proc; add this card to a Thanatos Weapon and use a Rideword and you'll notice you get full health in no time while killing monsters, basically making you unstoppable machine that does not need a support or potions.
 Archer Skeleton Card Archer Skeleton A very classic and straightforward card, this will give you 10% Ranged damage, one of the few modifiers you can get to increase DB's damage.
 Enchanted Archer Skeleton Card Enchanted Archer Skeleton This is slightly stronger than the good old Archer Skel card by 2%, this is fine to get if you have one lying around but otherwise if you want to buy it, beware as the price for this card tends to be very expensive because of its use in a combo for Genetics.
 Greater Ruba Papilla Card Greater Ruba Papilla This card is part of the 17.2 DB RK card set, while completely useless by itself because of its critical bonuses, it helps complete a set that will heavily boost DB's damage so it is very interesting to get.
 Greater Research Assistant Bot Card Greater Research Assistant Also coming from the 17.2 update, this will only work if you are using a spear, it will give you a big quantity of ranged% modifier based on refine.
 Rekenber Senior Guard Card Rekenber Senior Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; just like the GRAB this will only work if you are somehow using a spear and it will give you more ranged% damage based on refine.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Royal Guard Shield [1] Banquet for Heroes This shield is quite rare because nobody bothers trying to get one. It gives you the ability to use Shield Spell Lv 1, which gives you a %max HP regen regularly; this is kinda neat to get because your damage on DB depends partly on current HP, so a free buff that helps regen it to the max is not a bad idea to get.
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here. You'll be able to get a nice ACD bonus as well as the possibility to get more ACD through the special Purified enchant.
 Illusion Silver Guard [1] Illusion of Twins The newest option currently, the refines on it will help us reach high ACD% amounts and the illusion enchants will help get more tankiness with Stamina Nives, or it is possible too to get Dexterous Nives for more damage and more DEX (for instant cast).
 Andre Egg card Ant Egg A very basic and cheap card for a little %HP bonus, doesn't hurt if you don't have anything else since it boosts your tankiness as well as your damage.
 Gaster card Gaster If you plan on benefitting that means you'll be facing 90% of the time normal monsters. Gaster Card is perfect for that, since it reduces the damage of ALL the non-boss type monsters by 25%.
 Alice Card Alice The opposite of the Gaster card, useful for places with lots of boss protocol monsters. You might want to keep different shields to swap depending on the area you venture in.
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is a pretty versatile card that gets even better if you play it together with White Knight for the combo, may be useful if you wish to stack on size resist.
 Diligent Andre card Diligent Andre A card from Illusion of Twins which interests us because it offers HP% per refine, which will be mostly useful for minmaxing damage but you'll lose in tankiness against non-Insect monsters.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can rise if it's a perfect one stat only GSS. You'll want to get GSS with full STR enchants; if combined with a Poison Breath hat for the combo it will provide lots of interesting bonuses.
 Illusion Engine Wing B-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice; you'll want to get 2 Fast modules as well as one Above All module. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This is an OK garment with ranged enchants, but it doesn't provide any HP or SP and you'll need it +9 to get the possibility of having 3 ranged enchants; this is nice to use if you got one already made lying around, but I wouldn't recommend trying to craft one from clean nowadays.
 Fallen Warrior Manteau [1] Tomb of the Fallen A very good and versatile garment that's only good when comboed with a Vicious Mind Aura. It gives us Neutral resist%, ASPD% and ACD% with the combo. It's a very interesting garment for solo play as you'll most likely be looking for ACD.
 Automatic Engine Wing B-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. You'll want to go for the  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings more %Ranged boost. The remaining slots can be filled with anything you desire.
 Gray Wolf Muffler [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The muffler is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing B-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a 10% ACDr bonus. The enchant slots are different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be our main enchant source of damage upgrade with the Ranged% it brings. The second slot can be enchanted with the Wolf Orb (Speed) which will help out with our usually abysmal ASPD. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, you might want to go for Wolf Orb (Vit) or (Dex) on this one.
 Jejeling Card Jejeling This cheap card provides a lot of HP based on your VIT, fairly good if you plan on sharing the garment it's socketed on with something like a tank/devo character.
 Ancient Stalactic Golem Card Ancient Stalactic Golem A card oriented for bulkiness without forgetting the necessities of DB RK, it'll provide you with HP, ASPD% and ACD% based on your VIT.
 Menblatt Card Menblatt An old card that scales with DEX for % ranged damage, fairly good as a single card.
 Empathizer Card Empathizer Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is pretty strong because at 120 DEX it gives 55% Ranged damage increase, so far more than a Menblatt ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Dame of Sentinel card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Variant Shoes Beelzebub These boots used to be expensive in Pre-Renewal but not anymore, since most players prefer using the "new" Temporal Boots from Old Glast Heim. I suggest getting them from the market, because killing Beelzebub is difficult. They give a big 20% increase in both HP and SP but beware, don't upgrade them or you'll lose % bonuses per refine made on the shoes. For a beginner DB player without much money, this is a pretty huge boon that I encourage you to get !
 Temporal Boots of Dex [1] Old Glast Heim This is an old pair of boots that still holds its ground today, thanks to the potential the enchants have. You will want EA4 for raw damage, and for special enchant Muscular Endurance as it will give a huuuuge 200 VIT bonus when getting hit sometimes, heavily amplifying your DB damage if you heal quickly your health to your temporary new max HP.
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new pair of boots sports special enchants weaker but similar to temporal boots, however they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces so feel free to combo it with an Engine Wing B for more % ranged mod. You'll want to get either  Modification Module (Firing Shot) or  Modification Module (Unlimited Vital) enchanted on it alongside  Modification Module (Fixed Casting).
 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a stronger combo with the Engine Wing, and can get several legendary enchants, so feel free to pick the automatic versions of the 3 recommended enchants of the Illusion Leg (Firing Shot, Unlimited Vital and Fixed Casting).
 Unknown VIT Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of boots which gives HP and SP per refine rate, its main advantage is that it allows you to gain +175 VIT kinda similarly to Muscular Endurance with Temporal Boots, except this time it's when you are dealing damage. This means that you can keep this up and bulk up your damage without the need to get hit, thus potentially keep it up all day if you're quick enough when grinding. It also gives you a bit of ACD% reduction which is neat. The big issue with those boots as you may have noticed, is that it does not provide any FCT reduction. You will have to find the 0.5s elsewhere, there are a few options that can take care of that (The easiest and smallest one being the Casting Onyx costume enchant).
 Hero Boots-LT [1] Item Reform The last version of the Hero Boots which comboes with the LT weapons, this is mostly interesting if you consider you'll not get hit because of how you play, and thus will not manage to proc things like Muscular Endurance (Temporal Boots). These boots give us HP&SP both flat and percentage per refine, and will also take care of the FCT and a tiny bit of the ACD.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Firing Shot) to help with cast time and get some Ranged% as well. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants, so we will go for the FCT one since Wolf Orb (Physical Force) only provides Size%, except if you plan on focusing on Dragonic Breath later down the road. The last slot is actually pretty important for us for once, we want to go for Wolf Orb (Robust) as it provides both great amounts of HP&SP, and it will in most builds boost the damage more than Vital or Mental.
 Matyr Card Matyr A cheap choice that combines survivability (+10% HP) and a tiny +1 AGI bonus, better than nothing.
 Green Ferus Card Green Ferus The usual easy-to-get card that gives you a nice +10% HP buff like Matyr but gives 1 VIT instead, better for us.
 Verit Card Verit Easy to obtain, it's fairly good for a Dragon Breath build as it increases both your HP and your SP by 8%.
 Verporta Card Verporta One of the 3 cards of the 17.2 DB RK card set making it pretty alluring for us, this card is one of the best by itself because of its huge 10% HP and SP bonuses.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Sheriff's Left Badge Rock Ridge's main quest For what it does, this accessory is pretty strong. It increases your HP by 1000 and your ranged damage by 3% if you leveled up your stats to at least 90. (respectively VIT and DEX). To get it, you only need to do the main quest of Rock Ridge (Fistful of Zeny), which is mostly speaking to NPCs and you only need to be level 100 to do it.
 Sarah's Left Earring

 Sarah's Right Earring

Sarah and Fenrir Another slot-less accessory which is quite popular because it's a very affordable spam-enabler accessory since you can reach up to 10% ACD reduction and I highly recommend getting the perfect enchant as it's not very hard. The right accessory comes with the Teleport skill which will be useful to you if you plan on farming with DB.
 Expert Ring [1] Ragged Zombie or Prison Breaker An alternative to Sarah Earrings, that gives half the performance but allows you to put a card on the accessory. The only downside is the SP consumption increase. You may also enchant it for some ranged damage through an EA enchantment.
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The Illusion Boosters are fairly good budget choices nowadays because you can get at the same time enchanted on them a ranged mod (Expert Archer), ASPD mod (Attack Speed) and HP/SP leech mod (Drain Life/Soul).
 Royal Guard Ring [1] Friday This is a pretty affordable accessory that will give us all the interesting stats we want : HP/SP% by default, and we can enchant on it some Expert Archer for ranged% mods, as well as a basic stat up to +7, in our case we want DEX or VIT.
 Rigid Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. It can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. In our case since we'll most likely use Muscular Endurance, we can get the paired enchant Rigid which will give us a neat 10% more ACD reduction.
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: you still want as usual the  Automatic Module (Expert Archer),  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) and  Automatic Module (Drain Life)/ Automatic Module (Drain Soul). You may also trade one of these for a VIT module.
 Sinful Topaz Ring [1]

 Sinful Topaz Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, we don't really care about the base bonus (except maybe the ASPD I guess ?), the most important is their enchants; we can get the Regret enchant which depending on its level, can bring us up to +10% HP and SP.
 Brilliant Light Emerald Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Emerald Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update like the sinful but the light version, we can also get the HP/SP enchant the same way, it is instead named Solace.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one that interests us most is Expert Archer. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to +10% Ranged. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for VIT or DEX if possible.
 Broken Cleaner Card Broken Cleaner The last part of the trinity (17.2 RK set), this card brings us both 10% HP and DB skill mod, as well as even more DB skill mod based on the refine of shoes and weapon.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can put in one of these essences.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil DEX 3 DEX + 4 Hit + 8 LUK - 4 It's pretty nice if you want to spam the most possible by reaching Instant Cast with stat reduction.

Feel free to optimize your build with these if you need to reduce the amount of DEX you got in your stats or are lacking.

Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it's easy to get. Without any refine we get access thanks to it, to +10 All Stats and 5% Max HP and SP, a very welcome buff early on for a DB user.
 Reload Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears One of the important stats and not always easy to fetch, is the After Cast Delay reduction. This set allows us to get 15% more reduction of it, without changing any of our gears, which is a big asset because it allows us to focus more on damage in equipments. You will need to refine the whole set to +9 to benefit from the big ACD% bonus. Don't forget to transform the Reload Shadow Armor into its version 2 to get slightly more ACD reduction as well as some VIT.
 Fire Breath Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets One of two sets meant for boosting Dragon's Breath builds, it will give us based on refine of the pieces all that we need : % Ranged damage, % Max HP&SP and also DB % skill modifier.
 Cold Breath Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets The other set for DB RK, it works exactly the same as the Fire Breath set except this one boosts DB Water, and will provide ACD % reduction instead of HP and SP. These two sets can be used together as they use different shadow gear slots.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.

 Ranged Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Chaotic Hunter Fly
  • Middle: Abyssman/Toxious
  • Lower: Deep Sea Swordfish
 This set of stone will boost up your Ranged % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot.
 Reload Onyx Set Onyx Shop An alternative to damage if once again you are lacking ACD for maximum spammability, you may go for this option to get the few remaining % you need.
 SP Absorb Onyx [G] Onyx Shop If you need to fill the remaining slot in case you went for the Ranged or Reload sets, you may get this utility onyx that will help you triggering some SP leech when necessary.
 Casting Onyx [G] Onyx Shop A great garment onyx which will remove the fixed cast time of Dragon Breath, this will allow us to disregard the usual shoes options that take care of that part.
 Rune Knight Stones I Onyx Shop This is one of the two class sets made for RK, which directly boosts the DB build; we get 20% DB skill mod from it as well as 5% ACD reduction so it's a pretty good option for us.

Hundred Spear

The most thematic spear build of Rune Knight, this lightning fast AOE ranged attack is a great tool for farming packs of monsters. Currently WIP !

Stats

Here are the stats for Hundred Spear :

  • STR 120
  • AGI 90~
  • VIT 90+
  • INT 50+
  • DEX 120
  • LUK 90~

We're of course putting 120 STR in this build because it relies heavily on ATK. Only around 90 AGI because of the big cooldown this skill has, even with the gear reductions. The 90 VIT is there to help build up your natural HP pool, help eliminate the stun possibility. We mostly increase INT to have a bigger SP pool, considering the casting time of HS is extremely low by default. We got 120 DEX to reduce further the cast time and most importantly build up our HIT rate. LUK will also help us get more HIT rate.


Skills

Since this is a spear-only build, it is highly recommended that you take Dragon Training and get a mount so that you do not suffer from size penalty. Do not forget also to level up Spiral Pierce as its level is part of the formula of Hundred Spear. You'll want also to level up Charging Pierce for the occasional boosted damage every 11th attack, and Dragonic Breath since it allows you to build up AP, eventually to be able to cast Dragonic Aura which boosts temporarily Hundred Spear.

Strategy

Hundred Spear is a skill with 0.5s ACD, but it is not necessary to reduce it because at the time of writing this, there is no gear combination that allows players to drop the CD of Hundred Spear from 3s to below 0.5s. However if you feel like maximizing your damage output then maybe you can mix up some another skill (Spiral Pierce ? Dragonic Breath ?) during the cooldown of HS, and get some ACD % reduction.

Equipment

List of the key pieces of equipment recommended for the Hundred Spear build.

Sets
Set Way to obtain Notes
 Ur's set *Armor dropped by Khalitzburg
  • Accessory dropped by Vanberk and Isilla
  • Greaves and Manteau : Mora Equipment
 The Ur set is one of two Mora sets for RK, that is made mainly for Hundred Spear. If you complete the set it'll provide you with +50% damage with Hundred Spear, at least +14% MHP (+1% every refine of the armor), 15% resist to Neutral attacks and will allow you to use Auto Guard level 1.
 Illusion Sprint set Illusion of Twins The Illusion Sprint combo between the Mail and the 2 accessories (Ring and Glove) is actually a very interesting underdog option. The armor by itself offers 12% ACD and a few VIT points as well as 2 Nive slots on which you can put Powerful Nives for up to +14% damage to all races, and can be comboed with the 2 accessories for a whooping +15% max HP/SP ! The Illusion Sprint Ring comboes with the Mail for 10% more ACD reduction, and comboes with the Illusion Sprint Glove for 5% more ACDr (the Glove itself giving 3% ACDr). The accessories cannot have Nives but they can be enchanted with some stats; this cheap 3-pieces set will bring you a total of 30% ACD which will help you reaching high amounts of ACDr early on. You can then combo these pieces with the Shoes as well, which will bring a lot to the table as well: +10% ATK, +70 ATK, +25% damage against bosses when comboing the Mail and the Shoes, then with the Shoes and the accessories you will get some on-hit chances to gain the gigantic +150 STR and +150 AGI buffs ! Beweare though, the combo of the shoes with the accessories will continuously drain your HP and SP, so you might want to have some swap equipment to avoid losing HP&SP when not fighting, and bring some leech effects if you plan on using this combo so you can regenerate in the middle of the fight. Feel free as well to swap the Powerful Nives on armor and shoes for Dexterous Nives if you have some issues with Cast Time.
Headgears
Item Type Way to obtain Notes
 Rideword's Hat [1] Top Custom Headgear Quests This is a really strong hat as it gives you a chance to convert your damage as HP and/or SP. It might be necessary to fight the SP consumption of Spiral Pierce.
 White Drooping Eddga [1] Top Master of Coin This hat is very refine dependant because it relies on a transformation proc to provide you with +25 ATK per refine of your hat. It can be interesting if you already have it on hand or got too much of skill modifiers.
 Temporal Circlet (Rune Knight) [1] Top Glast Heim Challenge Mode A potential option if you're reusing it or have too much skill modifier, you can get Master Archer/Mettle at the same time as a Temporal Jewel Str enchant which gives flat ATK, hit rate and ATK% based on the hat's refine.
 Old Rune Circlet [1] Top Tomb of the Fallen Currently one of the strongest hats for its refine bonuses and enchants. Every 2 refines, you have +15% damage on Hundred Spears. For HS, you'll want the Master Archer enchantment for its %ranged damage, or Mettle which gives ATK+3% and HIT+3 every level; it could help a lot in case you're trying to hit high FLEE enemies.
 Goral Crown [1] Top Goral Crown One of the latest hats pre-4th classes, it offers a pretty good boost at high refine without the need to invest into an annoying RNG enchant system. If you are playing with an Argen Blanco, you'll get 0.5s more CD reduction, and +10% skill mods every refine of the weapon.
 Tiger King Doll Hat-LT [1] Top Master of Coin An improved version of the White Drooping Eddga, this one provides a lot of bonuses even outside of the transformation: +2 STR,DEX,POW,CON and 10% ASPD and damage against Brute monsters by default, up to +10% ATK through refines, as well as up to 5% ATK, +3 POW and +9 P.ATK through grading. For the transformation part, we get gifted with amazing boosts: +35 ATK per refine and +20 P.ATK if the hat is refined at least to +10 ! It's more of a raw ATK hat that is not really tailored for our build, but it provides a lot of damage steroid by itself when it triggers.
 Angel Spirit Middle Nova Shop ATK and MATK+2%, STR+2. Similar to Ancient Gold Ornament, it's great if you want to keep increasing your ATK; but you won't have a slot on this hat.
 New Wave Sunglasses Middle Custom Headgear Quests The current middle hat trend for skill-spam builds. Its 10% ACD bonus is awesome for the slot it occupies, and should be fairly affordable these days if you wish to build some ACD% reduction.
 Victory Wing Ears [1] Middle Ancient Juperos A hat which can be found in the custom episode Ancient Juperos, it brings us by default some ATK and a bit of ACD% reduction, which we can increase even more through enchants while keeping a card slot.
 Samurai Mask Lower Nova Shop Samurai Mask is a good budget choice thanks to its +1% physical damage bonus. If you're looking for something cheaper, go for a Bandit Scarf.
 Well-chewed Pencil Lower Nova Shop A very good choice as it is quite cheap, and actually gives you a good stat bonus for a lower hat (DEX+2), as well as HIT to help you clear these pesky and agile enemies.
 Poison Breath Lower Custom Headgear Quests A pretty nice middle budget hat that only works when used in pair with a Giant Snake Skin.
 Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest This pretty interesting all-stats lower hat can be obtained by doing a small but rewarding quest.
 Magical Rosary In Mouth Lower Rosary In Mouth quest and Headgear Awakening The awakened version of the Rosary In Mouth, which is in our case more interesting thanks to the +2 all stats bonus it gives instead of +1 for our Instant Cast goal.
 Vicious Mind Aura Lower Bioresearch Laboratory One of the strongest hats to get ACD reduction when in combo with the Fallen Warrior Manteau: the main reason behind it, is the great amount of ACD reduction it gives based on your VIT. You get 4% every 30 VIT base points.
 Golden Artifact Lower Ancient Laboratory One of two rare lower headgears that can be crafted from Ancient Laboratory, this is a straightforward damage option which gives us +5% Ranged damage, which is fairly strong for a lower hat.
 Furious Hero Card Card Deranged Adventurer This new card seems like a valid choice in case you already got a sky high ATK, otherwise you should go for an EoE DEX or STR 3.
 Purple Ferus Card Card Purple Ferus A new hat card slot option, it gives raw ATK% as well as an amount based on the refine of your hat. The only downside is the HP/SP penalty, which can be solved with the combo with the Gold Acidus.
Armors
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Excellion Suit Craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis This used to be one of the best budget armors you can get for offensive purposes, as you can get big ATK bonuses with a combination of enchants on it (STR, ATK, ATK) and it gives you ACD reduction. Going for the Unfrozen blueprint might be nice too to prevent mistakes (monsters who cast Frost Diver for example ?). Check out the Verus Equipment Exchange page of the wiki.
 Lava Leather Suit [1] Magma Dungeon F3 An old armor which gives a lot of flat ATK, it is pretty much the physical version of the Flattery Robe once you get it +7, since it gives +150 ATK at this refine (only +100 before +7).
 Lava Leather Armor [1] Magma Dungeon F3 A more defensive choice compared to the LLSuit shown before, instead of getting +50 ATK at +7, you get a +100 DEF bonus. A possibility to consider and ponder on since RKs have a low DEF without Hagalaz.
 YSF01 Plate [1] Werner Laboratory This bad boy Seyren has allowed us to wear his awesome armor, which will totally power us up ! His plate gives a huge ATK% bonus, based on your STR (if it reaches 125) and the refine of the armor. Definitely top tier for our build, especially with the combo with the manteau that you'll see in the Garments section ! It is now kinda outdated, you can get it for cheap nowadays.
 Illusion Armor A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) This new armor beats hands down the other previous armors thanks to its high ATK bonus that scales with refines, and it can be enchanted up to 3 times, with enchants similar to Excellion. As an RK, you need to get 2 Power enchants at least, and if you wanna use that armor on other classes like SS Ranger, you'll want to put a Delay after skill module for 15% ACD reduction. You have the possibility of combining it with other Illusion gears to combo and get interesting bonuses (shown later).
 Str Soutane [1] Odin's Past One of the new possibilities from the level 200 patch, this armor offers us a lot of STR and ATK% per refine, as well as some neat HP/SP% and ASPD% by default. It also increases damage against angels and demons, which makes it pretty strong for this kind of hunting (pretty interesting for grinding at the actual place you get the armor from, Odin's Temple). If you get it +9, you can enchant it with a special enchant tied to the version of the soutane, which in this case gives us STR, ATK%, DEF, MDEF and damage against all races. In total at +12 with the special enchant you get +33% ATK, +30 STR and +12% DMG against all races. The big downside to it is the lack of ACD.
 Automatic Armor A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new contender from 17.2 ! This armor can be enchanted with a variety of different enchants, the interesting ones for us are:  Automatic Module (Hundred Spiral) for the skill modifiers and CD reduction it provides and  Automatic Module (Delay After Skill) for the ACD it provides just like its Illusion counterpart. You may also go for  Automatic Module (Power) and/or  Automatic Module (Range Force) if you want a more generic armor.
 Illusion Sprint Mail [1] Illusion of Twins Alongside the Sprint Shoes you'll see later in the Shoes section, this armor was released to combo with all the Illusion Sprint parts. In our case it'll be interesting to use if we go for the shoes as you get through the combo everything you would normally find on an Illusion/Automatic armor : ATK, ATK%, Melee/Ranged% and ACD% reduction; and it will also solve the FCT issue through a whooping 0.7s FCT reduction bonus. On top of that you even get damage against bosses, isn't that neat ?
 Gray Wolf Suit [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The new Episode 18 armor, it is similar to the Automatic Armor but stricter on how enchants are done; the skill mods are now only on the 1st slot of enchant, are stronger than 2 Automatic skill modules combined. We will want to get the Wolf Orb (Hundred Wave) which gives +45% skill mods and 0.5s CD reduction. The 2 other slots can be filled with more generic physical damage/tankiness enchants with several levels of strength to them; the most interesting enchants for us will be Wolf Orb (Warrior) for the huge amount of ATK, ATK% and it provides, Wolf Orb (Shooter) for its big quantity of %ranged mods, or Wolf Orb (Physical Defense) because of how crazy the DEF bonus can be.
Porcellio Card Porcellio This card gives +25 ATK and -5 DEF. A super cheap budget choice.
Restless Dead Card Illusion Ghoul or Illusion Zombie It gives only +20 ATK but it makes both your weapon and your armor indestructible, and it's pretty cheap ! Might be interesting if you pick a weapon that can be destroyed and need to use Rhydo.
Hardworking Pitman Card Hardworking Pitman A new and much better choice overall for armor than the old usual cards, this one adds 5% ATK. It also gives +10 HIT, it will contribute towards a tailored HIT stuff for high FLEE monster mobbing.
Contaminated Raydric Card Contaminated Raydric It's the same as the Pitman one but without the HIT part, except it has a combo with the Raydric Card which will make you much tankier : +10% Neutral Resistance (Raydric already gives +20%) and +5% more ATK. The ATK part of the combo is pretty neat because it compensates for the loss of a damage card on the garment slot like Brown Rat Card or Wakwak Card.
Dame of Sentinel Card Observation This card by itself does not do much aside from giving us a bit more DEX for instant cast, but it's an important part for a combo with of the strongest garment cards for us (Empathizer).
