It's one of these very rare 3 slots level 4 weapons, which allows for a great variety of card combinations. It brings a lot of ranged% as well as flat ATK based on refinement, and +10% size modifier against medium and large monsters.
 Illusion Pole Axe [3] Illusion of Abyss This weapon by itself does not provide much offensive capabilities but it reduces the skill's CD by 2 seconds, and if you equip it with Illusion Shoes you'll get +40% skill mods, as well as +40 ATK and +10% ATK.
 Argen Blanco [2] Abyss Glast Heim One of the 3 EDDA weapons for RK, this weapon will shine as well through its combo with the Goral Crown. It provides us with 1.5s CD reduction but no skill mods by itself. However it can be enchanted with the Seyren Memory to get 5% skill mod evey 3 refines, and also a more generic enchant where you'll want to get Expert Archer for more ranged % mod.
 Adulter Fides Lance [2] Villa of Deception A new two-handed spear from Episode 18, just like the Adulter Fides 2HS it's a level 4 weapon with fairly high weapon ATK, ATK per refine and Ranged%, which can be enchanted with some more Ranged% or ACD%. Sadly it lacks the ACD% reduction that the 2HS offers. We can get up to 55% skill mod on this weapon, and 1.5s CD reduction.
 Vivatus Fides Lance [2] Villa of Deception This is the upgraded versions of the Adulter Fides one; they have the same stats and boosts per refine, except this one is a level 5 weapons; this means P.ATK per refine (which is huge) and some pretty neat Grading bonuses. Like the Adulter version, it's possible to enchant it, and if you want your weapon to be versatile, you may want to aim for ACD% reduction or Ranged% enchants.
 White Knight Card Old Glast Heim White Knight is the most interesting card for endgame currently as it increases your damage against medium and large enemies (most of the monsters from the game).
 Contaminated Wanderer Card Contaminated Wanderer The current strongest size modifier card for weapons ! They give 10% more than WK cards, so you should aim for these for an endgame build. If you can use a shield somehow though, you will want to use a WK to combo with the KK card as it is stronger (you can only use the combo once).
 Greater Research Assistant Bot Card Greater Research Assistant Coming from the 17.2 update, this will only work if you are using a spear, it will give you a quantity of ranged% modifier based on refine.
 Rekenber Senior Guard Card Rekenber Senior Guard A card that appeared with the last update on Bioresearch Laboratory; just like the GRAB this will only work if you are using a spear and it will give you more ranged% damage based on refine.
 Gan Ceann Card Gan Ceann This very specific card is an optional choice you may opt for. It only gets to its fullest effect if you do the weapon card combo it offers.
 Brutal Murderer Card Brutal Murderer Same as above except this time for Medium enemies.
Shields
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Mad Bunny [1] Nova Shop This shield is pretty neat as it's more focused on offensive than usual shields, because it gives 5% ATK and MATK; you'll get more bonuses if you manage to refine it to +7 and later but it's quite hard and expensive. In PvM there are 2 other effects otherwise not available, which are a 10% reflect damage and a 10% chance to be able to reflect magic attacks for a few seconds.
 Ultralight Magic Shield [1] Cutie A new shield that appeared with Episode 16.2; this shield is really awesome because it's kind of a jack of all trades. You get ASPD depending on the refine (5% at +0, can go as far as 10% at +9), and a Neutral reduction which works the same way as the ASPD bonus. I consider it as good as the Mad Bunny, but for other purposes; it all depends on your needs (ASPD or more ATK). This shield is outshined by Cursed Knight's Shield on low DEF monsters, but it's a great way to increase your DPS on all high DEF monsters and players.
 Cursed Knight's Shield [1] Nova Shop or Master of Coin The CK's shield is often the BiS, for most builds. It gives a nice 10% ASPD bonus, increases a bit less than Mad Bunny at +0 your ATK and MATK (3% instead of 5%) and you get 7% damage reduction from all properties. If you end up getting a +9, you'll get 1 flat ASPD. We finally got the Purified Knight's Shield update, and all Knight's Shield can be enchanted. If you got lots of Endeavor Coins, you may as well try to transform your shield Knight's Shield into a Purified Knight's Shield and enchant it, all the info you need is compiled here.
 Khalitzburg Knight card Old Glast Heim Khalitzburg Knight is really pretty good if you play it together with White Knight for the combo. It will increase both the offensive and defensive effects of the 2 cards.
Garments
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Giant Snake Skin [1] Faceworm's Nest The Giant Snake Skins can be found in bulk because of the random refine & stat enchants. It can be found for a cheap price in case it's full of random or not really good bonuses, or the price can skyrocket if it's a perfect one stat only GSS (DEX and INT GSSs are the most expensive ones). If you don't have any, you might want to get one of the cheapest for starters. The +10 MDEF is really neat and if you get a pair of Temporal Boots (any of the boots, even the basic ones should work), you'll also get a +15% HP and +5% SP set bonus. You could look for a cheap GSS with a combination of DEX and INT if you want to get easy IC.
 Excellion Wing Possible to craft & enchant in Verus at the 2 tiny robot NPCs, with components you get from Charleston Crisis If you want to go full ATK, you can always pick the wing and put 3 ATK enchants on it; the combo with the Excellion Suit will also increase your survivability with some P.Dodge.
 Heroic Backpack [1] Monster Hunter Although the HBP doesn't give any ACD reduction, it still is a solid choice for the versatility it has : ATK, ASPD and ranged damage bonuses. If you feel like other garments kill too much your ASPD, you may go for this one as it improves your attack speed and your damage overall, so you're not losing too hard on DPS.
 YSF01 Manteau [1] Werner Laboratory Next in the badass set of Seyren, we got the manteau ! Although it requires us having 125 VIT for its big 10% ACD reduction at +0, the fact that we get even more reduction from both the refine of the garment and from the combo with the armor, makes it a very powerful choice. Definitely something you'll want at +9 otherwise the garment is not worth wasting your stat points on it.
 Fallen Angel Wing [1] Monster Hunter 2 This garment has a very good %ranged damage potential with the enchants on it and will beat the Engine Wing from 17.1, but it lacks ACD reduction, so beware of the spammability.
 Illusion Engine Wing B-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new garment from the 17.1 episode Illusion can be enchanted thrice and you'll want to get 2 Fast modules. These enchants' strength depends on the refine of your garment so if you go for this one, you'll need to refine it to at least +7, and +9 if possible. Since it's the B-type, when combined with the A-type armor we'll get 10% ACD so it's pretty strong for us, especially if you don't use a weapon that gives ACD like the TGL.
 Automatic Engine Wing B-Type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The 2.0 version of the old Illusion Engine Wing, it is the same as the old one but with slightly higher stats. We still have access to interesting modules like  Automatic Module (Fast) but the new addition that may make you think twice about getting this garment or another is the new  Automatic Module (Powerful) that brings a very welcome %Ranged boost.
 Temporal Str Manteau [1] Legacy of Glast Heim The STR manteau, as many originally cash shop items, is a very powerful option for all non-crit physical builds. That garment bombs you with raw ATK, refined ATK% and spicy %size modifiers ! You'll want to put ACD% enchant on the garment, or Ranged% if you somehow already got too much ACD%.
 Gray Wolf Muffler [1] Gray Wolf Equipments The muffler is the Episode 18 replacement for the Engine Wing B-Type, as it plays the same function of comboing with the physical armor for a 10% ACDr bonus. While it may not surpass the Str Manteau in both ACD% reduction and damage, it wins in utility (and ultimately damage, you will see why). The enchant slots are very different: on the 1st one we'll want the Wolf Orb (Powerful) which will be our main enchant source of damage upgrade with the Melee% it brings. The second slot (which is the most interesting one I believe) can be enchanted with Wolf Orb (Guide Attack), which can bring up to 24 Perfect Hit rate ! This is extremely important for us as our main counter is very high FLEE which some monsters boast thanks to using the skill Agi Up. Perfect Hit will allow us to hit while ignoring FLEE, much like a Critical hit. Finally, the third slot is a fairly minor boost, it's recommended to go for Wolf Orb (Str) on this one or (Dex) if you need to reduce your cast time.
 Raydric Card Raydric If you think you need more resistance, then feel free to take the Raydric Card ! 20% reduction of the neutral damage coming from the monsters' basic attacks, hell yes.
 Brown Rat Card Brown Rat This gives a nice amount of ATK on garment, as well as a bit of ASPD%. If you feel like you're lacking too much attack speed, you might want to go for that one.
 Menblatt Card Menblatt One of the few cards in garment that give %ranged damage, this is a good cheap option even up to endgame.
 Empathizer Card Empathizer Part of the new Thanatos Tower update, this card is pretty strong because at 120 DEX it gives 55% Ranged damage increase ! Definitely an asset, but be careful because you need a Dame of Sentinel card equipped in your armor to benefit of the biggest part of the card.
Shoes
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Temporal Boots of Dexterity

 Temporal Boots of Strength

Old Glast Heim Either the Strength ones for its ATK and potential combo with the Temporal STR manteau, or the DEX if you need more cast time reduction and % ranged.
  • Bear's Might will give you the biggest damage increase out of all the enchants (+200 STR) but you have to get hit. I kept it here because it's really strong, but keep in mind that if you get too much strong monsters hitting you, yes you'll proc it, but you will also probably die staggered by the mobs.
  • Lucky Day doesn't have any con; you'll get +200 LUK so you'll have a bit more of ATK, HIT, P.Dodge. Probably your safest bet !
  • Hawk eye procs faster than Lucky Day and will increase your ASPD by a few points, but you'll suffer a SP drain
 Illusion Leg A-type [1] Illusion (17.1) That new pair of boots sports special enchants similar to temporal boots but they proc much more often and for a longer time than our old ones. It comboes with other Illusion pieces: you'll get a +5% ATK when paired with the Illusion Armor A-type. It brings 2 strong enchants that will interest us :
    • Overpower which gives +50 STR (which synergizes well with our high weapon ATK weapons) and +15% ATK, when physically attacking and for a whooping duration of 10 seconds
    • Firing Shot which gives +50 DEX and +10% Ranged damage.

While Overpower will usually give you more damage, you need to think about your cast time and your ASPD, which Firing Shot will take care of. Up to you to find the one that fits the most with the equipments you chose !

 Automatic Leg A-type [1] Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Leg, this one comes with a stronger combo with the Engine Wing, as well as the usual  Automatic Module (Overpower) and  Automatic Module (Firing Shot) modules.
 Illusion Sprint Shoes [1] Illusion of Twins A very strong contender that appeared within the Illusion dungeons, these shoes provide us by themselves a +15% increase on all sizes at +11, and then as all illusion gears we can enchant them and go for double Powerful Nives (Try to get Lv 2); through this we will also obtain +14 STR and +14% damage to all Races, which is the other reason they are so strong. You may also go for DEX nives if you need the stats for cast reduction, with lower damage boost.
 Unknown STR Boots [1] Airship Crash A new pair of stat boots that was added with Airship Crash, these give a bit of ATK, HP and SP based on the refine of the boots which ain't crazy for lvl 5 boots. The main attraction comes from the potential proc when dealing damage which will grant a whooping +175 STR for 10 seconds, basically permanent when continuously hitting groups of enemies (kinda like the Illusion & Automatic procs). The STR boost can be increased through grading. While this gives no interesting modifier like the other previous boots, the STR boost is quite phenomenal; I'd recommend checking with a calculator if this would be stronger for you than Illusion Sprint Shoes as usually multiplcative modifiers tend to do better.
 Unknown DEX Boots [1] Airship Crash Another pair of stats boots just like above, this one is an interesting alternative for us because of the huge quantity of DEX it brings, getting that 175 bonus DEX should allow you to clear completely your VCT through stats.
 Gray Wolf Boots [1] Gray Wolf Equipments This is the Ep18 replacement for Automatic Legs, and works slightly differently: you can now only choose one legendary enchant which will be on the first slot of those boots, so you will want Wolf Orb (Firing Shot) to get some DEX to clear cast time and for more HIT, as well as some Ranged%. The second enchant only has FCT, magic damage or physical damage enchants so we will go for the physical one, Wolf Orb (Physical Force), which provides a good amount of the size% modifier (up to +16%). The last slot is negligible, being HP/SP/Heal power... Just try to aim for HP through the Wolf Orbs (Vital) and (Robust) if possible or if your survivability needs a boost.
 Outrageous Cookie Card Outrageous Cookie It's a cheaper choice than Ifodes, the downside is that your HP gets reduced and you don't get that neat ASPD bonus. You can though get a bigger ATK% if your boots are heavily refined.
 White Porcellio Card White Porcellio Another budget choice if you're planning to go cheap, this card gives you some flat ATK, and more if you refine your shoes or combo it with the Porcellio Card.
 Rigid Nightmare Terror Card Rigid Nightmare Terror This card is underestimated and allows you to get 10% ATK for a budget investment by putting a Nightmare Terror Card in your armor. Definitely something to look for if you don't wanna invest in the pricier options down there.
 Ifodes Card Ifodes This card gives ATK+3% and ASPD+5%; a bit expensive but the ATK% increase is great for a footgear card.
 Odoric Card Odoric Here we have a card that fits more the ranged bill as it improves your ranged damage by 5% and your ASPD by 3%. It is a mix between Ifodes and Blut Hase, perhaps something you'll be interested in if you're lacking ASPD.
 Blut Hase Card Blut Hase That card is a pretty good damage-oriented card you could ever get for boots as it gives +3% ATK as well as +5% ranged damage. Its price is also the highest of the non-mvp/miniboss cards, it's usually twice or thrice the price of an Ifodes.
 Deep Sea Merman Card Deep Sea Merman A newer option that appears here actually as a mid-tier choice, it gives you a bunch of ATK depending on your base STR.
 Arena Arhi Card Geffen Night Arena A nice new addition from the revisited Geffen Tournament instance, this card provides us with +5% damage to all sizes, which can be pretty useful if you're low on size modifiers.
 Arena Blut Hase Card Geffen Night Arena The new updated version of the Blut Hase, this version provides instead 5% ATK and 7% Ranged.
Accessories
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Sheriff's Left Badge Rock Ridge's main quest For what it does, this accessory is pretty strong. It suits every build you could play as a RK since it increases your ATK by 3%, your HP by 1000 and your ranged damage by 3% if you leveled up your stats to at least 90. (respectively STR, VIT and DEX). To get it, you only need to do the main quest of Rock Ridge (Fistful of Zeny), which is mostly speaking to NPCs and you only need to be level 100 to do it.
 Pendant of Maelstrom [1] Nightmarish Jitterbug This used to be one of the most offensive-oriented accessories you could get, it has an all stats bonus so another good addition for your cast time ! Get this one if you're playing on a budget build (the price decreased since the GMT update).
 Broken Chip 1 [1]

 Broken Chip 2 [1]

Last Room They used to be a no-brainer back when bragi gave 100% ACD reduction because getting the 2 accessories give you +12 STR and +12 INT, and they're slotted, making them the best accessories for reducing VCT by stats. Now it's a little more delicate as we have to get ACD as well since Bragi got nerfed.
 Bakonawa Agimat Tattoo Festival Tattoos Even though it has no slot, the effects are quite strong: you get a 7% ATK bonus (1% more than PoM) and 10% ASPD. A well-spent investment if the only thing you lack is ASPD.
 Physical Enhancer Ring [1] Geffen Magic Tournament A good accessory which could go from 5M with bad enchants, to... a very high price with godly enchants. It gives by default ATK+5%, and it should be pretty simple to get "correct" enchantments on it, making it a better choice than Pendant of Maelstrom damage-wise. Try to get 2 ATK% enchants on each ring.
 Expert Ring [1] Ragged Zombie or Prison Breaker A very budget choice compared to Sarah Earrings, that gives half the performance but allows you to put a card on the accessory. The only downside is the SP consumption increase.
 Sarah's Left Earring

 Sarah's Right Earring

Sarah and Fenrir Another slot-less accessory which is quite popular because it's a very affordable spam-enabler accessory since you can reach up to 10% ACD reduction and I highly recommend getting the perfect enchant as it's not very hard. It is account-bound so you'll have to make them yourself.
 Illusion Boosters L [1]

 Illusion Boosters R [1]

Illusion (17.1) The new addition of modular accessories from the episode Illusion (17.1), it has the same base stats as a PER but unlike that one, you choose the enchants you put on it. The enchants that will be useful for us, are the ASPD, Expert Archer and the Drain modules.
 Strong Insignia [1] Fall of Glast Heim Released after 17.1, this instance's most interesting piece of gear is an accessory that can be only used on one slot, which is the insignia. The most interesting one for physical classes is the Strong Insignia which gives 10% ATK (this is pretty huge by itself, compared to that the critical insignia is crap with its small 7% critical damage) and can be enchanted for a combo with Temporal Boots special enchants. The most interesting enchantments for Crit RK are Strong and Flash:
  • Strong : When equipped with Bear's Might, increases physical damage against all size enemies by 25%. This is by far the strongest one as it increases the size modifier, which is kinda the rarest modifier you can get.
  • Hawkeye : When equipped with Hawkeye, increases ATK by 10%. It's a more affordable but weaker option compared to the Strong enchant, still might be worthwhile !
 Automatic Booster L [1]

 Automatic Booster R [1]

Automatic Equipments (17.2) The new version of the Illusion Boosters, these come with better versions of the previous modules: the  Automatic Module (Attack Speed) adds 20 ATK now, the  Automatic Module (Expert Archer) has now a HIT bonus which is very welcome for us, and there is a pretty rare and expensive module that boosts all kinds of damage by 5% : the  Automatic Module (All Force).
 Sinful Ruby Ring [1]

 Sinful Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Emerald or Opal versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Dragons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus.
 Brilliant Light Ruby Ring [1]

 Brilliant Light Ruby Necklace [1]

Thanatos Tower I will only put here the Ruby version of those accessories, but you can also go for the Zircon or Aquamarine versions. New accessories coming out of the Thanatos Tower revamp update, they bring out a huge amount of ATK% both by themselves and through their enchants; it is possible to get up to 10% ATK on each, and you can also get a very big racial bonus towards Angels and Demons. You can increase further the racial damage with the pair set bonus. This only gives 0.2 FCT with the combo but if you're running already FCT elsewhere, this won't be an issue for you.
 Gray Wolf Pendant [1]

 Gray Wolf Ring [1]

Gray Wolf Equipments Those Episode 18 accessories are quite the opposite of the other Gray Wolf pieces, in the sense that we get more freedom enchants wise when comparing to Automatic, for a single reason : we can get twice one of the typical enchants like Fighting Spirit/Spell/Expert Archer. And the one which interests us the most is Expert Archer. Depending on the level you obtain it at, you can fetch up to +10% Ranged damage and +20 HIT, so pretty much with 2 accessories with 2 perfect enchants each, that means +40% Ranged and +80 HIT ! This is very helpful in order to solve our troubles trying to hit high FLEE enemies. The third and last enchant will be one of the stats Wolf Orbs, you can try and aim for STR or DEX if possible.
Gold Scaraba Card Gold Scaraba This is the second card that gives the most flat ATK on the accessory slot (Gigantes gives the double).
Revolver Buffalo Bandit Card and Shotgun Buffalo Bandit Card Revolver Buffalo Bandit Shotgun Buffalo Bandit The combo of the 2 Buffalo cards will help improving your ASPD as well as getting a bit more damage with their great +7% ATK and +7 AGI.
 Gigantes Card Gigantes A big flat 40 ATK that is only available on left slot, pretty interesting if your other accessory slot is busy and you can't use the buffalo combo, or you're simply missing one (because you're using a sarah earring for example).
 Sharp Magic Card /  Magic Poisoned Sanare Card /  Sewage Cramp Card /  Sewage Cramp Card /  Sewage Venenum Card 17.2 Cards These new options that came from 17.2 are listed here as possible options to further help on your cast time since they all give a combination of stats that include DEX, and they give a nice %HP boost as well, which will help you survive more.
Essences of Evil

Any slot where you can't get the recommended card or you're not satisfied with it, you can usually put in this essence.

Item Effect Notes
 Essence of Evil STR 3 STR+4, ATK+12, INT-4 It's sometimes better or cheaper than some other options (like Gold Scaraba).
 Essence of Evil DEX 3 DEX + 4 Hit + 8 LUK - 4 It's actually core if you want to spam the most possible by reaching Instant Cast with stat reduction.

Feel free to optimize your build with these if you need to reduce the amount of DEX you got in your stats.

Shadow Gears
I have only introduced here the most commonly picked shadow gears, please not forget there's still a plethora of them that could suit your needs more here.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Rune Knight Class Shadow Set Class Shadow Gear Sets This set was during quite a while the main shadow set we had and it still is fairly easy to get in shape as it doesn't require any refinement; it provides 4 very interesting bonuses for us which are:
  • ASPD% and flat ASPD temporary buff when casting Enchant Blade based on Shadow Shield refine
  • +10 All Stats : Very welcome stats as we get a bit more strength and tankiness, and most importantly a lot of status reduction for our VCT !
  • +50% DEF Pierce on Normal Monsters : When you get closer to endgame and start entering areas such as Einbech Mine 3, you'll have quite the hard time trying to one shot these monsters, the reason being they have high DEF. 50% pierce is not perfect but it helps a lot !

Keep in mind that while the bonus is great, you do not have any space left for other shadow gears. Also, this DEF pierce does not work on boss protocol monsters so beware !

 Reload Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears One of the important stats and not always easy to fetch, is the After Cast Delay reduction. This set allows us to get 15% more reduction of it, without changing any of our gears, which is a big asset because it allows us to focus more on damage in equipments. You will need to refine the whole set to +9 to benefit from the big ACD% bonus. Don't forget to transform the Reload Shadow Armor into its version 2 to get slightly more ACD reduction as well as some VIT.
 Force Shadow Set Sub Stat Shadow Gears Part of the early batch we got with MH2, this set will fill the remaining slots when using an armor/shield/shoes set, just like the Reload set. It'll provide us with a bunch of extra ATK and ATK%, so this is a nice addition if we don't need DEF pierce.
 Penetration Shadow Set Penetration Shadow Gears In case you really need a versatile and stronger DEF Pierce set that works on all kinds of Normal monsters, you may go for this one instead of the previous one; it will allow you to reach up to 80% DEF Pierce on Normal monsters if you refine all pieces to +10. You'll only require then something like Expiatio to reach full pierce on everything (or pick up some specific racial pierce gears to complete the missing pierce amount if you dislike using an alt or playing with a party). The biggest issue with this set is the amount of shadow gears that require refinement, which sometimes require expensive components.
 Single Race Pierce Shadow Set Racial Pierce Shadow Gears Compared to the 2 previous sets, a smaller but more effective set exists, based on the 2 Penetration Shadow accessories. But in this case it comboes with a shadow weapon tied to a specific race, allowing a complete DEF pierce on that race, against both Normal and Boss monsters ! The only prerequisite to getting that bonus is to have the sum of the refines of the 3 pieces to reach 25. Considering you will probably want several racial sets, it is thus recommended to refine the 2 Penetration accesssories to +10 because of their cheap refine cost as older gears, compared to the racial gauntlets that require more expensive, endgame components, and leave that last part only refined to +5.
 Double Race Pierce Weapon Shadow Set Racial Pierce Weapon Shadow Gears Alongside the big Ancient Juperos custom episode came lots of new shadow gears, and part of them are combined versions of the previous single racial pierce gauntlets, which allows you to have one piece doing 2 races at the same time. This could be fairly useful for example in the Thanatos Tower instance (and upper floors 11 and 12) where Demon and Angel monsters roam together.
 Double Race Pierce Armor Shadow Set Racial Pierce Armor Shadow Gears At the same time as the previous shadow gears, a set of Shadow Armors appeared with the same goal in mind of having 2 races fully DEF pierced, this will allow you more flexibility on your shadow gears choices, or even allow you to have full pierce on 4 races at the same time considering this set does not conflict with the weapon one.
 Almighty Shadow Focus

 Almighty Shadow Brooch

Nightmare Toy Factory & Thanatos Tower (Hard) 2 popular shadow gears that actually do not combo together, these will only give bonuses through refines. You get +1 to All Stats every refine of the shadow gear, meaning with both you can reach +20 All Stats. This will help us eliminate the remaining super small casting time of HS, as well as help us with HIT rate and ASPD.
 Liberation Shadow Boots Class Modifiers Shadow Gears These boots give us up to +5% damage against bosses, and it's possible to get +5% more through the combo with the Safeguard Shadow Shield.
 Ancient Shadow Vest Sub Stat Shadow Gears The shadow armor slot is not very generous with damage boost choices, but there are also utility-oriented gears we can look at. This vest is one of them, bringing us up to +20 HIT, which will help us fight against high FLEE targets.
 All Race Shadow Boots Racial Modifiers Shadow Gears A very interesting choice on the shoes slot as Racial modifiers can be sometimes rare, this pair of boots will give us up to +5% damage on all races.
 Perfect Size Shadow Gauntlet Size Modifier Shadow Gears If you have the freedom of choosing this slot separately, this shadow weapon is pretty good because of the size bonus (up to 7%) it brings, this modifier is usually lower than the other ones (especially if you're not using Illu Sprint Shoes nor the Insignia combo anymore) so it's a great option.
 Infinity Shadow Ring

 Infinity Shadow Bracer

Size Modifier Shadow Gears This shadow set allows us to completely ignore size penalty, but this is normally not necessary if you are riding your dragon mount. Only useful for the cool kids who use their legs.
Costume Enchants
And now yet another layer of gears appeared with the Costume Enchants ! It is also a fairly big system that can only grow more with time and content releases, so feel free to head here if you don't find what you want on the guide.
Item Way to obtain Notes
 Ranged Amber Set Field and Dungeon Stones
  • Upper: Chaotic Hunter Fly
  • Middle: Abyssman/Toxious
  • Lower: Deep Sea Swordfish
 This set of stone will boost up your Ranged % modifier by 15%, while retaining a free slot on the garment slot. This is your main damage option.
 Reload Onyx Set Onyx Shop An alternative to damage if once again you are lacking ACD for maximum spammability, you may go for this option to get the few remaining % you need.
 SP Absorb Onyx [G] Onyx Shop If you need to fill the remaining slot in case you went for the Ranged or Reload sets, you may get this utility onyx that will help you triggering some SP leech when necessary.
 Lord Knight Onyx II [U] Onyx Shop One of the three specific costume enchants for us, this one gives % ranged damage based on the learnt level of Spiral Pierce.
 Lord Knight Onyx II [G] Onyx Shop The reason why we would pick this Ignition Break costume stone solely is for its combo with the Lord Knight Onyx II [L] stone, which will offer us +30% damage with Hundred Spear.

Leveling

This is the usual routine I go through when making a new character. I think trying out the instances, if you have the possibility to do so with friends or a guild, is a better way to enjoy the game than simply grinding mindlessly the Gramps maps. Do not switch directly to 3rd class. Please do not forget that going down the rebirth path is required for the Critical build and simply too good to be avoided anyway, here's why.

Lv 1 - Lv 99

The easiest way to level up as a Swordsman/Knight, is to go down the AGI path. Make sure you level first your STR and your DEX to 50, then increase your AGI to 90. When you're finished with AGI, get your DEX to 70 and max your STR and AGI.

  • Lv 1+
    • First thing to do if you haven't done the tutorial: Go kill some Porings in Hidden Dungeon to get Job Lv 10 and switch to Swordsman, then start grinding at Payon Cave. It is advised that you use your Novice Potions here if you got any, because your HP pool is very low at the beginning; Red Potions will do in case you didn't do the tutorial. Since the Renewal update the Zombies are much weaker so kill them first to get a few levels. Once you get around level 10-15, start killing the Skeletons and the other monsters.
  • Lv 26+
    • When you think you're doing fine at Lv 1 of the dungeon and the pace is getting slower, go straight to Lv 2. The skeletons are now much weaker compared to their old self years ago in Pre-Renewal.
  • Lv 45+
    • At this level I usually go to Orc Dungeon and kill groups of Orc Zombies with AoE skills. If you want to grind faster, you may use Fire Elemental Converters since the monsters here are weak against Fire. It'll be also useful later at Glast Heim, where you'll be hunting Evil Druids and Wraiths. If you're between level 50 and 59, you can try the Eden quests for the Orcs if you want to get a free leveling bonus in Orc Dungeon: Go to Eden, talk to Secretary Lime Evenor to register, then you can ask Instructor Boya to test you, you should get the Orc Dungeon quest. Don't forget talk to the Eden Group Member outside of Orc Dungeon before you start hunting Orc Zombies and Orc Skeletons. When you've completed them, report to the Eden Group Member then to Instructor Boya. Since you passed the test, you'll have access to some special equipments for beginners, available by talking to Administrator Michael in the equipment storage room. If there' something you don't understand, you should check out the Eden Group wiki page.
  • Lv 70-79
    • Here we'll keep doing the Eden quests since they give out nice EXP, and you get access to better items: Instructor Ur's Eden Equipment Quest at Glast Heim. I recommend here that you also get the Hunting Board Quests for both Evil Druid and Wraith. This way you kill 2 birds with one stone, or rather you earn twice EXP with one hunt.
Talk to the Eden Group Member outside of Glast Heim Churchyard before you start hunting Wraiths and Evil Druids. Watch out for Mimics there since they're quite nasty and will easily kill you if you aren't prepared. Most players do this quest too while leveling, so do not hesitate to ask other players if they want to team up, it'll make your hunting quest faster and safer. Also do not forget that you have to kill 20 Wraiths first, talk to Johan, then you can kill the Evil Druids. You may then talk to Johan again, then go see Instructor Ur and Administrator Michael to get your rewards.
  • Lv 85+
    • Level 85 is the minimum level required to join the first bracket of the Gramps quests. Gramps quests are usually rotated at the start of every month, so try to end your quest before that. It is highly recommended that you do the Gramps quests whenever you can if you want to level as fast as possible. Once per day is already good enough but if you want to tryhard even further, the cooldown resets after 4 hours once you've turned in the quest (you can still go back in Gramps' map and grind without the quest). You can stay here until level 115 (the other Gramps map) if you want.
  • Lv 99
    • This is where it gets really important: if you want to "skip" the transcendent 2nd leveling phase, you can do a simple trick that consists of doing high-level quests when you're at level 99, and get the experience rewards only after rebirthing to level 1. This is what I usually do :
      • Get level 99 at Gramps 85+, but I do not turn in the two 400-monsters hunting quests.
      • Do Cautious Village and stop before the king's reward (Watch on the link where you get the EXP and stop doing the quest before getting it, where you stop isn't really important).
      • Rebirth, then kill some Porings to switch to High Swordsman.
      • Turn in Cautious Village, you should get around Base Level 70 and Job Level 50, you can then change to Lord Knight.
      • After becoming Lord Knight, go turn in the Gramps quests at Eden, you should be somewhere close to 98/69. You can then finish your levels at Gramps 85+, or go to Rock Ridge and go east to kill the cowboy buffalos; the Shotgun Buffalo gives like triple the job exp of the other monsters, so focusing them will make your last levels faster. You're finally 99/70 ? Congratz ! You can go to the Main Office and become a Rune Knight. Do not worry about your level progression bar not reappearing, it's just a visual bug; you can disconnect and reconnect to make it appear again.
Lv 100+

Once you become a Rune Knight, your primary goal should be to get Wind Cutter as soon as possible, because it's your best early AoE skill with a Peuz set thanks to its amazing set bonus, it will help a TON for leveling. Also, don't forget that you can use Battle Manuals to get a big increase on Eden board quests and Gramps quests.

  • Lv 100
    • At this level I always do the Rock Ridge main quest Fistful of Zeny. It gives enough exp to get your first skill points, you get a free accessory good enough for beginners, and it's pretty easy to do. You may also do the daily quests for quick EXP everyday.
    • Once you finished Rock Ridge, you can start doing the Banquet for Heroes quests. You only need to walk and talk to NPCs until you get to Room of Consciousness. This quest which contain an instance, will be too hard for you even though it's available at lvl 100; you need to ask for help from someone strong enough to solo it on #lfg. Once you've finished these, you may do the Royal Families quests and the dailies if you're still not 115. Another possibility is grinding at the ruins of Juperos, the dungeon is full of Venatus; you can start training your kiting skills here with Ignition Break, as they are quite unforgiving in mob trains since they are so many in there. It is recommended that you stay with the Neutral element as the Venatus have different elemental properties, depending on their color.
  • Lv 115+
    • When you get level 115, you can join the 2nd Gramps map and do the 400 mobs quests again there. If you want to get quickly to the 145+ Gramps tier, try getting an HE Battle Manual as it triples the EXP you earn; it only lasts 15 minutes so try to use it near the end of your 115+ Gramps run.
    • If you're not satisfied with Gramps, you can always go back to Juperos. If the Venatus do not give much EXP anymore, you can try out Rachel Sanctuary with the Vanberks and Isillas. They're easier to kite than Venatus since they're much slower so you shouldn't have too much trouble there. Your only doom here is the Hodremlin, it bites hard; try to avoid it or take more distance between the mob train and yourself so you can have some time to kill the Hodremlin.
  • Lv 145+
    • Level range to join the third bracket of Gramps quests. The third map of Gramps should be pretty fast as there is usually a level max doing the map for one of his characters or friends in the team.
    • You may also join the Charleston Crisis teams who run quite often the instance, to start farming up some items for your stuff (if you plan on getting an Excellion Suit) or to get money, while increasing your levels.
  • Lv 160+
    • At this level, you're pretty close to the max level (175), and you'll be able to join all the instances without prerequisite. Running them is a quick way to get the max level, as well as starting to farm for your items. What I usually do here, is run Room of Consciousness, Nightmarish Jitterbug, Charleston Crisis, Ghost Palace, Old Glast Heim Normal. If you cannot get into an instance team, go back to Gramps' 3rd level.
  • Lv 175
    • You did it ! Finally you're level 175, I'm proud of you grasshopper :>. It is now time to farm your stuff, and join bigger instances like Bios Island, Morse Cave, Temple of the Demon God, Old Glast Heim Hard... The rest is up to you ! If there are things you still don't understand or need more information, feel free to PM me on Discord (my ID is at the top of the guide).
  • Lv 175+
    • If you are well-stuffed, you can try accessing some old endgame PvM contents such as Magma Dungeon F3, the Illusion Dungeons, Abyss Glast Heim, Gramps 175+... Another slower way is to keep on doing instances, because they usually reward you a nice amount of EXP either when you clear them or when you kill the MvP. Be careful as getting past level 175 is not needed for most contents and is usually pretty HARD on the new players. At this stage, I'd recommend instead that you grind for money and starting improving your gears.
Lv 200+

If you got here then it means you have evolved to a Dragon Knight, congratulations ! You'll now be able to access the new stats system called traits, if you forgot how they work I recommend to check back the beginning of the guide in the Stats section. The traits will give you a nice power spike thanks to the impact of the POW stat both for its scaling in some 4th class skills and also mostly because of the P.ATK it gives. At this moment if you are still very poorly geared, you'll be facing a wall unless you get carried by EXP teams (which probably is the same thing that might have been happening on the previous levels too). In this case it is time that you give leveling a rest and focus on getting some basic gears (it could be at least a +9 Grace set that you can get for basically free here, or some overrefined Illusion gears). The important is that you become able to hold your ground by yourself against enemies of content of endgame 3rd class content, so that you can check out easily instances and dungeons by yourself.

  • Lv 200+
    • At this level several possibilities are available; either you can try out the new 4th class maps (Niflheim Dungeon 1 or Rudus 4), either you can stick to some late endgame contents of 3rd classes like the last levels of Thanatos Tower which still give a good amount of EXP. If you die too much, you may want to join some leveling teams like the many Thanatos Tower 12 parties. After a dozen levels earnt on your character, you'll want to dump it all on the POW stat to get a big damage boost, whatever build you are currently running.
  • Lv 215+
    • On level 215 opens a singular new map which is Amiticia Dungeon; the density of monsters is not as good as Niflheim Dungeon or Thanatos Tower, but the monsters give correct EXP. Thus swapping to this map is not obligatory but it's available.
  • Lv 230+
    • After level 230 a dive in the earnt EXP will be noticed, it slows down pretty hard and it is usually recommended to run on Field Manuals at this point. It is an alright level to stop at if the grind gets too difficult for you, as you have access at this level to a maxed trait, which in our case should be POW at 100 for maximum damage boost. This and the potentially good new damage skills which can replace or complement your current main skill. If you want to keep on grinding though, you will want to head to the level 2 of Amiticia Dungeon.
  • Lv 240+
    • At 240 the exp requirement skyrockets once again, but if you are ready to keep going until the end you may want to swap to the second floor of the Niflheim dungeon.

2HS = Two-handed Sword

ACD = After Cast Delay

AP = Activity Point

BB = Bowling Bash

BiS = Best-in-Slot

FWM = Fallen Warrior Manteau

GRAB = Greater Research Assistant Bot

GSS = Giant Snake Skin

HS = Hundred Spears
